3.10.11	oṣadhīr ājye 'vadhāya yā te agne pavamānā paśuṣu priyā tanūr yā pṛthivyāṃ yāgnau yā rathaṃtare yā gāyatre chandasīdaṃ te tām avarundhe tasyai te svāhā yā te agne pāvakāpsu priyā tanūr yāntarikṣe yā vāyau yā vāmadevye yā traiṣṭubhe chandasīdaṃ te tām avarundhe tasya te svāhā / yā te agne sūrye śuciḥ priyā tanūr yā divi yāditye yā bṛhati yā stanayitnau yā jāgate chandasīdaṃ te tām avarundhe tasyai te svāheti tisraḥ pavamānāhutīr hutvā
3.10.12	laukikam agnim āhṛtya mathitvāhavanīyād vā sabhyāvasathyāv ādadhāti
3.10.13	pratiṣiddhau sabhyāvasathyāv ekeṣām
3.10.14	agna āyūṃṣi pavasa iti tisṛbhir āśvatthīs tisraḥ samidha ādadhāti
3.10.15	sarvā ekaikasmin
3.11.1	agnir ṛṣiḥ pavamānaḥ pāñcajanyaḥ purohitaḥ / tam īmahe mahāgayam iti tṛtīyām eke samāmananti
3.11.2	samudrād ūrmir madhumāṃ udārad upāṃśunā sam amṛtatvam ānaṭ / ghṛtasya nāma guhyaṃ yad asti jihvā devānām amṛtasya nābhiḥ / vayaṃ nāma prabravāmā ghṛtenāsmin yajñe dhārayāmā namobhiḥ / upa brahmā śṛṇavac chasyamānaṃ catuḥśṛṅgo vamīd gaura etat / catvāri śṛṅgā trayo asya pādā dve śīrṣe sapta hastāso asya / tridhā baddho vṛṣabho roravīti maho devo martyāṃ āviveśa svāheti śamīmayīr ghṛtānvaktāḥ sarvā ekaikasmin
3.11.3	preddho agne dīdihi puro na ity audumbarīṃ samidham ādadhāti vidhema te parame janmann agna iti vaikaṅkatīṃ tāṃ savitur vareṇyasya citrām iti śamīmayīṃ śamīmayīṃ pūrvām eke samāmananti vaikaṅkatīm uttarām
3.11.4	prātaragnihotrasyāvṛtā tūṣṇīṃ prātaragnihotraṃ juhoti
3.11.5	juhūṃ sruvaṃ ca saṃmṛjya
3.11.6	caturgṛhītenāṣṭagṛhītena dvādaśagṛhītena vā srucaṃ pūrayitvā sapta ta iti pūrṇāhutiṃ juhoti
3.11.7	tam ekeṣāṃ tūṣṇīm agnihotram ity adhikurute
3.11.8	ye agnayo divo ye pṛthivyāḥ samāgacchantīṣam ūrjaṃ duhānāḥ / te asmā agnayo draviṇaṃ dattveṣṭāḥ prītā āhutibhājo bhūtvā yathālokaṃ punar astaṃ pareta svaheti dvitīyām
3.12.1	tadānīm evāgneyasyāṣṭākapālasyānvādhānādīni karmāṇi pratipadyate
3.12.2	yat prāk prokṣaṇāt tat kṛtvā
3.12.3	sabhāyāṃ madhye 'dhidevanam uddhatyāvokṣyākṣān nyupya vyūhya samūhya prathayitvākṣeṣu hiraṇyaṃ nidhāya niṣasāda dhṛtavrata iti juhoti
3.12.4	āvasathe madhye pariṣado hiraṇyaṃ nidhāya pra nūnaṃ brahmaṇaspatir mantraṃ vadaty ukthyam / yasminn indro varuṇo mitro aryamā devā okāṃsi cakrira iti juhoti
3.12.5	uta no 'hir budhniyaḥ śṛṇotv aja ekapāt pṛthivī samudraḥ / viśve devā ṛtāvṛdho huvānāḥ stutā mantrāḥ kaviśastā vahantv enā rājan haviṣā mādayasvety āvasatham abhimantrya
3.12.6	śatam akṣān yajamānāya prayacchati
3.12.7	teṣu kṛtaṃ vijitya
3.12.8	sabhāsadbhyaḥ pradīyamāneṣu vrīhibhyo gāṃ dīvyatāhiṃsantaḥ parvāṇi viśasateti saṃpreṣyati
3.12.9	kalpetāṃ dyāvāpṛthivī ye 'gnaya iti yathartu kl̥ptisāmanasībhyām agnīn upatiṣṭhate
3.12.10	prokṣaṇaprabhṛtīny āgneyasya karmāṇi pratipadyate siddhaṃ saṃtiṣṭhate
3.12.11	pavamānahavirbhir yajate saṃvatsara ṛtau māse 'rdhamāse dvādaśāhe caturahe tryahe dvyahe śvo bhūte sadyo vā
3.12.12	somena yakṣyamāṇasyādadhānasya pavamānahaviṣāṃ sāṃvatsarikaḥ kalpaḥ/
3.12.13	agnaye pavamānāya puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvaped agnaye pāvakāyāgnaye śucaye
3.12.14	samānabarhiṣi nānābarhiṣi vā
3.12.15	prathamaṃ vā nirupyottare samasyet
3.12.16	āgneyena vāṣṭākapālena samānatantrāṇi kuryāt
3.12.17	agnīṣomīyam ekādaśakapālam anunirvapaty āgnāvaiṣṇavam ekādaśakapālam aindrāgnam ekādaśakapālam adityai ghṛte caruṃ viṣṇave śipiviṣṭāya tryuddhau ghṛte caruṃ saptadaśādityasya sāmidhenyo bhavanty ādityasyeḍābhāgaṃ brahmaṇe parihṛtya sarve prāśnanti tathā cāturdhākaraṇikāni
3.12.18	athāgnihotrārambhaḥ
3.12.19	agnihotram ārapsyamāno daśahotāraṃ manasānudrutya sagrahaṃ hutvā sāyamagnihotrasyāvṛtā mantreṇa sāyamagnihotraṃ juhoti vyāhṛtībhiḥ prathamam agnihotram upasādayati tathā saṃvatsare
3.13.1	atha darśapūrṇamāsayor ārambhaḥ
3.13.2	darśapūrṇamāsāv ārabhamānaḥ pūrvasya parvaṇa aupavasathye 'hani caturhotāraṃ manasānudrutya sagrahaṃ hutvā pūrṇā paścād yat te devā adadhur iti sārasvatau homau hutvā
3.13.3	anvārambhaṇīyām iṣṭiṃ nirvapati
3.13.4	āgnāvaiṣṇavam ekādaśakapālaṃ sarasvatyai caruṃ sarasvate dvādaśa kapālam agnaye bhagine 'ṣṭākapālaṃ yaḥ kāmayeta bhagy annādaḥ syām iti nityavad eke bhagine samāmananti
3.13.5	purastāt sviṣṭakṛtaś cittaṃ ca svāhā cittiś ca svāheti dvādaśagṛhītena dvādaśa jayāñ juhoti
3.13.6	prajāpatir jayān indrāyeti trayodaśīm
3.13.7	agne balada saha oja ākramamāṇāya me 'dāḥ / abhiśastikṛte 'nabhiśastenyāyāsyai janatāyai śraiṣṭhyāyeti caturdaśīṃ yāṃ janatāṃ dviṣyāc citraṃ tasyāṃ janatāyāṃ bhavatv iti śabalam iva tasyātmañ jāyate
3.13.8	api vā nānvārambhaṇīyāṃ kurvītāgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapet
3.13.9	amāvāsyāyām ādadhānasyaitad avikṛtam
3.13.10	paurṇamāsyāṃ tu pūrvasya parvaṇa aupavasathye 'hany agnīn ādhāya seṣṭyapavṛjya
3.13.11	tadānīm eva caturhotāraṃ sārasvatau homāv anvārambhaṇīyāṃ ca kurute
3.13.12	śvo bhūte paurṇamāsena yajate vyāhṛtībhir havīṃṣy āsādayati tathā saṃvatsare
3.14.1	punarādheyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmas tasyāgnyādheyena kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
3.14.2	agnīn ādhāyaitasmin saṃvatsare jyāniṃ putramartyāṃ vābhyeti svena vāṅgena virudhyate na vardhnoti sa punarādheyaṃ kurvīta
3.14.3	paurṇamāsyeṣṭvāmāvāsyāyām āgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvaped vaiśvānaraṃ dvādaśakapālam agnim udvāsayiṣyann ity ekeṣām
3.14.4	agnīṣomīyam ekādaśakapālam anunirvaped agnaye 'psumate 'ṣṭākapālaṃ maitraṃ carum
3.14.5	purastāt sviṣṭakṛto yā te agna utsīdataḥ pavamānā paśuṣu priyā tanūs tayā saha pṛthivīm āviśa rathaṃtareṇa sāmnā gāyatreṇa chandasā tato no maha āvaha yā te agne pāvakā yā manasā preyasī priyā tanūs tayā sahāntarikṣam āviśa vāmadevyena sāmnā traiṣṭubhena chandasā tato na ūrjam ākṛdhi gṛhamedhīyaṃ ca vardhaya yā te agne sūrye śuciḥ priyā tanūs tayā saha divam āviśa bṛhatā sāmnā jāgatena chandasā tato no vṛṣṭyāvadhi yās te agne vibhaktīr indra sūkara ābhara tāsu śociṣu sīdeha bhasma vaiśvānarasya yat / yās te agne kāmadughā vibhaktīr anusaṃbhṛtāḥ / tābhir naḥ kāmān dhukṣveha prajāṃ puṣṭim atho dhanam / ye te agne vānaspatyāḥ saṃbhārāḥ saṃbhṛtāḥ saha tebhir gaccha vanasptīn svāṃ yoniṃ yathātatham / agann agnir yathālokam asadat sadane sve / avīrahatyaṃ deveṣūpāgāṃ manasā saheti saptāhutīr hutvā jvalato 'gnīn avasṛjati yāvad darśapūrṇamāsāv abhihutau tāvac ciram avasṛṣṭāgnir bhavati
3.15.1	saṃvatsaraṃ dvādaśāhaṃ vā
3.15.2	rohiṇī punarvasū anūrādhāś ca punarādheyanakṣatrāṇi
3.15.3	varṣāsu śaradi vādhatte
3.15.4	sarvān madhyaṃdine
3.15.5	kṛtākṛtāḥ saṃbhārāḥ
3.15.6	sarvābhiḥ sārparājñībhir gārhapatyam ādadhāti
3.15.7	darbhair upolavaiḥ saṃvatsarapravātair gārhapatyād āhavanīyaṃ jvalantam uddharati
3.15.8	yat tvā kruddhaḥ parovapeti dakṣiṇāgnim ādadhāti yat te manyuparoptasyety āhavanīyam
3.15.9	mano jyotir juṣatām ity āhitamā havanīyam upatiṣṭhate
3.15.10	punas tvādityā rudrā vasavaḥ samindhatām ity upasamindhe
3.15.11	punas tvādityā rudrā vasavaḥ samindhatām ity upasamindhe punas tvādityā rudrā vasavaḥ samindhatāṃ punar brahmāṇo vasunītha yajñaiḥ / yā iṣṭā uṣaso nimrucaś ca yājyās tāḥ saṃdadhāmi haviṣā ghṛtena svāhety āhutiṃ juhoti / mano jyotir juṣatām iti dvitīyām
3.15.12	juhūṃ sruvaṃ ca saṃmṛjya caturgṛhītenāṣṭagṛhītena dvādaśagṛhītena vā srucaṃ pūrayitvā sapta ta iti pūrṇāhutiṃ juhoti
3.15.13	āgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ pañcakapālaṃ vāgnyādheyikasyāṣṭākapālasya sthāne nirvapati
3.15.14	tasyopāṃśu sarvaṃ kriyata ottamād anūyājāt
3.15.15	agnāgne 'gnāv agne 'gnināgne 'gnim agna iti caturṣu prayājeṣu catasro vibhaktīr dadhāti purastād vaṣaṭkārāt
3.15.16	punar ūrjeti purastāt prayājānām āhutiṃ juhoty upariṣṭād eke samāmananti
3.15.17	vṛdhanvantam āgneyasyājyabhāgasya nigameṣūpalakṣayet
3.15.18	pavamānaṃ saumyasya
3.15.19	saha rayyeti purastād anūyājānām āhutiṃ juhoty upariṣṭād eke samāmananti
3.15.20	devo agnau devo agnir iti dvayor anūyājayor dve bibhaktī dadhāti
3.15.21	uccair uttamam anūyājaṃ saṃpreṣyati
3.15.22	āgnivāruṇam ekādaśakapālam anunirvapet
3.15.23	yaḥ parācīnaṃ punarādheyād agnim ādadhīta sa etān homāñ juhuyāl lekaḥ salekaḥ sulekaḥ ketaḥ saketaḥ suketo vivasvāṃ aditir devajūtir iti
3.15.24	ādhānaprabhṛti yāvajjīvaṃ gārhapatyadakṣiṇāgnī dhāryete tathā sabhyāvasathyau dakṣiṇāgnes tv anugatasya manthanakalpo yadi mathitvādhīyate yady āhārya āharaṇam arthāyārthāyāhavanīyaṃ gārhapatyād uddharati nityaṃ gataśriyo dhāryata āyuṣkāmasya vā
3.16.1	agnihotraṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
3.16.2	tasmai sāyaṃprātar jvalantaṃ gārhapatyād āhavanīyam uddharati
3.16.3	adhivṛkṣasūrye sāyamagnihotrāyoṣasi prātaragnihotrāya
3.16.4	naktaṃ vā dhārayeyuḥ
3.16.5	uddhareti preṣite vācā tvā hotrā prāṇenodgātrā cakṣuṣādhvaryuṇā manasā brahmaṇā śrotreṇāgnīdhaitais tvā pañcabhir daivyair ṛtvigbhir uddharāmi jahāmi mṛtyum amṛtenādadhāmi bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar uddhriyamāṇa uddhara pāpmano mā yad avidvān yac ca vidvāṃś cakāra / ahnā yad enaḥ kṛtam asti pāpaṃ sarvasmān moddhṛto muñca tasmād iti sāyam
3.16.6	rātryā yad enaḥ kṛtam asti pāpaṃ sarvasmān moddhṛto muñca tasmād iti prātaḥ
3.16.7	amṛtāhutim amṛtāyāṃ juhomy agniṃ pṛthivyām amṛtasya jityai / tayānantaṃ kāmam ahaṃ jayāmi prajāpatir yaṃ prathamo jigāyāgnim agnau svāheti sāyam āyatane pratiṣṭhāpayati
3.16.8	sūryam agnau svāheti prātaḥ
3.16.9	prathamāstamite sāyamagnihotraṃ juhoti nakṣatraṃ dṛṣṭvā pradoṣe voṣasi prātaragnihotraṃ purodayam udite vā yarhi vāk pravadet tarhi hotavyam ity ekeṣām
3.16.10	etasmin kāle sarvakarmāṇi kriyante 'nyatroddharaṇāt
3.16.11	parisamūhanenāgnīn alaṃkaroty agne gṛhapate śundhasveti gārhapatyam agne vahne śundhasveti dakṣiṇāgnim agne samrāṭ śundhasvety āhavanīyam
3.16.12	purastād alaṃkārāḥ sāyam upariṣṭād alaṃkārāḥ prātaḥ
3.16.13	ubhayato'laṃkārān eke samāmananti
3.16.14	agnihotrapātrāṇi prayunakti khādiraṃ sruvaṃ vaikaṅkatīm agnihotrahavaṇīm acakrāvartām aśūdrakṛtām ūrdhvakapālām agnihotrasthālīm
3.16.15	dakṣiṇena vihāraṃ gaur avasthitā bhavati
3.16.16	iḍa ehy adita ehi sarasvaty ehi gaur ehīti tām āhūya pūṣāsīti vatsam upasṛjati dhāvantaṃ vānumantrayate
3.16.17	prācīm udīcīṃ vāvṛtyānyaḥ śūdrād dogdhi na saṃmṛśati yathopalambham anūco vā
3.16.18	pūrvau duhyāj jyeṣṭhasya jyaiṣṭhineyasya yo vā gataśrīḥ syād aparau duhyāt kaniṣṭhasya kāniṣṭhineyasya yo vā bubhūṣet
3.16.19	dohane dugdhvā sthālyām ānayati sthālyāṃ vā dogdhi
3.16.20	dvayoḥ payasā paśukāmasya juhuyāt pūrvam adhiśrityottaram ānayet
3.17.1	ṛtaṃ tvā satyena pariṣiñcāmīti sāyaṃ pariṣiñcati satyaṃ tvartena pariṣiñcāmīti prātaḥ
3.17.2	āhavanīyaṃ pariṣicya gārhapatyam atha dakṣiṇāgniṃ gārhapatyaṃ vā pariṣicya dakṣiṇāgnim athāhavanīyam
3.17.3	yajñasya saṃtatir asi yajñasya tvā saṃtatyai nayāmi saṃtatyai tvā yajñasyeti gārhapatyāt saṃtatām apāṃ dhārāṃ srāvayaty āhavanīyāt
3.17.4	dhṛṣṭir asīty upaveṣam ādāya nirūḍhaṃ janyaṃ bhayaṃ saha tena yaṃ dviṣmaḥ subhūtāya śrayadhvam iti tena gārhapatyād udīco 'ṅgārān nirūhati
3.17.5	vyantān karoti
3.17.6	iḍāyāḥ padaṃ ghṛtavac carācaraṃ jātavedo havir idaṃ juṣasva / ye grāmyāḥ paśavo viśvarūpās teṣāṃ saptānām iha rantir astu puṣṭir iti teṣv agnihotram adhiśrayati
3.17.7	samudantaṃ hotavyam
3.17.8	anantaraṃ vādhiśrayaṇād udbhavaḥ sthod ahaṃ prajayā paśubhir bhūyāsam iti tṛṇaṃ pradīpyāvekṣate
3.17.9	haras te mā vinaiṣam iti sruveṇādbhiḥ pratiṣiñcaty amṛtam asīti vā
3.17.10	godohanasaṃnejanena pratiṣicyam ekena stokena pratiṣicyaṃ pratiṣiktaṃ paśukāmasya
3.17.11	apratiṣiktaṃ tejaskāmasyābhicaratas titīrṣato vā
3.17.12	yaḥ kāmayeta śūro me rāṣṭra ājāyeteti punar eva tasyāvekṣate yathā purastāt
3.17.13	antaritaṃ rakṣa ity ulmukena triḥ paryagni karoti pari vājapatir iti vā
3.17.14	prajāṃ me yacchety ante dhārayati
3.17.15	pratyūḍhaṃ janyaṃ bhayaṃ saha tena yaṃ dviṣmaḥ subhūtam akarteti tena gārhapatye 'ṅgārān pratyūhati bhūtakṛtaḥ sthāpyeti sasyaṃ yajamānasyeti vā
3.17.16	devasya tveti sruvam agnihotrahavaṇīṃ cādāya
3.17.17	pratyuṣṭam ity āhavanīye gārhapatye vā niṣṭapati
3.17.18	suparṇāṃ tvā suparṇamayīṃ hiraṇyayaṣṭir asy amṛtapālāśāḥ sroto yajñānām ity agnihotrahavaṇīṃ saṃmārṣṭi
3.17.19	ariṣṭo yajamānaḥ patnī cety ubhayam
3.17.20	om unneṣyāmi havyaṃ devebhyaḥ pāpmano yajamānam iti sāyam āmantrayate
3.17.21	om unnayāmi havyaṃ devebhyaḥ pāpmano yajamānam iti prātaḥ
3.17.22	pravasaty om unnayeti svayam ātmānaṃ praty eva brūyāt
3.17.23	agnaye ca tvā pṛthivyai connayāmi vātāya ca tvāntarikṣāya connayāmi sūryāya ca tvā dive connayāmy adbhyaś ca tvauṣadhībhyaś connayāmīti caturaḥ sruvān unnayaty uttamena dviḥ pañcāvattinaḥ
3.17.24	bhūr iḍā bhuva iḍā suvar iḍā karad iḍeti vā jvalad iḍeti pañcavattinaḥ
3.17.25	yaṃ prati putrāṇāṃ kāmayetānenardhnuyām iti taṃ prati pūrṇam unnayet
3.17.26	yadi kāmayeta sarve sadṛśāḥ syur iti sarvān samaśa unnayet
3.17.27	unnītaṃ daśahotrābhimṛśati na vābhimṛśati
3.17.28	sajūr devaiḥ sāyaṃyāvabhiḥ sāyaṃyāvāno mā devāḥ svasti saṃpādayantu paśubhiḥ saṃpṛcīyeti sāyam unnītaṃ sthālīṃ cābhimṛśati sajūr devaiḥ prātaryāvabhiḥ prātaryāvāṇo mā devāḥ svasti saṃpādayantu paśubhiḥ saṃpṛcīyeti prātaḥ
3.17.29	prācīm udīcīṃ vāhṛtyāpareṇa gārhapatyam upasādayatīty ekeṣām
3.18.1	pālāśīṃ samidhaṃ prādeśamātrīm ekāṃ dve tisro vopariṣṭāt srugdaṇḍa upasaṃgṛhya
3.18.2	urv antarikṣaṃ vīhīti samayā gārhapatyasyārcir harati
3.18.3	prāg uddravan daśahotāraṃ vyācaṣṭe
3.18.4	agnaye tvā vaiśvānarāyeti madhyadeśe nigṛhṇāti
3.18.5	vātāya tvety udyacchati
3.18.6	āyur me yacchety apareṇāhavanīyam oṣadhīṣūpasādayati
3.18.7	eṣā te agne samid iti samidham ādadhāti
3.18.8	hiraṇyayaṃ tvā vaṃśaṃ svargasya lokasya saṃkramaṇaṃ dadhāmīti vā tā asya sūdadohasa iti vā rajatāṃ tvā haritagarbhām agnir jyotiṣā jyotiṣmatīṃ svargyāṃ kāmadughām akṣitām akṣityā āptyai vyāptyai samāptyai kāmāya svargāya lokāyāmṛtatvāya rātrim iṣṭakām upadadha iti sāyaṃ hariṇīṃ tvā rajatagarbhāṃ sūryo jyotiṣā jyotiṣmatīṃ svargyāṃ kāmadughām akṣitām akṣityā āptyai vyāptyai samāptyai kāmāya svargāya lokāyāmṛtatvāyāhar iṣṭakām upadadha iti prātaḥ
3.18.9	vidyud asi vidya me pāpmānam ṛtaṃ satyam upaimi mayi śraddhety apa upaspṛśya
3.18.10	yadā śyāvevātha juhoti jvalantyām
3.18.11	yadā vā vītārcir lelāyatīva
3.18.12	dhūpāyantyāṃ grāmakāmasya
3.18.13	dvyaṅgule mūlāt samidham anusrāvayan
3.18.14	hotrā bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar agnir jyotir jyotir agniḥ svāheti sāyaṃ hotrā bhūr bhuvaḥ suvaḥ sūryo jyotir jyotiḥ sūryaḥ svāheti prātaḥ
3.18.15	saṃsṛṣṭahomam eke samāmananti
3.18.16	agnir jyotir jyotiḥ sūryaḥ svāheti sāyaṃ sūryo jyotir jyotir agniḥ svāheti prātaḥ
3.18.17	varco me yaccheti punar oṣadhīṣūpasādayati
3.18.18	lepam ādāyauṣadhībhyas tvauṣadhīr jinvety uttarato barhiṣi lepaṃ nimārṣṭi
3.18.19	agne gṛhapate mā mā saṃtāpsīr ātmann amṛtam adhiṣi prajā jyotir aśīyeti gārhapatyam avekṣate
3.18.20	atihāya tūṣṇīm uttarāṃ samidhi bhūyasīṃ juhoti
3.18.21	sajūr jātavedo diva ā pṛthivyā juṣāṇo asya haviṣo ghṛtasya vīhi svāhety ājyena juhuyād yatra paśupatiḥ paśūñ chāmayet
3.18.22	agne duḥśīrtatano juṣasva svāheti juhuyād yadi tad atihanyāt
3.18.23	dvādaśa rātrīḥ sāyaṃsāyaṃ juhuyād yadi tad atihanyāt
3.18.24	nādṛtyam
3.18.25	iṣe tveti sāyaṃ lepam avamārṣṭi
3.18.26	ūrje tveti prātar unmārṣṭi
3.18.27	yaṃ kāmayetāvatarāṃ pāpīyān syād iti bhūyas tasya pūrvaṃ hutvottaraṃ kanīyo juhuyāt
3.18.28	yaṃ kāmayeta na pāpīyān na śreyān syād iti samaṃ tasya juhuyāt
3.18.29	yaṃ kāmayeta vasīyān syād iti kanīyas tasya pūrvaṃ hutvottaraṃ bhūyo juhuyāt
3.18.30	bhūyo bhakṣāyāvaśinaṣṭi
3.18.31	hutvā mahad abhivīkṣeta
3.18.32	rudra mṛḍānārbhava mṛḍa dhūrta mṛḍa namas te astu paśupate mā mā hiṃsīr iti srucā trir udañcam agnim ativalgayati
3.18.33	srucaṃ nidhāya lepam ādāya
3.18.34	apa upaspṛśya
3.18.35	pūṣāsīti dvir aṅgulyā prāśyācamya punaḥ prāśnāti
3.18.36	srucaṃ darbhāṃś cādāyodaṅṅ utsṛpya
3.18.37	āgneyaṃ retaḥ prajananaṃ me astu daśavīraṃ sarvagaṇaṃ svastaye / ātmasani prajāsani paśusany abhayasani lokasani vṛṣṭisani / agniḥ prajāṃ bahulāṃ me karotv annaṃ payo reto asmāsu dhatta / rāyaspoṣam iṣam ūrjam asmāsu dīdharad iti
3.19.1	prāgdaṇḍayodagdaṇḍayā vā srucā dvir ācāmati dviś ca nirleḍhi
3.19.2	garbhebhyas tvā garbhān prīṇīhīti vā
3.19.3	sauryaṃ retaḥ prajananaṃ me astv iti prātaḥ
3.19.4	srucam adbhiḥ pūrayitvā sarpebhyas tvā sarpāñ jinveti vidhukṣati
3.19.5	ācamya
3.19.6	srucaṃ darbhaiḥ prakṣālya
3.19.7	pūrayitvā sarpān pipīlikāñ jinvety apa utsiñcati
3.19.8	sarpadevajanāñ jinveti dvitīyāṃ bhūtebhyas tveti tṛtīyāṃ mahate devāyeti caturthīm
3.19.9	srucam adbhiḥ pūrayitvā pṛthivyām amṛtaṃ juhomi svāhety apareṇāhavanīyam apareṇa vā gārhapatyaṃ ninayati
3.19.10	gṛhebhyas tvā gṛhān prīṇīhīti tasyaikadeśam añjalau patnyaḥ
3.19.11	patnī yadi nānvāste sarvaṃ pṛthivyām
3.19.12	hastaṃ pratāpya srucy avadadhāti srucaṃ vā niṣṭapya haste 'vadadhāti saptarṣibhyas tvā saptarṣīñ jinveti srucodag uddiśati
3.19.13	srucaṃ nidhāya pratyetya sruveṇa gārhapatyadakṣiṇāgnyor juhoti pratyāhuti samidho 'bhyādhāya
3.19.14	mayi puṣṭiṃ puṣṭipatir dadhātu rāyaspoṣam iṣam ūrjam asmāsu dīdharat / agnaye gṛhapataye rayipataye paśupataye puṣṭipataye kāmāyānnādyāya svāheti dve gārhapatye juhoti
3.19.15	annapate 'nnasya no dehīti dve dakṣiṇāgnau
3.19.16	api vā catasro gārhapatye juhuyāc catasro dakṣiṇāgnau
3.19.17	na vā juhuyāt
3.19.18	piprer agniḥ svāṃ tanuvam ayāḍ dyāvāpṛthivī ūrjam asmāsu dhehi iti sthālyāṃ tṛṇam aṅktvāhavanīye 'nupraharati na vā
3.19.19	dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ tvā dyāvāpṛthivī jinvety antarvedyāṃ saṃkṣālanaṃ ninayati
3.19.20	pariṣiñcati yathā purastāt
3.19.21	dīdihi dīdyāsaṃ dīdidāsīty upasamindhe
3.19.22	ājyena juhuyāt tejaskāmasya payasā paśukāmasya dadhnendriyakāmasya taṇḍulair ojaskāmasya yavāgvā grāmakāmasyaudanenānnādyakāmasya māṃsena vīryakāmasya somena brahmavarcasakāmasya
3.19.23	yad anyad adhiśrayaṇāt pratiṣecanāc ca tad dadhnas taṇḍulānāṃ somasya ca kriyate
3.19.24	apāṃ pratyasanakāle darbhatṛṇābhyām ājyaṃ pratyasyet pratiṣekaṃ yavāgūṃ śrapayati / yathā yavāgūm evaṃ māṃsam
3.19.25	parvaṇi rājanyasyāgnihotraṃ juhuyān nāntarāle
3.19.26	yat tv asya gṛhe 'nnaṃ kriyate tasmād brāhmaṇāya mukhato haranti taddhutam asyāgnihotraṃ bhavati ya ṛtaṃ satyam iva vadann ījānaḥ somena syāt tasya sadāgnihotraṃ juhuyāt
3.20.1	ṛte gṛhasya pravāsaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
3.20.2	sagṛhastu prayāsyan yatra pañca nava daśa vā saṃhitā vasati yatra vā navarātraṃ vāstu punar abhyety ekāṃ vasati tatra vāstoṣpatīyaṃ juhoti
3.20.3	sarvaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ yāneṣv ādadhāti
3.20.4	yad anyaj jihīrṣanti pūrvaṃ tat pravahanti
3.20.5	ahute vāpoddharanti tasmād deśāt
3.20.6	sarveṣu yukteṣu dakṣiṇo 'gniṣṭhasya yukto bhavati savyasya yoktraṃ parihṛtam anūtsaktam atha vāstoṣpatīyam anudruyottarayā juhoti
3.20.7	na hute 'bhyādadhāti
3.20.8	nāvakṣāṇāny asaṃprakṣāpya prayāti
3.20.9	ayaṃ te yonir ṛtviya iti pṛthagaraṇīṣv agnīn samāropya prayāti
3.20.10	atho khalv āhur yad araṇyoḥ samārūḍho naśyed ud asyāgniḥ sīdet punarādheyaḥ syād iti yā te agne yajñiyā tanūs tayehy ārohātmātmānam acchā vasūni kṛṇvann asme naryā purūṇi / yajño bhūtvā yajñam āsīda svāṃ yoniṃ jātavedo bhuva ājāyamānaḥ sakṣaya ehīty ātman samāropya prayāti
3.20.11	yatra vasati tatra prāg astamayān manthati
3.20.12	upāvaroha jātavedaḥ punas tvaṃ devebhyo havyaṃ vahataḥ prajānan / āyuḥ prajāṃ rayim asmāsu dhehy ajasro dīdihi no duroṇa ity ātman samārūḍham araṇyor upāvarohya manthati
3.20.13	laukikaṃ vāgnim āhṛtya tasminn upāvarohayate
3.20.14	idaṃ śreyo 'vasānaṃ yad agāt syono me dyāvāpṛthivī abhūtām / anamīvāḥ pradiśaḥ santu mahyaṃ gomad dhanavad aśvavaddhiraṇyavat puruṣavat suvīravat svāhety avasite juhoti
3.20.15	darvihomān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
3.20.16	juhotīti codyamāne darvihomo yatra ca svāhākāraḥ
3.20.17	tāṃs tūṣṇīkenājyena sakṛdgṛhītenāgreṇāhavanīyaṃ parītya dakṣiṇatas tiṣṭhañ juhvāhavanīye 'dhvaryuḥ svāhākāreṇa juhoti
3.20.18	dviprabhṛtyāhutigaṇeṣu pratyāhuti gṛhītvā pratyāhuti samidho 'bhyādhāya vigrāhaṃ juhoti
3.20.19	yatra mantragaṇena karma codayet pratimantraṃ tatra juhuyāt
3.20.20	juhotiśabde pradeśān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
3.20.21	svakṛta iriṇe pradare darbhastambe sthāṇāv iti
3.21.1	āhavanīyāpanayo 'nagnau tasminn eva deśe juhoti
3.21.2	dārśapaurṇamāsikāni pradhānāny uttarasyāṃ tatau codyante 'nyatra somād dharmād darvihomebhyaś ca
3.21.3	tāni svadharmāṇi
3.21.4	sādṛśyādv ikāraḥ
3.21.5	sa liṅgena gamyeta
3.21.6	devatāsāmānyena haviḥsāmānyena vā yatra haviḥ pradīyate
3.21.7	vipratiṣedhe haviḥsāmānyaṃ balīyaḥ
3.21.8	yathā vaiṣṇavaḥ puroḍāśaḥ
3.21.9	ekadevatās tv āgneyavikārā anyatra prakṛtidevatābhyo yathā saumyaś carur aindraḥ puroḍāśa iti
3.21.10	athetare 'gnīṣomīyasyaindrāgnasya vā
3.21.11	prakṛtau viśiṣṭadharmāṇām uttarasyāṃ tatau samavetānām aṅgavipratiṣedhe mukhyatvaṃ balīyaḥ
3.21.12	mukhyatvād bhūyastvam
3.21.13	bhūyastvāt sthānam
3.21.14	sthānād vidhiḥ
3.21.15	vidher aṅgam
3.21.16	aṅgāt pradhānam
3.21.17	darśapūrṇamāsayor vikṛteś ca saṃnipāte darśapūrṇamāsau balīyāṃsau
3.21.18	yāni tviṣṭipaśubandhānāṃ pratyakṣāṇi tāni tatra
3.21.19	darśapūrṇamāsaprakṛtaya iṣṭipaśubandhās te svadharmāṇaḥ sāmānyād vikāraḥ
3.21.20	karmasaṃyuktāni dravyāṇi prakṛtau tatsaṃyogād dharmaṃ labhante karmaṇy avidyamāne sahadharmadravyaṃ nivartate
3.21.21	yathā kṛṣṇaleṣv avahananam
3.21.22	anyasmiṃś ca dravye tenārthena saṃyujyamāne dharmāveśaḥ
3.21.23	sthālyāṃ kapāladharmaḥ śyāmākeṣu vrīhidharmaḥ
3.21.24	yajñotpattau pratiṣiddhe sarvaṃ pratiṣidhyeta
3.21.25	na yūpaṃ minvanti nottaravedim upavapanti
3.21.26	anyasmiṃś ca dravye tenārthena saṃyujyamāne dharmāveṣa utkare vājinam āsādayanty aśve paśūn niyuñjanti paridhau paśūn niyuñjanti
3.21.27	sāmidhenīṣu vardhamānāsu
3.22.1	kāṣṭhāni vardhante saṃhriyamāṇāsu yathāprakṛti
3.22.2	yathārtham ūhaḥ
3.22.3	na prakṛtāv ūho vidyate
3.22.4	patnīṃ saṃnahyopahūto 'yaṃ yajamāna iti
3.22.5	tathottarasyāṃ tatau yathāsamāmnātam
3.22.6	pratinidhiṣv arthaluptāni na kriyeran yathā lūne lavanamantracchinne chedanamantraḥ
3.22.7	yatra payaḥ śrapaṇārthena śrūyate devas tvā savitotpunātv ity utpavanaṃ saṃnamati payo devāgreṣv agra ity abhimantraṇam evam ājye
3.22.8	carukalpān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
3.22.9	sthālīṃ kapālānāṃ sthāne prayunakti
3.22.10	tasya prasiddhamātriṣphalīkṛtebhyaḥ
3.22.11	prathamena kapālamantreṇa sthālīm upadhāya
3.22.12	śūrpād eva taṇḍulān samopyotpūyādhiśrayaṇamantreṇopya paryagni kṛtvā śrapayitvābhighārya sthālyaivodvāsayati
3.22.13	puroḍāśena puroḍāśagaṇe
3.22.14	yathābhāgaṃ vyāvartadhvam ity ekaikaṃ piṇḍam apacchinatti yathābhāgaṃ vyāvartethām ity avaśiṣṭau
3.22.15	tayor eva devatādeśanam
3.22.16	carupuroḍāśyān prāg adhivapanād vibhajyeraṃs tatra vibhāgamantraṃ japati samān dvaidhaṃ karoti viṣamān yathābhāgam
3.22.17	idam amuṣmai cāmuṣmai cety ekaikasmin rāśāv ekaikāṃ devatām upalakṣayet
3.22.18	pauṣṇam apacchidya saha puroḍāśyaiḥ pinaṣṭi
3.22.19	adhiśrayaṇakāle mitho vibhajyeran
3.22.20	tatra vibhāgamantraṃ japati
3.22.21	nānābījeṣu samaveteṣv ekam ulūkhalaṃ musalaṃ śūrpaṃ kṛṣṇājinaṃ ca
3.22.22	prathame bīje haviṣkṛtam āhvayaty uttame vācaṃ visṛjate
3.22.23	somenāgrayaṇeṣṭyā paśubandhena vāmāvāsyāyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ vā yajeta
3.22.24	saptadaśānubrūyād iṣṭyāḥ paśubandhasya vā pañcadaśabhir vikalperann avikalpo vā
3.23.1	āgrāyaṇeṣṭiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
3.23.2	tayā nāniṣṭvā navānām oṣadhīnāṃ phalāny aśnāti grāmyāṇām āraṇyānāṃ ca
3.23.3	vrīhīṇām agrapākasya yajate tathā śyāmākānaṃ yavānām agrapākasya yajate
3.23.4	tathā vrīhīṇāṃ nirvapaṇakāle purāṇānāṃ vrīhīṇām āgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapati navānām itarāṇi
3.23.5	āgnendram aindrāgnaṃ vā dvādaśakapālaṃ vaiśvadevaṃ caruṃ payasi śṛtaṃ saumyaṃ śyāmākaṃ caruṃ dyāvāpṛthivyam ekakapālam
3.23.6	nānātantraṃ śyāmākam eke samāmananti
3.23.7	upasanne haviṣyaprokṣite śatāyudhāyeti pañcājyānīr juhoti
3.23.8	purastāt sviṣṭakṛta eke samāmananti
3.23.9	ekakapālānāṃ vaiśvadevīyenaikakapālena kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
3.23.10	nāviḥpṛṣṭhaṃ karoti
3.23.11	na māsanāmabhir abhijuhoti
3.23.12	vrīhibhir iṣṭvā vrīhibhir eva yajetāyavebhyo yavair iṣṭvā yavair eva yajetāvrīhibhyaḥ
3.23.13	veṇuvānāṃ śyāmākam eke samāmananti
3.23.14	api vā nāgrayaṇeṣṭiṃ kurvīta navair evāmāvāsyāyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ vā yajeta
3.23.15	navair vāgnihotraṃ juhuyād agnihotrīṃ vā navān ādayitvā tasyāḥ kṣīreṇa juhuyāc catuḥśarāvam odanaṃ vā paktvāgrayaṇadevatābhyaḥ sviṣṭakṛccaturthībhyo hutvā tadvyañjanaṃ bhojayati bhojayati
4.1.1	aindrāgnena paśunā ṣāṇmāsyeṣāṇmāsye yajata āvṛttimukhaāvṛttimukhe saṃvatsaresaṃvatsare vā
4.1.2	sauryaḥ prājāpatyo vā
4.1.3	taṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
4.1.4	sūryaṃ te cakṣur iti ṣaḍḍhotāraṃ manasānudrutya sagrahaṃ hutvānvārambhaṇīyām iṣṭiṃ nirvapati
4.1.5	āgnāvaiṣṇavam ekādaśakapālam
4.1.6	siddhaṃ saṃtiṣṭhate
4.1.7	api vā caturgṛhītam ājyam āgnāvaiṣṇavayarcāhavanīye juhoti
4.1.8	śeṣam ājyasya karoti dhārayaty āhavanīyam
4.1.9	uru viṣṇo vikramasveti sruveṇāhavanīye yūpāhutiṃ juhoti
4.1.10	ājyaśeṣaṃ sruvaṃ cādatte takṣṇe paraśuṃ prayacchati tad gacchanti yatra yūpaṃ chetsyanto bhavanti
4.1.11	pālāśaḥ khādiro bailvo rauhītakaś ca yūpyā vṛkṣāḥ
4.1.12	pālāśaṃ brahmavarcasakāmasyānnādyakāmasya vā khādiraṃ svargakāmasya bailvaṃ brahmavarcasakāmasya rauhītakaṃ prajākāmasya
4.1.13	tryavarārdhyān yūpyān vṛkṣān atikramya
4.1.14	ya ṛjur ūrdhva ūrdhvaśakala ūrdhvaśākhaḥ same bhūmyai svād yone rūḍhaḥ
4.1.15	yaṃ kāmayetāpratiṣṭhitaḥ syād ity ārohaṃ tasmai vṛśced yaṃ kāmayetāpaśuḥ syād ity aparṇaṃ tasmai śuṣkāgraṃ kāmayeta paśumān syād iti bahuparṇaṃ tasmai bahuśākham aśuṣkāgram
4.1.16	pratiṣṭhitaṃ pratiṣṭhākāmasya
4.1.17	yaḥ pratyaṅṅ upanatastaṃ vṛśced yaḥ prāṅṅ udaṅ vopanataḥ
4.1.18	yasya carjoḥ sata īṣad ivāgram upanatam
4.1.19	aty anyān agām iti
4.2.1	yaṃ joṣayate tam upatiṣṭhate
4.2.2	devas tvā savitā madhvānaktv iti sruveṇa gulphadaghne jānudaghne vā paryaṇakti
4.2.3	oṣadhe trāyasvainam ity ūrdhvāgrām oṣadhim antardadhāti svadhite mainaṃ hiṃsīr iti paraśunā praharati yaḥ prathamaḥ śakalaḥ parāpatati tam upayacchate
4.2.4	anakṣasaṅgaṃ sthāṇum ucchiṃṣan vṛścati gulhadaghnaṃ vā
4.2.5	divam agreṇeti prāñcam udañcaṃ vā prahāpayati
4.2.6	vanaspate śatavalśo virohety āvraścane juhoti sahasravalśā vi vayaṃ ruhemety ātmānaṃ pratyabhimṛśati
4.2.7	yaṃ tvāyaṃ svadhitir ity anulomaṃ paraśunāṅgān kalpayati
4.2.8	acchinno rāyaḥ suvīra ity agraṃ parivāsayati
4.2.9	ekāratniprabhṛtīni brāhmaṇavyākhyātāni kāmyāni yūpapramāṇāni teṣāṃ yāthākāmī
4.2.10	sahopareṇa saṃkhyā syād ā trayastriṃśadaratneḥ
4.2.11	tryaratnir vā caturaratnir vā pālāśo nirūḍhapaśubandhasya yūpo 'to 'nye saumyasyādhvarasya
4.2.12	aṣṭāśriṃ takṣṇoti nātisthūlaṃ nātyaṇum ataṣṭam uparam
4.2.13	puraḥpuroṇīyāṃsaṃ gopucchaṃ vā
4.2.14	tasyaiva vṛkṣasyāgrataś caṣālaṃ karoti
4.2.15	aṣṭāśriṃ pṛthumātraṃ madhye saṃnatam
4.2.16	yāvad idaṃ prathamam aṅgulikāṇḍaṃ tāvad ūrdhvaṃ caṣālād yūpasyātirecayati
4.2.17	aṅgulimātraṃ kanīyo vāṅguleḥ
4.2.18	dvyaṅgulaṃ tryaṅgulaṃ caturaṅgulaṃ vaiteṣām eva takṣaṇānāṃ svaruṃ karoti
4.2.19	yaṃ kāmayetānyo 'sya lokam abhyārohed ity anyavṛkṣasya svaruṃ caṣālaṃ ca kuryāt
4.2.20	vedaṃ kṛtvāgreṇāhavanīyam
4.3.1	rathamātrīṃ vediṃ karoti
4.3.2	ratheṣāmātrīṃ prācīṃ rathākṣamātrīṃ paścāttiraścīṃ vipathayugamātrīṃ purastādudīcīm
4.3.3	api vā ṣaḍaratniṃ prācīṃ caturaratniṃ paścāttiraścīṃ tryaratniṃ purastāttiraścīm asaṃnatā bhavati
4.3.4	yat prāguttarasmāt parigrāhāt tat kṛtvā pūrvārdhe veder yūpāvaṭāyāvakāśam avaśiṣya śamyayottaravediṃ vimimīte
4.3.5	purastād ucīcīnakumbāṃ śamyāṃ nidhāya vittāyanī me 'sīti sphyenodīcīṃ lekhāṃ likhati
4.3.6	dakṣiṇataḥprācīnakumbāṃ nidhāya tiktāyanī me 'sīti dakṣiṇataḥprācīṃ paścādudīcīnakumbāṃ nidhāyāvatān mā nāthitam iti paścādudīcīmuttarataḥ prācīnakumbāṃ nidhāyāvatān mā vyathitam ity uttarataḥ prācīm abhyantaraṃ parilikhati
4.3.7	uttareṇottaraṃ vedyaṃsaṃ prakrame cātvālas taṃ parilikhaty anenaiva kalpena yad anyan mantrebhyaḥ
4.3.8	devasya tvety abhrim ādāya vider agnir nabho nāmeti khanati
4.3.9	jānudaghnaṃ trivitastaṃ vā khātvā
4.3.10	agne aṅgira ity abhriṃ praharati
4.3.11	yo 'syāṃ pṛthivyām iti pāṃsūn apādatte
4.3.12	āyuṣā nāmnehīti harati
4.3.13	yat te 'nādhṛṣṭam ity uttaravedyāṃ nivapati
4.3.14	evaṃ dvitīyaṃ haraty evaṃ tṛtīyam
4.4.1	yo dvitīyasyām iti dvitīyam apādatte yas tṛtīyasyām iti tṛtīyaṃ tūṣṇīṃ caturtham
4.4.2	siṃhīr asi mahiṣīr asīty uttaravediṃ karoti
4.4.3	uru prathasveti prathayati
4.4.4	dhruvāsīti śamyayā saṃhanti
4.4.5	devebhyaḥ kalpasveti kalpayati
4.4.6	devebhyaḥ śundhasvety adbhiḥ prokṣati
4.4.7	devebhyaḥ śumbhasveti sikatābhir anuprakirati
4.4.8	yat te krūraṃ yad āsthitam iti punar evādbhir avokṣati
4.4.9	uttarato dakṣiṇato vā sphyenaikasphyāṃ niḥsāryāpo ripraṃ nirvahatety apāṃ śeṣaṃ ninayati
4.4.10	vibhrāḍ bṛhat pibatu somyaṃ madhv āyur dadhad yajñapatāv avihrutam / vātajūto yo abhirakṣati tmanā prajāḥ piparti bahudhā virājatīty uttaravedyā antān kalpayati
4.4.11	catuḥśikhaṇḍe yuvatī kanīne ghṛtapratīke bhuvanasya madhye / tayor devā adhisaṃvasanta uttame nāka iha mādayantām iti vedim uttaravediṃ ca saṃmṛśati
4.4.12	uttaravedyāṃ madhye goṣpadamātrīm aśvaśaphamātrīṃ prādeśamātrīṃ vottaranābhiṃ karoti
4.4.13	indraghoṣas tvā vasubhiḥ purastāt pātv iti pradakṣiṇam anuparikrāman pratidiśam uttaravediṃ prokṣati
4.4.14	tvaṣṭā tvā rūpair upariṣṭāt pātv ity upariṣṭāt prokṣati
4.4.15	śeṣaṃ ninayati yathā purastāt
4.4.16	audumbaraśākhābhiś channāṃ parivāsayati yadi śvaḥ kālaḥ
4.5.1	āhavanīye 'gnipraṇayanāny ādīpayati
4.5.2	sikatāś copayamanīr upakalpayate
4.5.3	udyacchatīdhmam upayacchaty upyamanīr upayate dhāryamāṇe
4.5.4	yat te pāvaka cakṛmā kaccid āgaḥ pūrvo yat sann aparo bhavāsi / ghṛtena tvaṃ tanuvo vardhayasva mā mā hiṃsīr adhigataṃ purastād iti śeṣe juhoti
4.5.5	agnaye praṇīyamānāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati praṇīyamānāyānubrūhīti vā
4.5.6	triranūktāyāṃ haraty uttaravediṃ prāpya juhvāṃ pañcagṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā hiraṇyam antardhāyākṣṇayottaravediṃ vyāghārayati
4.5.7	siṃhīr asi sapatnasāhī svāheti dakṣiṇe 'ṃse
4.5.8	siṃhīr asi suprajāvaniḥ svāhety uttarasyāṃ śroṇyām
4.5.9	siṃhīr asi rāyaspoṣavaniḥ svāheti dakṣiṇasyāṃ śroṇyām
4.5.10	siṃhīr asy ādityavaniḥ svāhety uttare 'ṃse
4.5.11	siṃhīr asy āvaha devān devayate yajamānāya svāheti madhye
4.5.12	bhūtebhyas tveti srucaṃ hiraṇyaṃ codgṛhya
4.5.13	pautudravaiḥ paridhibhiḥ paridadhāti
4.5.14	viśvāyur asīti madhyamaṃ dhruvakṣid asīti dakṣiṇārdhyam acyatakṣid asīty uttarārdhyam
4.5.15	upakl̥ptāḥ saṃbhārā guggulusugandhitejanaṃ śuklorṇāstukā petvasyāntarāśṛṅge yā
4.5.16	tān agner bhasmāsīti sakṛd evottaranābhyāṃ nivapati
4.5.17	ūrṇāvantaṃ prathamaḥ sīda yonim ity ucyamāne yajña pratitiṣṭha sumatau suśevā ā tvā vasūni purudhā viśantu / dīrgham āyur yajamānāya kṛṇvann athāmṛtena jaritāram aṅdhi yajñaḥ pratyaṣṭhād iti saṃbhāreṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati
4.5.18	agneḥ kulāyam asīti dakṣiṇata upayamanīr upanivapati
4.5.19	manuṣvat tvā nidhīmahi manuṣvat samidhīmahi / agne manuṣvad aṅgiro devān devāyate yajety upasamindhe
4.5.20	agnir yajñaṃ nayatu prajānan mainaṃ yajñahano 'vidan / devebhyo yajñaṃ prabrūtāt pra pra yajñapatiṃ tira svāhā vāyur ādityo yajño yajñaṃ nayatu prajānan mainaṃ yajñahano 'vidan / devebhyo yajñaṃ prabrūtāt prapra yajñapatiṃ tira svāheti catasro 'timuktīr hutvā
4.5.21	juhūṃ sruvaṃ ca saṃmṛjya caturgṛhītenāṣṭagṛhītena dvādaśagṛhītena vā srucaṃ pūrayitvā sapta ta iti pūrṇāhutiṃ juhoti
4.6.1	eṣo 'trāhavanīyo yataḥ praṇīyate sa gārhapatyaḥ
4.6.2	āhavanīyaṃ gārhapatyaṃ dakṣiṇāgniṃ cānvādhāyedhmābarhir āharati
4.6.3	saptadaśa sāmidhenyo na paridhīn idhma upasaṃnahyati
4.6.4	agnīn paristīrya pāṇī prakṣālyolaparājīṃ stīrtvā
4.6.5	yathārthaṃ pāśukāni pātrāṇi prayunakti
4.6.6	sphyam agnihotrahavaṇīṃ sruvasvadhitī dve juhūvasāhomahavanīṃ dvitīyāṃ dve copabhṛtau pṛṣadājyadhānīṃ dvitīyāṃ dhruvāṃ dve ājyasthālyau dadhidhānīṃ dvitīyāṃ vedaṃ samavattadhānīṃ dve raśane dviguṇāṃ dvivyāyāmāṃ triguṇāṃ trivyāyāmāṃ dve kārṣmaryamayyau vapāśrapaṇyau dviśūlām ekaśūlāṃ ca kumbhīṃ hṛdayaśūlaṃ plakṣaśākhāṃ svaruṃ maitrāvaruṇadaṇḍaṃ yūpaṃ yūpaśakalam araṇī yena cārthaḥ
4.6.7	pavitre kṛtvā yajamāna vācaṃ yaccheti saṃpreṣyati vāgyataḥ pātrāṇi saṃmṛśati
4.6.8	prokṣiteṣu vācaṃ visṛjate
4.6.9	uttaraṃ parigrāhaṃ parigṛhya saṃpraiṣeṇa pratipadyata ājyena dadhnā codehīti saṃpraiṣasyāntaṃ saṃnamati
4.6.10	yat prāg ājyanirvapaṇāt tat kṛtvājyaṃ nirūpya dadhi pṛṣadājyārthaṃ nirvapati
4.6.11	tasminn ājyadharmāḥ kriyante yad anyad adhiśrayaṇāt
4.6.12	ājyagrahaṇakāle juhūpabhṛtoś caturgṛhīte gṛhitvā tṛtīyam ājyasya dadhany ānīya
4.6.13	jyotir asi viśvarūpaṃ viśveṣāṃ devānāṃ samid iti pañcagṛhītaṃ pṛṣadājyaṃ gṛhṇāti mahīnāṃ payo 'sīti vā
4.6.14	yathāprakṛti dhruvāyām
4.6.15	sanneṣv ājyeṣu yūpasaṃmānena pratipadyate
4.6.16	devasya tvety abhrim ādāya parilikhitam iti triḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ yūpāvaṭaṃ parilikhaty ardham antarvedy ardhaṃ bahirvedi
4.6.17	parilikhyāgnīd yūpāvaṭaṃ khanoparasaṃmitaṃ dvyaṅgulena tryaṅgulena caturaṅgulena voparam atikhanatād iti saṃpreṣyati
4.6.18	uparamātraṃ khātvā
4.7.1	yat te śilpaḥ parāvadhīt takṣā hastena vāśyā / āpas te tad yajñiyāḥ punantu śucayaḥ śuca iti yūpaṃ prakṣālayati
4.7.2	yavamatīḥ prokṣaṇīḥ kṛtvā pṛthivyai tveti mūlaṃ prokṣaty antarikṣāya tveti madhyaṃ dive tvety agraṃ śundhatāṃ lokaḥ pitṛṣadana iti yūpāvaṭe 'po 'vanayati
4.7.3	yavo 'sīti yavaṃ prāsyati pitṝṇāṃ sadanam asīti prācā barhiṣāvastṛṇāti
4.7.4	svāveśo 'sīti pratham aparāpātitaṃ śakalam adhastātvakkam avaṭe 'vadadhāti ghṛtena dyāvāpṛthivī āpṛṇethāṃ svāheti hiraṇyam antardhāya sruveṇābhijuhoti
4.7.5	yūpāyājyamānāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyaty ajyamānāyānubrūhīti vāgreṇāhavanīyaṃ laukikenājyena purastāt pratyaṅ tiṣṭhan yajamāno yūpaśakalenānakti
4.7.6	laukikeneti
4.7.7	devasas tvā savitā madhvānaktv ity agram aindram asīti caṣālam
4.7.8	supippalābhyas tvauṣadhībhya iti caṣālaṃ pratimuñcati
4.7.9	devas tvā savitā madhvānaktv ity āntam agniṣṭhām aśrim anakti
4.7.10	raśanādeśe triḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ parimṛśati madhye vā
4.7.11	anaktam uparam
4.7.12	āñjanaprabhṛti yajamāno yūpaṃ nānūtsṛjaty ā parivyayaṇāt
4.7.13	yūpāyocchrīyamāṇāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyaty ucchrīyamāṇāyānubrūhīti vā
4.7.14	ud divaṃ stabhānāntarikṣam ity ucchrayati
4.7.15	te te dhāmānīty avaṭe 'vadadhāti
4.7.16	viṣṇoḥ karmāṇi paśyateti dvābhyāṃ kalpayaty agnināgniṣṭhāṃ sadiśaṃ minoti
4.8.1	yaṃ kāmayeta tejasainaṃ devatābhir indriyeṇa vyardhayeyam ity agniṣṭhāṃ tasyāśrim āhavanīyād itthaṃ vetthaṃ vātināvayet tejasaivainaṃ devatābhir indriyeṇa vyardhayati yaṃ kāmayeta tejasainaṃ devatābhir indriyeṇa samardhyeyam ity agniṣṭhāṃ tasyāśrim āhavanīyena saṃminuyāt
4.8.2	agniṃ pratyupanataṃ bahiṣṭhe nirṇutam anāvir uparaṃ saṃminoti
4.8.3	brahmavaniṃ tveti pradakṣiṇaṃ purīṣeṇa paryūhati
4.8.4	brahma dṛṃheti maitrāvaruṇadaṇḍena paridṛṃhati
4.8.5	unnambhaya pṛthivīm iti pradakṣiṇam apo 'nupariṣiñcati
4.8.6	devasya tveti triguṇāṃ trivyāyāmāṃ dārvīṃ raśanām ādāya
4.8.7	idaṃ viṣṇur vicakrama iti saraśanena pāṇinā yūpaṃ trir unmārṣṭi
4.8.8	tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam iti yūpasyāgraṃ prekṣate
4.8.9	yūpāya parivīyamāṇāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati parivīyamāṇāyānubrūhīti vā
4.8.10	parivīr asīti tayā nābhideśe triḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ parivyayati madhye vā
4.8.11	uttaramuttaraṃ guṇaṃ karoti
4.8.12	yaṃ kāmayetorjainaṃ vyardhayeyam ity ūrdhvāṃ vā tasyāvācīṃ vāvohet
4.8.13	yadi kāmayeta varṣukaḥ parjanyaḥ syād ity avācīm avohet
4.8.14	yadi kāmayetāvarṣukaḥ syād ity ūrdhvām udūhet
4.8.15	yaṃ kāmayeta stry asya jāyetety upānte tasya vyatiṣajya na praveṣṭayed yaṃ kāmayeta pumān asya jāyetety āntaṃ tasya praveṣṭya sthavimad aṇīyasi pravayati
4.8.16	divaḥ sānur asīti svarum ādatte divaḥ sūnur asīti vā divaḥ sānūpeṣeti vāntarikṣasya tvā sānāv avagūhāmīty uttareṇāgniṣṭhāṃ madhyame guṇe svarum upagūhaty uttame vā
4.9.1	upakl̥ptaḥ paśur akūṭo 'karṇo 'kāṇo 'khañjo 'khaṇḍo 'ṣaṇḍho 'ghṛṣṭo 'śloṇo 'saptaśaphaḥ pannadañ chāgo yamānyataro yūthyo mātṛmān pitṛmān bhrātṛmān sakhimāṃs taṃ snāpayati
4.9.2	iṣe tveti barhiṣī ādātte
4.9.3	upavīr asīti plakṣaśākhām
4.9.4	indrāgnibhyāṃ tvā juṣṭam upākaromy upo devān daivīr viśaḥ prajāpater jāyamānā imaṃ paśuṃ paśupate ta iti barhirbhyāṃ plakṣaśākhayā ca paśum upākaroti
4.9.5	prajānanta ity upākṛtya pañca juhoti
4.9.6	paśupateḥ paśavo virūpāḥ sadṛśā uta / teṣāṃ yaṃ vivrire devās taṃ svarāḍ anumanyatām iti vā madhye pañcamīṃ juhoti
4.9.7	agner janitram asīty adhimanthanaśakalam ādāyāpareṇāhavanīyaṃ barhiṣi nidadhāti
4.9.8	vṛṣaṇau stha iti prāñcau darbhau śakale 'vadadhāti
4.9.9	urvaśy asīty adharāraṇim ādatte purūravā ity uttarāraṇim
4.9.10	ghṛtenākte ity ājyasthālyā bile 'nakti
4.9.11	āyur asīti samavadadhāti vṛṣaṇaṃ dadhāthām iti vā
4.9.12	agnaye mathyamānāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati mathyamānāyānubrūhīti vā
4.9.13	trir anūktāyāṃ gāyatraṃ chando 'nuprajāyasvety etais triḥ pradakṣiṇam ārabhya yathāsukham ata ūrdhvaṃ manthati
4.9.14	jātāyānubrūhīti
4.10.1	jāte saṃpreṣyati prahriyamāṇāyānubrūhīti prahriyamāṇe
4.10.2	bhavataṃ naḥ samanasāv ity agreṇottaraṃ paridhisaṃdhiṃ praharati
4.10.3	agnāv agnir iti prahṛtya sruveṇābhijuhoti
4.10.4	devasya tveti dviguṇāṃ dvivyāyāmāṃ dārbhīṃ raśanām ādāya tasya raśanāntena dakṣiṇaṃ bāhum unmārṣṭi
4.10.5	ṛtasya tvā devahaviḥ pāśenārabha iti dakṣiṇe pūrvapāde 'rdhaśirasi ca pratimuñcati
4.10.6	dharṣā mānuṣān iti purastāt pratyañcam udañcaṃ vā yūpe niyunakti
4.10.7	adbhyas tvauṣadhībhyaḥ prokṣāmīti prokṣati
4.10.8	apāṃ perur asīti pāyayati
4.10.9	svāttaṃ cit sadevam ity adhastād upokṣati
4.10.10	sāmidhenīprabhṛtīni karmāṇi pratipadyate
4.10.11	āghāram āghārya paśuṃ samanakti
4.10.12	saṃ te prāṇa iti dakṣiṇe 'rdhaśirasi saṃ yajatrair aṅgānīty aṃsoccāre saṃ yajñapatir āśiṣeti bhasadi
4.10.13	dhruvāsamañjanaprabhṛtīni karmāṇi pratipadyate
4.10.14	pravaraṃ pravṛtya
4.10.15	maitrāvaruṇāya daṇḍaṃ prayacchati
4.10.16	avikṣuro vikhuro bhūyāsam iti pratigṛhṇāti
4.10.17	prayājānūyājeṣu paśupuroḍāśasviṣṭakṛti vanaspatau paśusviṣṭakṛti ca yājyāsaṃpraiṣasya praiṣāḥ
4.10.18	tatrādhvaryur āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite 'muṣmai preṣyeti maitrāvaruṇaṃ preṣyati sa hotāraṃ codayati
4.10.19	samidbhyaḥ preṣyeti prathamaṃ prayājaṃ saṃpreṣyati preṣya preṣyety uttarān
4.10.20	caturthe samānīyāṣṭame sarvaṃ samānayate
4.10.21	daśeṣṭvaikādaśāyājyam avaśiṣya
4.10.22	ghṛtenāktāv iti juhvā svarusvadhitī anakti
4.10.23	dviḥ svaruṃ sakṛt svadhiter anyatarāṃ dhārām
4.10.24	ghṛtenāktau paśuṃ trayethām iti tābhyāṃ paśuṃ samanakti
4.10.25	śamitar eṣā te 'śriḥ prajñātāsad ity aktāṃ dhārām ādiśañ chamitre svadhitiṃ prayacchati
4.10.26	yathāsthānaṃ svarum avaguhya
4.11.1	paryagnaye kriyamānāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati paryagnaye 'nubrūhīti vā
4.11.2	āhavanīyād ulmukam ādāyāgnīdhraḥ pari vājapatir iti pañca paryagni karoti paśuṃ śāmitradeśaṃ cātvālaṃ yūpam āhavanīyaṃ ca triḥ paridravati
4.11.3	ājyāni cety ekeṣām
4.11.4	ye badhyamānam anubadhyamānā iti paryagnau kriyamāṇe trīṇy apāvyāni juhoti
4.11.5	āhavanīya ulmukaṃ nidhāya triḥ punaḥ pratiparyeti
4.11.6	pramucya paśum āśrāvya pratyāśrāvita upapreṣya hotar havyā devebhya iti saṃpreṣyati
4.11.7	adhriguṃ hotā pratipadyate
4.11.8	revatīr yajñapatiṃ priyadhāniśateti barhirbhyāṃ vapāśrapaṇībhyāṃ plakṣaśākhayā ca paśum anvārabhete yajamāno 'dhvaryuś ca
4.11.9	nānā prāṇa ity adhvaryur yajamānam abhimantrayate
4.11.10	prāsmā agniṃ bharatety ucyamāne tad evolmukam ādāyāgnīdhraḥ pūrvaḥ pratipadyate
4.11.11	uro antarikṣety antareṇa cātvālotkarāv udañco niṣkrāmanti
4.11.12	uttareṇa cātvālaṃ śāmitradeśas tasminn ulmukaṃ nidhāyottareṇa śāmitram atikrāmati
4.11.13	udīcīnāṃ asya pado nidhattād ity ucyamāne sam asya tanuvā bhavety upākaraṇayor barhiṣor anyatarat prāgagram udagagraṃ vā nyasyati tasminn enaṃ pratyakśirasam udīcīnapādaṃ nighnanty amāyuṃ kṛṇvantaṃ saṃjñapayatācchaṅkyaṃ prabrūtād ity uktvā
4.11.14	parāṅ āvartate yajamāno 'dhvaryuś ca nānā prāṇa ity adhvaryur yajamānam abhimantrayate
4.11.15	iha paśavo viśvarūpā ramantām agniṃ kulāyam abhisaṃvasānāḥ / asmāṃ avantu payasā ghṛtena / yāsām ūdhaś caturbilaṃ madhoḥ pūrṇaṃ ghṛtasya ca / tā naḥ payasvatīḥ santv asmin goṣṭha ṛtāvṛdha iti pṛṣadājyam avekṣamāṇau vāgyatāv āsāte yajamāno 'dhvaryuś ca
4.11.16	indrasya bhāgaḥ suvite dadhātanemaṃ yajñaṃ yajamānaṃ ca sūrau / yo no dveṣṭy anu taṃ rabhasvānāgaso yajamānasya vīrā ity adhvaryuḥ paśum abhimantrayate yadi rauti
4.12.1	yat paśur māyum akṛteti saṃjñapte juhoti
4.12.2	śamitāra upetaneti saṃjñaptam upāyanti
4.12.3	aditiḥ pāśaṃ pramumoktv etam iti paśoḥ pāśaṃ pramucyaikaśūlayopasajjya cātvāle 'vadadhāti
4.12.4	abhicarato 'rātīyantam adharaṃ kṛṇomīti śuṣke sthāṇau darbhastambe vābhinidadhāti
4.12.5	namas ta ātāneti patny ādityam upatiṣṭhate
4.12.6	anarvā prehīti pratiprasthātā pūrṇapātraṃ dhārayamāṇāṃ patnīm udānayati

4.12.8	pratiṣiddham ekeṣām
4.12.9	etenaiva sarve samutkramya cātvāle mārjayante
4.12.10	adhvaryur abhiṣiñcati patny āpyāyayati patny abhiṣiñcaty adhvaryur āpyāyayatīty ekeṣām
4.12.11	vāk ta āpyāyatām ity etair yathārūpam
4.12.12	nābhis ta āpyāyatām iti nābhiṃ meḍhraṃ ta āpyāyatām iti meḍhraṃ pāyus ta āpyāyatām iti pāyuṃ śuddhāś caritrā iti saṃnidhāya pādāñ śam ahobhyām ity anupṛṣṭhaṃ śeṣaṃ ninayati
4.12.13	uttānaṃ paśum āvṛtyauṣadhe trāyasvainam ity upākaraṇayor barhiṣor avaśiṣṭaṃ dakṣiṇena nābhiṃ dvyaṅgule tryaṅgule caturaṅgule vā vapādeśe nidadhāti
4.12.14	svadhite mainaṃ hiṃsīr iti svadhitinā tiryag ācchinatti
4.12.15	chinnasya tṛṇasyāgraṃ pāṇau kṛtvā sthavimal lohite 'ṅktvā rakṣasāṃ bhāgo 'sīty uttarāparam avāntaradeśaṃ nirasyāpa upaspṛśya
4.12.16	iṣe tveti vapām utkhidaty ūrje tveti tanniṣṭhayaikaśūlayopatṛṇatti
4.12.17	devebhyaḥ śundhasvety adbhiḥ prokṣati devebhyaḥ śumbhasveti svadhitinā vapāṃ nimārṣṭi
4.12.18	ghṛtena dyāvāpṛthivī prorṇvāthām iti dviśūlām ekaśūlāṃ ca pracchādayati
4.12.19	indrāgnibhyāṃ tvā juṣṭām utkṛntāmīty utkṛntaty acchinno rāyaḥ savīra iti vā
4.12.20	muṣṭinā śamitā vapodgrahaṇam abhigṛhyāsta āvapāhomāt
4.12.21	pratyuṣṭam iti śāmitre vapāṃ pratitapati
4.12.22	namaḥ sūryasya saṃdṛśe yuyothā ity ādityam upatiṣṭhate
4.12.23	śrapaṇārtham agnim avaśiṣya tad evolmukam ādāyāgnīdhraḥ pūrvaḥ pratipadyate
4.12.24	urv antarikṣam iti gacchati
4.12.25	vapāśrapaṇī punar anvārabhete yajamāno 'dhvaryuś ca
4.13.1	upa tvāgne divediva iti tisṛbhir āhavanīyam upāyanti
4.13.2	upasṛṣṭa ulmuke pratyuṣṭam ity āhavanīyasyāntime 'ṅgāre vapāṃ nigṛhṇāti
4.13.3	vāyo vīhi stokānām iti barhiṣo 'graṃ prāsyaty adhastād vapāyā upāsyatīty ekeṣām
4.13.4	antarā yūpam āhavanīyaṃ ca pratiprasthātre vapāṃ prayacchati
4.13.5	dakṣiṇata udaṅṅ āsīnaḥ pratiprasthātā vapāṃ śrapayati
4.13.6	tvām u te dadhire havyavāham iti vapām abhijuhoti
4.13.7	prādurbhūteṣu stokeṣu stokebhyo 'nubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
4.13.8	śyenīṃ suśṛtāṃ kṛtvā supippalā oṣadhīḥ kṛdhīti dakṣiṇasyāṃ vediśroṇyāṃ plakṣaśākhāyāṃ nidadhāti
4.13.9	prayutā dveṣāṃsi iti vapāśrapaṇī pravṛhati
4.13.10	srucau hotādāpayati ghṛtavatīm adhvaryo srucam āsyasvety ucyamāne juhūpabhṛtāv ādāyātyākramyāśrāvya pratyāśrāvite svāhākṛtībhyaḥ preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati vaṣaṭkṛte hutā pratyākramya prāyājaśeṣeṇa pṛṣadājyam abhighārya vapām abhighārayati dvir vapāṃ sakṛt pṛṣadājyam
4.13.11	dhruvāṃ vā prathamaṃ yady ājyabhāgau yakṣyan bhavati kṛtākṛtāv ājyabhāgau
4.13.12	juhvām upastīrya hiraṇyaśakalam avadhāya kṛtsnāṃ vapām avadyaty upariṣṭāddhiraṇyaśakalam avadhāyābhidhāryendrāgnibhyāṃ chāgasya vapāyā medaso 'nubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
4.13.13	āśrāvya na preṣyati maitrāvaruṇo hotāraṃ codayati
4.13.14	purastād vapāyā homāt svāhā devebhya iti pūrvaṃ parivapyaṃ juhoti
4.13.15	jātavedo vapayā gaccha devān iti vaṣaṭkṛte vapāṃ devebhyaḥ svāhety uttaram
4.13.16	pratyākramya svāhordhvanabhasaṃ mārutaṃ gacchatam iti viṣūcī vapāśrapaṇī praharati prācīṃ dviśūlāṃ pratīcīm ekaśūlām
4.13.17	saṃsrāveṇābhihutya
4.13.18	cātvāle mārjayante
4.14.1	āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhir idam āpaḥ pravahatāvadyaṃ ca malaṃ ca yat / yac cābhidudrohānṛtaṃ yac ca śepe abhīruṇam / agnir mā tasmād enaso viśvān muñcatv aṃhasaḥ / nir mā muñcāmi śapathān nir mā varuṇād uta / nir mā yamasya paḍbīśāt sarvasmād devakilbiṣād atho manuṣyakilbiṣād iti mārjayitvā
4.14.2	paśupuroḍāśasya pātrasaṃsādanaprabhṛtīni karmāṇi pratipadyate yathārtham auṣadhapātrāṇi prayunakty ekādaśa dvādaśa vā kapālāni taiḥ saha śūrpaṃ kṛṣṇājinaṃ śamyām ulūkhalaṃ musalaṃ dṛṣadam upalāṃ kuṭaruṃ pātrīṃ mekṣaṇaṃ vedaṃ prāśitraharaṇaṃ praṇītāpraṇayanam iḍāpātraṃ ca

4.14.29	tasmin kṛte juhvāṃ pañcagṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā

4.14.33	saṃ te manasā mana iti pṛṣadājyena hṛdayam abhighārayati

4.15.1	juhūpabhṛtor vasāhomahavanyāṃ samavattadhānyā copastṛṇīte

4.15.4	hṛdayasyāgre 'vadyaty atha jihvāyā atha vakṣasa ity eteṣām anupūrvam avadāya

4.16.1	yājyāyāḥ pratiprasthātā vasāhomaṃ juhoti
4.16.2	vasāhomodrekeṇa diśaḥ prati yajati
4.16.3	diśa iti purastāt pradiśa iti dakṣiṇata ādiśa iti paścād vidiśa ity uttarata uddiśa iti madhye svāheti sarvatrānuṣajati
4.16.4	svāhā digbhya iti pradakṣiṇam anupariṣiñcati
4.16.5	namo digbhya iti hutvopatiṣṭhate
4.16.6	atraiva tiṣṭhan pṛṣadājyasruvaṃ juhvām ānīya vanaspataye 'nubrūhi vanaspataye preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati
4.16.7	aupabhṛtaṃ juhvāṃ paryasyāgnaye sviṣṭakṛte 'nubrūhy agnaye sviṣṭakṛte preṣyeti paśusviṣṭakṛti saṃpreṣyati

4.17.1	etaiḥ pratiprathātānuyājānāṃ hutaṃhutam upayajati
