7.11.14	agniṃ rājānaṃ cāntareṇa mā saṃcāriṣṭeti saṃpreṣyati
7.11.15	udvapanaprabhṛtīni karmāṇi pratipadyate
7.11.16	gārhapatye nava kapālāny upadadhāti
7.11.17	caturgṛhītāny ājyāni gṛhṇāti
7.11.18	caturhotrātithyam āsādayati
7.11.19	saṃbhārayajūṃṣi vyākhyāya nirmanthyasyāvṛtā nirmanthyena pracarati
7.11.20	vedaṃ nidhāya sāmidhenībhyaḥ saṃpreṣyati
7.11.21	sarvam idhmam ādadhāti sarvam aupabhṛtaṃ samānayate
7.11.22	ājyabhāgābhyāṃ pracarya viṣṇuṃ haviṣā yajati
7.11.23	dhruvāyāḥ śeṣaṃ karoti
7.11.24	iḍāntātithyā saṃtiṣṭhate
7.11.25	dhruvāśeṣād āpataye tvā gṛhṇāmīti kaṃse camase vā tānūnaptraṃ samavadyati caturavattaṃ pañcāvattaṃ vā
7.11.26	avaśiṣṭo vikalpārtho yadi caturavattam
7.11.27	tad anādhṛṣṭam asīti sarvartvijaḥ samavamṛśanti
7.11.28	samavamṛṣṭaṃ prajāpatau tvā manasi juhomīti trir avaghrāyāntarvedi ninayati
7.11.29	pratiṣiddham ekeṣām
7.11.30	asaṃcara utsiñcatīty ekeṣām
7.11.31	agnīn madanty āpā3 iti pṛcchati
7.11.32	madanti devīr amṛtā ṛtāvṛdha ity agnīdhraḥ pratyāha
7.11.33	tābhir ādraveti saṃpreṣyati
7.11.34	madantībhiḥ pāṇīn prakṣālayante brahmā rājānaṃ visraṃsayati
7.11.35	aṃśuraṃśur iti taṃ sarve sahiraṇyaiḥ pāṇibhir āpyāyayanti
7.11.36	pratyupanaddhe 'pa upaspṛśyaiṣṭā rāya iti prastare nihnuvate savyānnīcaḥ pāṇīnkṛtvā dakṣiṇānuttānān
7.12.1	pravargyeṇa pracaryopasadā pracaraty upasadā vā pracarya pravargyeṇa pracarati
7.12.2	yad ātithyāyā barhis tad upasadāṃ tad agnīṣomīyasya tat prastaraparidhi
7.12.3	stīrṇaṃ prastarabarhir upasatsu śayāḥ paridhayaḥ
7.12.4	upasadas tantraṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
7.12.5	tasyām ājyaṃ haviḥ
7.12.6	agniḥ somo viṣṇur devatāḥ
7.12.7	upāṃśuyājena kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
7.12.8	agnīn anvādhāya ṣoḍaśadārum idhmaṃ saṃnahyati
7.12.9	vedaṃ kṛtvāgnīn paristīrya pāṇī prakṣālyolaparājīṃ stīrtvā yathārtham ājyapātrāṇi prayunakti sphyaṃ sruvaṃ sruca ājyasthālīṃ yena cārthaḥ
7.12.10	pavitre kṛtvā yajamāna vācaṃ yaccheti saṃpreṣyati vāgyataḥ pātrāṇi saṃmṛśati prokṣiteṣu vācaṃ visṛjate
7.12.11	sphyam ādāya stīrṇāyā veder lomabhyo 'dhi stambayajur haraty uttaraṃ parigrāhaṃ parigṛhya saṃpraiṣeṇa pratipadyate
7.12.12	yad anyad barhiṣaḥ patnīsaṃnahanāc ca tat saṃpreṣyati
7.12.13	yat prāg ājyagrahaṇāt tat kṛtvā dhruvāyām eva gṛhṇāti
7.12.14	prokṣaṇīr abhimantrya brahmāṇam āmantryedhmaṃ vediṃ ca prokṣya prokṣaṇyavaśeṣaṃ ninīya pavitre apisṛjyāgnim abhimantrya pūrvām āghārasamidham ādhāya dhruvāṃ sruvaṃ ca sādayaty eṣāsadad iti mantraṃ saṃnamati viṣṇv asi vaiṣṇavaṃ dhāma prājāpatyam ity ājyam abhimantrayate
7.12.15	vedaṃ nidhāya sāmidhenībhyaḥ saṃpreṣyati navadhedhmaṃ prativibhajya sarvam idhmam ādadhāti
7.12.16	oḍhāsu devatāsv agnim upavājya sruvāghāram āghāryāgnīt paridhīṃś cāgniṃ ca tristriḥ saṃmṛḍḍhīti saṃpreṣyati saṃmṛṣṭe pravaraṃ pravṛṇīte yathā mahāpitṛyajñe sīda hotar ity uktvā
7.13.1	dhruvāyā aṣṭau juhvāṃ gṛhṇāti catur upabhṛti
7.13.2	sādayati srucau hotādāpayati
7.13.3	ghṛtavatīm adhvaryo srucam āsyasvety ucyamāne juhūpabhṛtāv ādāya sakṛd atikrāntas tisro devatā yajati
7.13.4	uttarataḥ prathamāyāḥ puronuvākyāṃ saṃpreṣyati dakṣiṇata itarayoḥ
7.13.5	yaj juhvām ājyaṃ tasyārdhenāgniṃ yajaty ardhena somam
7.13.6	yad upabhṛti taj juhvām ānīya tena viṣṇum
7.13.7	pratyākramya yā te agne 'yāśayā tanūr iti sruveṇopasadaṃ juhoti
7.13.8	madantībhiḥ pāṇīn prakṣālayante brahmā rājānaṃ visraṃsayaty āpyāyayanti nihnuvate ca yathā purastād dakṣiṇottānaiḥ pūrvāhṇe savyottānair aparāhṇe
7.13.9	agnīddevapatnīrvyācakṣva subrahmaṇya subrahmaṇyāmāhvayeti saṃpreṣyati
7.13.10	vāg vāyoḥ patnīty apareṇa gārhapatyam upaviśyāgnīdhro devapatnīr vyācaṣṭe senendrasya dheneti vā
7.13.11	subrahmaṇyaḥ subrahmaṇyām āhvayati
7.13.12	anūpasadam etāni kriyante
7.13.13	evaṃ trirātraṃ sāyaṃprātaḥ pravargyopasadbhyāṃ pracarati
7.13.14	supūrvāhṇe paurvāhṇikībhyāṃ svaparāhṇa āparāhṇikībhyām
7.13.15	yā te agne 'yāśayā tanūr iti prathame 'hani sāyaṃprātaḥ sruvapradānāṃ juhoti
7.13.16	yā te agne rajāśayeti dvitīye
7.13.17	yā te agne harāśayeti tṛtīye
7.13.18	yadi puro yudhyeyur ayaḥ prathamāyām avadhāya juhuyāt
7.13.19	rajataṃ hiraṇyaṃ madhyamāyām
7.13.20	haritam uttamāyām
7.13.21	yadi saṅgrāmaṃ yudhyeyur ity ekeṣām
7.13.22	ayajñasaṃyuktaḥ kalpaḥ
7.14.1	madhyamābhyāṃ paurvāhṇikībhyāṃ pravargyopasadbhyāṃ pracaryāgreṇa prāgvaṃśaṃ trīn prācaḥ prakramān prakramya śaṅkuṃ nihanti sa paścārdhe vedeḥ
7.14.2	vimime tvā payasvatīṃ devānāṃ dhenuṃ sudughām anapasphurantīm indraḥ somaṃ pibatu kṣemo astu na iti ṣaṭtriṃśat prācaḥ prakramān prakramya śaṅkuṃ nihanti sa pūrvārdhe
7.14.3	paścārdhyāc chaṅkoḥ pañcadaśa dakṣiṇataḥ pañcadaśottarataḥ prakramya śaṅkū nihanti te śroṇī pūrvārdhyāc chaṅkor dvādaśa dakṣiṇato dvādaśottarataḥ prakramya śaṅkū nihanti tāv aṃsau
7.14.4	akṣṇayā mānena saṃpādya pradakṣiṇaṃ spandyayā paryātanoti
7.14.5	anvātanoti pṛṣṭhyām
7.14.6	tāṃ karoti yathā darśapūrṇamāsayor yad anyat saṃnāmāt
7.14.7	sphyena vighanena parśvā paraśunā ca
7.14.8	yat prāg uttarasmāt parigrāhāt tat kṛtvottaravedyāḥ kalpena daśapadām uttaravediṃ karoti
7.14.9	aṃhīyasīṃ purastād ity ekeṣām
7.14.10	uttareṇottaraṃ vedyaṃsaṃ prakrame cātvālaḥ paścād dvādaśasūtkaro vidyate 'parimite vā
7.14.11	tāv antareṇa vedeḥ saṃcaraḥ
7.14.12	prācīnam āgnīdhrāt pratīcīnaṃ cātvālād ity ekeṣām
7.14.13	udumbaraśākhābhiś channāṃ parivāsayati
7.14.14	śvo bhūte
7.15.1	uttamābhyāṃ paurvāhṇikībhyāṃ pravargyopasadbhyāṃ pracaryārdhavrataṃ pradāya tadānīm evāparāhṇikībhyāṃ pravargyopasadbhyāṃ pracarati
7.15.2	pravargyam udvāsyopasadam upaiti yadi pūrvo bhavati
7.15.3	ardhavrataṃ pradāyāgner āvṛtāgniṃ praṇīyāgnyāyatana ūrṇāstukāṃ nidhāyāgniṃ pratiṣṭhāpyāmikṣāyai maitrāvaruṇyai sāyaṃdohāya vatsān apākaroti
7.15.4	indrāya ca dadhigharmāya gharmadugho vatsam
7.15.5	sarvāṇy aindrāṇi bhavantīty ekeṣām
7.15.6	agnivaty uttaraṃ parigrāhaṃ parigṛhṇāti
7.15.7	na parigṛhītām aprokṣitām adhicaraty āstaraṇāt
7.15.8	sutyārthāni kāṣṭhāni māhāvedikaṃ ca barhir upakl̥ptaṃ bhavati tūṣṇīkābhir adbhiḥ kāṣṭhāni vediṃ barhiś ca tristriḥ prokṣati
7.15.9	tūṣṇīṃ barhiṣā vediṃ stṛṇāti yathā darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ
7.15.10	ā ghā ye agnim indhate stṛṇanti barhir ānuṣak / yeṣām indro yuvā sakheti staraṇīm eke samāmananti
7.16.1	upakl̥pte śakaṭe maṇḍalacakre prayuktapūrve tayoḥ purāṇān granthīn visrasya prakṣālya navān kurvanti cchadiṣmatī yugyakṛte kṛtvāgreṇa prāgvaṃśam avasthāpya yuñjate mana ity auttaravedike juhoti
7.16.2	devaśrutāv iti padatṛtīyasyaikadeśena patnī dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasya dakṣiṇām akṣadhuraṃ dakṣiṇenottānena triḥ parācīnam upānakty evam uttarasya
7.16.3	sarvā upānaktīty ekeṣām
7.16.4	ājyena cety ekeṣām
7.16.5	havirdhānābhyāṃ pravartyamānābhyām anubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati pravartyamānābhyām anubrūhīti vā
7.16.6	trir anūkāyāṃ prācī pretam iti samudgṛhṇantaḥ prācī pravartayanti
7.16.7	suvāg deva duryāṃ āvadety abhimantrayate yady akṣa utsarjet
7.16.8	yatra vedim avakrāmatas tad dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasyottarasyāṃ vartanyāṃ vedyante hiraṇyaṃ nidhāyedaṃ viṣṇur iti juhoti
7.16.9	irāvatī dhenumatī ity evaṃ pratiprasthātottarasya
7.16.10	adhvaryur dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasya karmāṇi karoti pratiprasthātottarasya
7.16.11	apa janyaṃ bhayaṃ nudāpa cakrāṇi vartaya gṛhaṃ somasya gacchatam indrasya saṃsadam iti paścārdhe veder vitṛtīyadeśe manasā hotā padā janyaṃ bhayaṃ pratinudaty adhvaryur yajamāno brahmā vā
7.16.12	apareṇottaravediṃ trīn pratīcaḥ prakramān prativikramyātra ramethām ity abhitaḥ pṛṣṭhyāṃ nabhyasthe sthāpayataḥ
7.16.13	yathārthaṃ havirdhānayoḥ
7.17.1	antarālaṃ kurutaḥ
7.17.2	vaiṣṇavam asi viṣṇus tvottabhnātv ity upastabhnutaḥ
7.17.3	purastādunnate bhavataḥ
7.17.4	divo vā viṣṇav uta vā pṛthivyā ity āśīr padayarcā dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasya dakṣiṇaṃ karṇātardam apareṇa methīṃ nihanti viṣṇor nu kam ity uttarasyottaraṃ karṇātardam apareṇa pratiprasthātā
7.17.5	viṣṇor dhruvam asīti tatraite nibadhnītaḥ
7.17.6	viṣṇor dhruvo 'sīti granthī kurutas tau prajñātau bhavataḥ
7.17.7	ūrdhvāḥ śamyāḥ samutkṛṣyopariṣṭāt pariveṣṭayato yathāsuṣṭhu
7.17.8	paryantyāḥ sthūṇā minutaḥ
7.17.9	yathāgreṇa kharaṃ saṃcaro bhavati
7.17.10	agreṇa havirdhāne sthūṇe nihatya tayor udagagraṃ vaṃśaṃ nidhāya prāco vaṃśān ādadhāti
7.17.11	viṣṇoḥ pṛṣṭham asīti madhyamaṃ chadir adhi nidadhāti
7.17.12	viṣṇo rarāṭam asīti purastād rarāṭīṃ pariśrayati
7.17.13	tejanī rarāṭyaiṣīkī prācyanūkāṇḍā madhye vitatāṃ tāṃ vaṃśe nibadhnāti
7.17.14	viṣṇoḥ śnyaptre stha iti rarāṭyā antau vyavāsyati
7.17.15	kaṭāṃs tejanīś ca pravartaṃ chadiṣām antarāleṣv anvavasyanti
7.17.16	tān antarvartā ity ācakṣate
7.17.17	pari tvā girvaṇo gira ity abhitaḥ pariśrayataḥ
7.17.18	pūrvam aparaṃ ca dvāre kurutaḥ
7.17.19	adhvaryur dakṣiṇāṃ dvāreyīṃ pariṣīvyati pratiprasthātottarām
7.17.20	viṣṇoḥ syūr asīti sīvyataḥ
7.17.21	viṣṇor dhruvo 'sīti granthī kurutas tau prajñātau bhavataḥ
7.17.22	vaiṣṇavam asi viṣṇave tveti saṃmitam abhimṛśataḥ
7.17.23	pra tad viṣṇuḥ stavate vīryāya mṛgo na bhīmaḥ kucaro giriṣṭhāḥ / yasyoruṣu triṣu vikramaṇeṣv adhikṣiyanti bhuvanāni viśveti saṃmitāddhavirdhānāt prāg upaniṣkrāmataḥ
7.17.24	upaniṣkramya vā japataḥ
7.17.25	trīn prācaḥ prakramān prakramya japata ity ekeṣām
7.18.1	dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasya purokṣaṃ catvāra uparavā bhavanty avāntaradeśeṣu prādeśamukhāḥ prādeśāntarālā bāhumātrāḥ saṃtṛṇṇā adhastād vidhṛtā upariṣṭāt
7.18.2	abhrer ādānaṃ parilekhanaṃ ca yūpe vyākhyātam
7.18.3	pūrvayor dakṣiṇaṃ parilikhyāparayor uttaraṃ parilikhaty aparayor dakṣiṇaṃ pūrvayoruttaram
7.18.4	evam anupūrvāṇy eṣāṃ karmāṇi kriyante
7.18.5	rakṣohaṇo valaganano vaiṣṇavān khanāmīti khanati
7.18.6	rakṣohaṇo valagahano vaiṣṇavān niṣkhidāmīti niṣkhidati
7.18.7	bṛhann asīty abhriṃ praharati
7.18.8	virāḍ asīti bāhum upāvaharati bāhū vā
7.18.9	idam ahaṃ taṃ valagam udvapāmīti pāṃsūn udvapati
7.18.10	idam enam adharaṃ karomīty uparavabile 'vabādhate
7.18.11	nirasto balaga iti harati
7.18.12	avabāḍho durasyur iti yatra kharaṃ kariṣyan bhavati tasmin deśe nivapati
7.18.13	evam itareṣu
7.18.14	uttareṇottareṇa mantreṇa bāhum upāvaharaty uttareṇottareṇa ca chandasā nigṛhṇāti
7.18.15	gāyatraṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ jāgatam ānuṣṭubham ity āmnātāni chandāṃsi
7.18.16	virāḍ asīti pūrvayor dakṣiṇaṃ yajamāno 'vamṛśati samrāḍ asīty aparayor uttaram adhvaryuḥ
7.18.17	saṃmṛśa imān āyuṣe varcase ca devānāṃ nidhir asi dveṣoyavano yuyodhy asmad dveṣāṃsi yāni kāni cakṛma devānām idaṃ nihitaṃ yad asty athābhāhi pradiśaś catasraḥ kṛṇvāno anyāṃ adharān sapatnān ity adhastāt saṃmṛśataḥ
7.18.18	kim atrety adhvaryuḥ pṛcchati bhadram iti yajamānaḥ pratyāha tan nau sahety adhvaryuḥ
7.18.19	svarāḍ asīty aparayor dakṣiṇaṃ yajamāno 'vamṛśati viśvārāḍ asīti pūrvayor uttaram adhvaryuḥ
7.18.20	saṃmṛśato yathā purastāt
7.18.21	kim atreti yajamānaḥ pṛcchati bhadram ity achvaryuḥ pratyāha tan ma iti yajamānaḥ
7.18.22	rakṣohaṇo valagahanaḥ prokṣāmi vaiṣṇavān iti
7.19.1	yavamatībhir adbhir uparavāṃs triḥ prokṣati
7.19.2	rakṣohaṇo valagahano 'vanayāmi vaiṣṇavān iti yavamatīr apo 'vanayati
7.19.3	yavo 'sīti yavaṃ prāsyati
7.19.4	rakṣohaṇo valagahano 'vastṛṇāmi vaiṣṇavān iti prācā barhiṣāvastṛṇāti
7.19.5	rakṣohaṇo valagahano 'bhijuhomi vaiṣṇavān iti hiraṇyam antardhāya sruveṇābhijuhoti
7.19.6	rakṣohaṇau valagahanau prokṣāmi vaiṣṇave ity adhiṣavaṇaphalake prokṣaty audumbare kārṣmaryamaye pālāśe vā taṣṭe pradhimukhe saṃhite purastāt samāpikarte paścād dvyaṅgulena tryaṅgulena caturaṅgulena vā paścād asaṃhite saṃtṛṇṇe asaṃtṛṇṇe vā
7.19.7	rakṣohaṇau valagahanāv upadadhāmi vaiṣṇavī ity adhiṣavaṇaphalakābhyām uparavān apidadhāti dvau dakṣiṇena dvāv uttareṇa
7.19.8	rakṣohaṇu valagahanau paryūhāmi vaiṣṇavī ity auparaveṇa purīṣeṇa paryūhati
7.19.9	rakṣohaṇau valagahanau paristṛṇāmi vaiṣṇavī iti darbhaiḥ paristṛṇāti
7.19.10	rakṣohaṇau valagahanau vaiṣṇavī ity abhimantrayate
7.19.11	rakṣohat tvā valagahat prokṣāmi vaiṣṇavam ity adhiṣavaṇacarma prokṣati
7.19.12	lohitam ānaḍuham upariṣṭāllomāsecanavad yathābhiṣavāyopāptaṃ bhavati
7.19.13	rakṣohat tvā valagahat stṛṇāmi vaiṣṇavam ity adhiṣavaṇaphalakayor āstṛṇāti
7.19.14	tasmiṃś caturo grāvṇaḥ saṃsādayaty ūrdhvasānūn āhananaprakārān uparaṃ prathiṣṭhaṃ madhye pañcamam
7.19.15	bṛhann asīty ekaikam
7.19.16	rakṣoghno vo valagaghnaḥ prokṣāmi vaiṣṇavān ity upare grāvṇaḥ saṃmukhān kṛtvā prokṣati
7.19.17	auparavasya purīṣasyāgreṇopastambhanaṃ caturaśraṃ kharaṃ karoti yāvantam āptaṃ pātrebhyo manyate
7.20.1	uttarata āgnīdhrīyaṃ minoti madhye veder ardham antarvedy ardhaṃ bahirvedi prācīnavaṃśaṃ vimitaṃ viminvanti dakṣiṇataupacāram
7.20.2	agreṇāparaṃ vedyantaṃ triṣu prakrameṣv aparimite vodīcīnavaṃśaṃ sado dakṣiṇataḥ pratikṛṣṭataraṃ yāvad ṛtvigbhyo dhiṣṇiyebhyaḥ prasarpakebhyaś cāptaṃ manyate
7.20.3	dakṣiṇena pṛṣṭhyāṃ prakrame madhye sadasa audumbaryavaṭaḥ
7.20.4	abhrer ādānaṃ parilekhanaṃ ca yūpe vyākhyātam
7.20.5	dive tveti parastād arvācīṃ prokṣati
7.20.6	apām avanayanaṃ yavaprāsanaṃ barhiṣāvastaraṇaṃ ca yūpe vyākhyātam
7.20.7	ucchrayasva vanaspate sajūr devena barhiṣeti prācīnakarṇām udgātrā sahocchrayaty ud divaṃ stabhāneti vā
7.20.8	dyutānas tvā māruto minotv ity avaṭe 'vadadhāti
7.20.9	paryūhaṇaṃ paridṛṃhaṇaṃ pariṣecanaṃ ca yūpe vyākhyātam
7.20.10	tasyāḥ karṇe viśākhe vā hiraṇyaṃ nidhāya ghṛtena dyāvāpṛthivī āpṛṇethāṃ svāheti sruveṇābhijuhoti
7.20.11	āmūlād anvavasrāvayati
7.20.12	yajamānamātrīsaṃmitā varṣiṣṭhāḥ sthūṇā minuto yathāsuṣṭhu
7.20.13	paryantyā nābhidaghnā audumbarīm abhyagrā minoti
7.20.14	nīcaiḥ sado vṛṣṭikāmasya minuyād uccair avṛṣṭikāmasya viparītam eke samāmananti
7.20.15	nava cchadīṃṣy upakl̥ptāni bhavanti
7.20.16	udīco vaṃśān ādhāya prāco vaṃśān ādadhāti
7.20.17	aindram asīti trīṇi madhyamāni chadīṃṣy udañci nidadhāti
7.20.18	indrasya sado 'sīti trīṇi dakṣiṇāni viśvajanasya chāyeti trīṇy uttarāṇi
7.20.19	dakṣiṇāny uttarāṇi karoty audumbarīm abhisaṃmukhāni
7.20.20	navachadi tejaskāmasya minuyād iti brāhmaṇavyākhyātāni kāmyāni chadīṃṣi teṣāṃ yāthākāmī
7.20.21	aindram asīndrāya tveti saṃmitam abhimṛśataḥ
7.20.22	prāgvaṃśasya sadohavirdhānayoś ca
7.21.1	samānaṃ sāṃkāśinam
7.21.2	nāsaṃsthite some 'dhvaryuḥ pūrveṇa dvāreṇa havirdhāne praviśyāpareṇa niṣkrāmed yadi niṣkrāmed idaṃ viṣṇur vicakrama iti japet
7.21.3	nāpareṇa sadaḥ praviśya pūrveṇa niṣkrāmed yadi niṣkrāmed uttiṣṭhann ojasā saheti japet
7.21.4	atroparavakarmaike samāmananti
7.21.5	cātvālāt purīṣam āhṛtya dhiṣṇiyān nivapati caturaśrān parimaṇḍalān vā
7.21.6	vibhūr asīty āgnīdhrīyam āgnīdhrāgāre yathottareṇāntarvedi saṃcaro bhavati
7.21.7	antaḥsadasam itarān
7.21.8	vahnir asīty apareṇa sadobilaṃ pṛṣṭhyāyāṃ prakrame hotrīyam
7.21.9	śvātro 'sīti dakṣiṇena hotrīyaṃ maitrāvaruṇasya
7.21.10	uttareṇa hotrīyam udagāyatān itarān
7.21.11	tutho 'sīti brāhmaṇācchaṃsina uśig asīti potur andhārir asīti neṣṭur avasyur asīty acchāvākasya pratikṛṣṭataram
7.21.12	śundhyūr asīti mārjālīyaṃ bahiḥsadasaṃ dakṣiṇārdhe vedeḥ samam āgnīdhrīyeṇa yathā dakṣiṇenāntarvedi saṃcaro bhavati
7.21.13	raudram anīkaṃ sarvatrānuṣajati
7.21.14	atra vedistaraṇam eke samāmananti
7.21.15	uttaravediṃ kharam uparavān dhiṣṇiyāṃś ca na stṛṇāti
7.22.1	agnīṣomīyasya paśos tantraṃ prakramayati
7.22.2	tasya nirūḍhapaśubandhena kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
7.22.3	ṣaḍḍhotā paśviṣṭiś cāṅgabhūte na vidyete
7.22.4	agnīn anvādhāyātithyāparidhīn idhma upasaṃnahyati
7.22.5	agnīn paristīrya pāṇī prakṣālyolaparājīṃ stīrtvā yathārthaṃ pāśukāni pātrāṇi prayunakti
7.22.6	yat prāg ājyagrahaṇāt tat kṛtvā pratihṛtya gārhapatye pāśukāny ājyāni gṛhṇāti
7.22.7	evā vandasvety upasthe brahmā rājānaṃ kurute
7.22.8	ādadate grāvṇo vāyavyāni droṇakalaśaṃ camasān ātithyābarhir idhmam ājyāny agnīṣomīyaṃ cānunayanti
7.22.9	ut patnīm ānayanty anv anāṃsi pravartayanti
7.22.10	praitu brahmaṇas patnīti neṣṭā patnīm udānayati
7.22.11	athāham anukāminīty ānīyamānā japati
7.22.12	suprajasas tvā vayam ity apareṇa śālāmukhīyam upaviśya dārśapaurṇamāsikān mantrāñ japati
7.22.13	śālāmukhīyaṃ gārhapatyakarmabhyo 'nvavasyanti tasmin gārhapatyakarmāṇi kriyante
7.22.14	sam apivratān hvayadhvam iti saṃpreṣyati
7.22.15	taṃ hvayante yajamānasyāmātyān
7.22.16	adhvaryuṃ yajamāno 'nvārabhate yajamānaṃ patnī patnīṃ yajamānasyāmātyāḥ
7.22.17	tān ahatena vāsasā pracchādya pracaraṇyāṃ caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā pracchādanārthasya vāsaso daśāyāṃ hiraṇyaṃ baddhvājye 'vadhāya srugdaṇḍe vāsaso 'ntam upaniyamya śālāmukhīye vaisarjanau juhoti tvaṃ soma tanūkṛdbhya iti pūrvām āhutiṃ juhoti juṣāṇo aptur ājyasya vetu svāheti dvitīyām
7.22.18	śeṣam ājyasya karoti
7.22.19	śālāmukhīye 'gnipraṇayanāny ādīpayati sikatāś copayamanīr upakalpayata udyacchatīdhmam upayacchaty upayamanīr upayate dhāryamāṇe
7.23.1	agnīṣomābhyāṃ praṇīyamānābhyām anubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati praṇīyamānābhyām anubrūhīti vā
7.23.2	trir anūktāyām ayaṃ no agnir ity agniprathamāḥ somaprathamā vā prāñco gacchanti
7.23.3	yathārtham anunayanti
7.23.4	anugacchanty amātyāḥ
7.23.5	anunayanty agnīṣomīyam
7.23.6	āgnīdhrīya etam agniṃ pratiṣṭhāpyāgne nayeti nayavatyarcāgnīdhre juhoti
7.23.7	śeṣam ājyasya karoti
7.23.8	nidadhati grāvṇo vāyavyāni droṇakalaśaṃ camasāṃś ca
7.23.9	atiharantītarāṇi
7.23.10	uttareṇāgnīdhrīyaṃ dhiṣṇiyaṃ parītyoru viṣṇo vikramasvety auttaravedike juhoti
7.23.11	yathetam amātyāḥ pratigacchanti
7.23.12	somo jigāti gātuvid iti saumyarcāpareṇa dvāreṇa havirdhāne brahmā rājānaṃ prapādayati
7.23.13	pūrveṇa gataśriyaḥ
7.23.14	urv antarikṣam anvemīti pūrveṇādhvaryuḥ praviśyādityāḥ sado 'sīti dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasya nīḍe kṛṣṇājinaṃ prācīnagrīvam uttaralomāstṛṇāti
7.23.15	prattaṃ rājānam adityāḥ sada āsīdeti tasminn āsādayati
7.23.16	prokṣaṇīr abhimantrya brahmāṇam āmantryedhmaṃ vediṃ ca prokṣya prokṣaṇyavaśeṣaṃ ninīya pavitre apisṛjyāpareṇottaravediṃ mantreṇa barhiḥ stṛṇāti yathā darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ
7.23.17	sanneṣv ājyeṣu yūpasaṃmānena pratipadyate
7.23.18	agnīṣomīyaṃ paśum upākaroti
7.24.1	sa vyākhyātarūpaḥ
7.24.2	pravaraṃ pravṛtyāśrāvam ṛtupraiṣādibhiḥ saumikān ṛtvijo vṛṇīte
7.24.3	indraṃ hotrāt sajūr diva ā pṛthivyā iti hotāram
7.24.4	apisṛjya tṛṇam asphya uttarān vṛṇīte
7.24.5	agnim āgnīdhrād ity āgnīdhram
7.24.6	aśvinādhvaryū ādhvaryavād ity ātmānaṃ pratiprasthātāraṃ ca
7.24.7	mitrāvaruṇau praśāstārau praśāstrād iti maitrāvaruṇam
7.24.8	indro brahmā brāhmaṇād iti brāhmaṇācchaṃsinaṃ
7.24.9	marutaḥ potrād iti potāraṃ
7.24.10	grāvo neṣṭrād iti neṣṭāram
7.24.11	agnir devīnāṃ viśāṃ puraetāyaṃ sunvan yajamāno manuṣyāṇāṃ tayor asthūri gārhapatyaṃ dīdāya gacchataṃ himā vā yu rādhāṃsīt saṃpṛñcānāv asaṃpṛñcānau tanva iti yajamānam
7.24.12	juṣṭo vāco bhūyāsam ity etābhyāṃ pravṛtaḥpravṛto juhoty anantaraṃ pravarāt
7.24.13	hutvādhvaryur uttarān vṛṇīte
7.24.14	savanīya eke pravarān āmananti
7.24.15	hutāyāṃ vapāyāṃ subrahmaṇya subrahmaṇyām āhvayeti saṃpreṣyati pitāputrīyā subrahmaṇyā bhavati
7.24.16	aparāhṇe vasatīvarīr gṛhṇāti vahantīnām
7.24.17	nāntamā vahantīr atīyāt
7.24.18	saṃdhāv ātapasya cchāyāyāḥ
7.24.19	kūlasya vṛkṣasya svayaṃ vā chāyāṃ kṛtvā
7.24.20	haviṣmatīr imā āpa iti pratīpaṃ tiṣṭhan kumbhaṃ kumbhīṃ vābhipūrayati
7.24.21	yady agṛhītāḥ sūryo 'bhinimroced yo brāhmaṇo bahuyājī tasya gṛhāt kumbhyānāṃ gṛhṇīyāt
7.24.22	yadi taṃ na vindeyur agniṃ hiraṇyaṃ cādāya pareyād yatrāpaḥ syus taj jyotir upariṣṭād dhārayan hiraṇyam antardhāya vare datte gṛhṇāti
7.24.23	agner vo 'pannagṛhasya sadasi sādayāmīty apareṇa śālāmukhīyam upasādayati
7.24.24	astamite saṃvādaprabhṛtinā paśutantreṇa pratipadyate
7.24.25	tasya dakṣiṇena havirdhānam uttareṇa vā samavattaṃ pariharati
7.24.26	na yajamāno bhakṣān bhakṣayati bhakṣaṇam eke samānanti
7.24.27	patnīsaṃyājāntaḥ
7.25.1	agnīṣomīyaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
7.25.2	niśāyāṃ vasatīvarīḥ pariharati sarvato na purastāt
7.25.3	utkrāmatety uktvāntarvedi yajamānaḥ patnī ca bhavataḥ
7.25.4	nādīkṣitam abhi pariharati
7.25.5	ādāya kumbhaṃ savye 'ṃse 'tyādhāyāpareṇa prājahitam atikramya dakṣiṇayā dvāropanirhṛtya dakṣiṇaṃ vedyantam anu parihṛtyendrāgniyor bhāgadheyīḥ stheti dakṣiṇasyām uttaravediśroṇyāṃ sādayati
7.25.6	ādāya kumbhaṃ dakṣiṇe 'ṃse 'tyādhāya yathetaṃ pratyetyottarapūrvayā dvāropanirhṛtyottaraṃ vedyantam anu parihṛtya mitrāvaruṇayor bhāgadheyīḥ sthety uttarasyām uttaravediśroṇyāṃ sādayati
7.25.7	ādāya kumbhaṃ savye 'ṃse 'tyādhāya tīrthena prapādya viśveṣāṃ vedānāṃ bhāgadheyīḥ sthety āgnīdhre sādayati
7.25.8	atra vasanti
7.25.9	subrahmaṇya subrahmaṇyām āhvayeti saṃpreṣyati pitāputrīyā subrahmaṇyā bhavati
7.25.10	yā yajamānasya vratadhuktām āśire duhrata yā patnyās tāṃ dadhigrahāya yā gharmadhuktāṃ dadhigharmāya taptam anātaṅkyaṃ payo maitrāvaruṇāya śṛtātaṅkyaṃ dadhy ādityagrahāya kurutād iti saṃpreṣyati
7.25.11	āgnīdhra ṛtvijo 'laṃkṛtā vasanti
7.25.12	prāgvaṃśe patnīṃ jāgarayanti
7.25.13	havirdhāne yajamāno rājānaṃ gopāyati gopāyati
8.1.1	mahārātre budhyante
8.1.2	tathā karmāṇy upakramante yathā purā vācaḥ pravaditoḥ prātaranuvāko bhavati
8.1.3	prajāpatir manasāndho 'ccheta iti trayastriṃśataṃ yajñatanūr āgnīdhre juhoti
8.1.4	pūrvāṃpūrvām anudrutyottarayottarayaikayā nu prathamayā
8.1.5	yajñārtiṃ prati juhotīty ekeṣām
8.1.6	savanīyasya paśos tantraṃ prakramayati
8.1.7	tasya nirūḍhapaśubandhena kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
8.1.8	na barhir vidyate prastaram evāharati barhiṣaḥ kalpena
8.1.9	pātrasaṃsādanakāle pracaraṇīṃ prathamāṃ srucaṃ prayunakti
8.1.10	ājyagrahaṇakāle pracaraṇyāṃ caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvottarāsu gṛhṇāti
8.1.11	prokṣaṇīr abhimantrya brahmāṇam āmantryedhmaṃ vediṃ prastaraṃ ca prokṣya prokṣaṇyavaśeṣaṃ ninīya pavitre apisṛjya prastaraṃ sādayitvā srucaḥ sādayati
8.1.12	ayaṃ no agnir varivaḥ kṛṇotv ity āgnīdhram abhimṛśati
8.1.13	idaṃ viṣṇur vicakrama iti havirdhāne
8.1.14	agna āyūṃṣi pavasa iti srucaḥ
8.1.15	ā vāyo bhūṣeti vāyavyāni
8.1.16	uttiṣṭhann ojasā saheti sadaḥ
8.1.17	khare pātrāṇi prayunakti
8.1.18	agnir devatā gāyatrī chanda ity etair yathārūpaṃ kas tvā yunakti sa tvā yunaktv ity avaśiṣṭāni
8.1.19	dakṣiṇe 'ṃsa upāṃśvantaryāmayoḥ pātre dakṣiṇam upāṃśor uttaram antaryāmasya
8.1.20	api vā pūrvam upāṃśor aparam antaryāmasya
8.1.21	te antareṇa vyānāya tvety upāṃśusavanaṃ grāvāṇaṃ saṃsṛṣṭam upāṃśupātreṇa prayunakti
8.1.22	pratyañci dvidevatyapātrāṇi parisrag aindravāyavasyājagāvan maitrāvaruṇasya dvisrakty āśvinasya
8.1.23	apare śukrāmanthinoḥ pātre dakṣiṇaṃ bailvaṃ śukrasyottaraṃ vaikaṅkataṃ manthinaḥ
8.1.24	apare āśvatthe aśvaśaphabudhne ubhayatomukhe ṛtupātre dakṣiṇam adhvaryor uttaraṃ pratiprasthātuḥ
8.1.25	dakṣiṇasyāṃ śroṇyām āgrayaṇasthālīm
8.1.26	uttarasyām ukthyasthālīm ukthyapātraṃ cāśvaśaphabudhnam
8.1.27	te antareṇodañci trīṇy atigrāhyapātrāṇi
8.1.28	dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasyāgreṇopastambhanam ādityasthālīm ādityapātraṃ cāśvaśaphabudhnam
8.1.29	uttarasya havirdhānasyāgreṇopastambhanam anupopte dhruvasthālīm
8.1.30	uttare 'ṃsa audumbaraṃ catuḥsrakti dadhigrahapātram
8.1.31	madhye pariplavām
8.1.32	yathāvakāśam ekādaśa camasān naiyagrodhān rauhitakān vā
8.2.1	tsarumato 'tsarukān vā
8.2.2	prādeśamātrāṇy ūrdhvasānūni madhye saṃnatāni vāyavyāni
8.2.3	yathā srug adaṇḍaivaṃ pariplavā
8.2.4	teṣāṃ yāny anādiṣṭavṛkṣāṇi vikaṅkatasya tāny ahomārthāni tu vāraṇasya
8.2.5	yunajmi te pṛthivīṃ jyotiṣā saheti dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasya paścādakṣaṃ droṇakalaśaṃ sadaśāpavitraṃ prayunakti
8.2.6	yunajmi vāyum antarikṣeṇa te sahety uttarasya nīḍa ādhavanīyam
8.2.7	yunajmi vācaṃ saha sūryeṇa ta iti tasyaiva pradhure pūtabhṛtam
8.2.8	paścādakṣaṃ tisra ekadhanā sthālī yunajmi tisro vipṛcaḥ sūryasya ta iti sruco 'bhimṛśati
8.2.9	atrādhiṣavaṇacarmaṇo grāvṇām iti prayojanam eke samāmananti
8.2.10	apāṃ kṣayā ṛtasya garbhā bhuvanasya gopāḥ śyenā atithayaḥ parvatānāṃ kakubhaḥ prayuto na pātāro vagnunendraṃ hvayata ghoṣeṇāmīvāṃś cātayata yuktāḥ stha vahata svargaṃ lokam abhivahata yajamānam ity upare grāvṇaḥ saṃmukhān kṛtvābhimantrayate
8.2.11	āsanyān mā mantrāt pāhīty āgnīdhre juhoti
8.2.12	hṛde tvā manase tveti dvābhyām antareṣāṃ rājānaṃ grāvasūpāvaharati
8.2.13	āgnīdhre pañcahotāraṃ juhuyāt svargakāmasyety ekeṣām
8.2.14	purā vācaḥ pravaditoḥ prātaranuvākam upākaroti
8.2.15	dveṣyasya proṣitāyām
8.2.16	devebhyaḥ prātaryāvabhyo 'nubrūhi brahman vācaṃ yaccha subrahmaṇya subrahmaṇyām āhvaya pratiprasthātaḥ savanīyān nirvapeti saṃpreṣyati
8.2.17	pratiprasthātā savanīyānāṃ pātrasaṃsādanaprabhṛtīni karmāṇi pratipadyate yathārtham oṣadhipātrāṇi prayunakti
8.2.18	dve bharjanārthe kapāle aṣṭau puroḍāśārthāny āmikṣārthāṃ sthālīm
8.2.19	nirvapaṇakāla indrāya harivate dhānā nirvapatīndrāya pūṣaṇvate karambhaṃ sarasvatyai bhāratyai parivāpalājān indrāya puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālam
8.2.20	prokṣiteṣu vibhāgamantreṇa vrīhīn vibhajyārdhān avahanty ardhāṃl lājārthān nidadhāti
8.2.21	prathamena kapālamantreṇa dhānārthaṃ lājārthaṃ ca kapāle upadadhāti
8.2.22	aṣṭau puroḍāśasyopadhāyāmikṣāyāḥ kalpena maitrāvaruṇīm āmikṣāṃ karoti
8.2.23	adhiśrayaṇamantreṇa dhānā lājāṃś ca bharjayati
8.2.24	anupadahyamānāḥ pariśerate
8.2.25	yat prāg alaṃkaraṇāt tat kṛtvā vibhāgamantreṇa dhānā vibhajya piṣṭānām āvṛtārdhāḥ saktūn kṛtvā saṃyavanamantreṇa saṃyauti sa karambho bhavati
8.2.26	analaṃkṛteṣv abhūd uṣā ruśatpaśur āgnir adhāyy ṛtviya ity etasyāṃ śasyamānāyāṃ śṛṇotv agniḥ samidhā havaṃ ma ity etac caturgṛhītaṃ juhoti
8.2.27	aparaṃ caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā
8.3.1	darbhamuṣṭiṃ dhārayamāṇo 'pa iṣya hotar maitrāvaruṇasya camasādhvaryav ādravaikadhanina ādravata neṣṭaḥ patnīm udānayonnetar hotṛcamasena vasatīvarībhiś ca cātvālaṃ pratyupāssveti saṃpreṣyati
8.3.2	maitrāvaruṇacamasādhvaryuś camasam ādāyādravati
8.3.3	trayavarārdhā ayuja ekadhanāsthālīr ādāyādravanti
8.3.4	prehy udehīti neṣṭā patnīm udānayati
8.3.5	yatra hotuḥ prātaranuvākam anubruvata upaśaṇuyāt tad apo 'dhvaryur gṛhṇīyāt
8.3.6	yadi dūre syur udūhya gṛhṇīyād yatra hotuḥ śṛṇoti
8.3.7	apsu tṛṇaṃ prāsya devīr āpa ity etac caturgṛhītaṃ juhoti
8.3.8	śeṣaṃ vā karoti
8.3.9	yadi vā purā tṛṇaṃ bhavati tasminn eva juhoti
8.3.10	kārṣir asīti darbhair āhutim apaplāvayati
8.3.11	samudrasya vo 'kṣityā unnaya ity aghṛtaliptānāṃ maitrāvaruṇacamasenonnayati
8.3.12	etenaiva mantreṇaikadhanāsu
8.3.13	vasubhyo rudrebhya ādityebhya iti patnī pannejanīr gṛhṇāti
8.3.14	ye sthālīr āharanti ta ānayanti
8.3.15	tenaiva mantreṇa neṣṭā patnīm udānayati
8.3.16	pūrveṇa dvāreṇa sadaḥ praviśyāgreṇa praśāstrīyaṃ dhiṣṇiyaṃ parītyāpareṇa neṣṭur dhiṣṇiyaṃ vasubhyo rudrebhya ādityebhya iti patnī pannejanīḥ sādayati
8.3.17	vasavo rudā ādityā etā vaḥ pannejanīs tā rakṣadhvam iti vā
8.3.18	cātvālam itare yanti
8.4.1	saṃ vo dadhātu varuṇaḥ sam indraḥ saṃ dhātā saṃ bṛhaspatiḥ / tvaṣṭā viṣṇuḥ prajayā saṃrarāṇo yajamānāya draviṇaṃ dadhātu yathādhuraṃ dhuro dhūrbhiḥ kalpantām ity upari cātvāle hotṛcamasaṃ maitrāvaruṇacamasaṃ ca saṃsparśya vasatīvarīr vyānayati
8.4.2	hotṛcamase vasatīvarīṇāṃ niṣicya maitrāvaruṇacamasa ānayati maitrāvaruṇacamasāddhotṛcamase
8.4.3	hotṛcamasaṃ maitrāvaruṇacamasaṃ ca pracaraṇyā samanakti saṃ vo 'naktu varuṇa iti mantrādiṃ saṃnamati
8.4.4	hotur antikam āyanati
8.4.5	adhvaryo 'ver apā3 iti hotādhvaryuṃ triḥ pṛcchati
8.4.6	utem anannamur uteti triḥ pratyāha
8.4.7	yam agne pṛtsu martyam iti pracaraṇyā kratukaraṇaṃ juhoti yadi śeṣo bhavati
8.4.8	avidyamāne 'nyac caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā tat sarvaṃ juhoti
8.4.9	dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasya pradhure pracaraṇīṃ sādayati
8.4.10	yaṃ kāmayeta klībaḥ syād ity adhastāt tasya
8.4.11	pūrveṇa dvāreṇa havirdhānam apaḥ prapādayati
8.4.12	tāsu dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasyottarasyāṃ vartanyāṃ purokṣaṃ hotṛcamasam āspṛṣṭaṃ sādayati
8.4.13	uttarasmin havirdhāne yathāvakalśam itarāḥ
8.4.14	nigrābhyāḥ stha devaśrutaḥ śukrāḥ śukrabhṛtaḥ pūtāḥ pūtabhṛta āyurme tarpayateti hotṛcamase yajamānaṃ vācayati tā nigrābhyā bhavanti
8.5.1	dadhigraheṇa pracarati
8.5.2	upayāmagṛhīto 'si prajāpataye tvā jyotiṣmate jyotiṣmantaṃ gṛhṇāmīti dadhigrahapātre dadhigrahaṃ gṛhṇāty apendra dviṣato mana iti harati prāṇāya tvāpānāya tveti juhoti
8.5.3	ājyagrahaṃ gṛhṇīyāt tejaskāmasya somagrahaṃ gṛhṇīyād brahmavarcasakāmasyeti
8.5.4	tayor dadhigraheṇa kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
8.5.5	dadhigrahaṃ gṛhṇīyātpaśukāmasyeti nitye kāmye
8.5.6	somagrahaṃ grahīṣyan rājānam apādatte yāvantam ekagrahāyāptaṃ manyate
8.5.7	pratyupanahyetaraṃ nidadhāti
8.5.8	tam upare nupya vasatīvarībhir upasṛjyāvīvṛdhaṃ va ity abhimantrya
8.5.9	tisro yahvasya samidhaḥ parijman devā akṛṇvann uśijo amartyave / tāsām ekām adadhur martye bhujaṃ lokam u dve upa jāmīnaṃ īyatur iti grāvṇā yathārtham abhiṣuṇoti
8.5.10	ā māskān iti yo 'bhiṣūyamāṇasya prathamo 'ṃśuḥ skandati tam abhimantrayate pratyāharati vā
8.5.11	drapsaś caskandeti vipruṣo 'numantrayate
8.5.12	sarvābhiṣavāṇām eṣa kalpaḥ
8.5.13	etasminn evaiṣo 'bhiṣavamantraḥ
8.5.14	taṃ sahiraṇyena pāṇinā gṛhītvā sahiraṇyena prāṅmukhas tiṣṭhan dakṣiṇārdhapūrvārdhe juhoty uttarārdhapūrvārdhe vā
8.5.15	yatraivaṃ tatra sarvasomāhutīḥ
8.5.16	hutvā śeṣaṃ vā karoti
8.5.17	pūrveṇa dvāreṇa sadaḥ praviśyāgreṇa hotāraṃ purastātpratyaṅṅ āsīno nṛcakṣasaṃ tvety avekṣya mandrābhibhūtir iti bhakṣayati
8.5.18	svayam āharan bhakṣam avekṣaṇaprabhṛtinā bhakṣamantreṇa pratipadyate
8.5.19	bhakṣehīty anyenāhriyamāṇaṃ pratīkṣate 'śvinos tvā bāhubhyāṃ saghyāsam iti pratigṛhya nṛcakṣasaṃ tvety avekṣya mandrābhibhūtir ity anudrutya vasumadgaṇasya soma deva ta iti
8.6.1	prātaḥsavane sarvasomān bhakṣayanti narāśaṃsapītasyeti nārāśaṃsān
8.6.2	rudravadgaṇasya soma deva ta iti mādhyaṃdine savane sarvasomān bhakṣayanti narāśaṃsapītasyeti nārāśaṃsān ādityavadgaṇasya soma deva ta iti tṛtīyasavane sarvasomān bhakṣayanti narāśaṃsapītasyeti nārāśaṃsān
8.6.3	yat prāg vasumadgaṇāt tat sarvatrānuṣajati
8.6.4	vāg devī somasya pibatv iti sārvatrikam eke samāmananti
8.6.5	hinva me gātrā hariva iti somaṃ bhakṣayitvātmānaṃ pratyabhimṛśante
8.6.6	mārjālīye pātraṃ prakṣālyāyatane sādayati
8.6.7	sarvasomānām eṣa kalpaḥ
8.6.8	graheṣu tu sahiraṇyatā
8.6.9	homābhiṣavābhyāṃ ca bhakṣo nānyatareṇa karmaṇā
8.6.10	dadhigrahasyāṃśor adābhyasya ca samānaṃ pātram
8.6.11	aṃśunā pracarati
8.6.12	rājānam apādatte yāvantam ekagrahāyāptaṃ manyate pratyupanahyetaraṃ nidadhāti tam upare nyupya vasatīvarībhir upasṛjya sakṛdabhiṣutasya prāṇyāpānya prāṇān vāmadevyaṃ manasā gāyamāno gṛhṇāti
8.6.13	kayā naś citra ābhuvad iti vā vāmadevyasyarcā
8.6.14	yady anavānaṃ na śaknuyād gṛhītum ā naḥ prāṇa etu parāvata iti hiraṇyaṃ śatamānam abhivyanya vare datte gṛhṇāti
8.6.15	taṃ sahiraṇyena śatamānena saṃsparśya hiraṇyenāpidadhāti
8.6.16	indrāgnī me varcaḥ kṛṇutām iti harati
8.6.17	dadhanve vā yad īm anv ity anavānaṃ juhoti
8.6.18	adbhiḥ pratiprasthātādhvaryuṃ pratyukṣati
8.6.19	adābhyena pracarati
8.6.20	vasavas tvā prabṛhantv ity etair upanaddhasya rājñas trīn aṃśūn asaṃspṛṣṭān pravṛhyānyasmin pātre dadhno nigrābhyāṇāṃ vā niḥṣicya māndāsu te śukra śukram ādhūnomīti tasminn etair etān aṃśūṃs triḥ pradakṣiṇam anupariplāvayati
8.6.21	catuḥ pañcakṛtvaḥ saptakṛtvo vāvaśiṣṭā vikalpārthāḥ
8.6.22	śukraṃ te śukreṇa gṛhṇāmy agniḥ prātaḥsavane viśve devā idaṃ tṛtīyaṃ savanaṃ kavīnām ity enābhirgṛhṇāti sarvāsāmantata upayāmā bhavanti
8.6.23	āsminn ugrā acucyavur iti harati
8.6.24	kakuhaṃ rūpaṃ vṛṣabhasya rocate bṛhad ity abhimantrayate
8.6.25	somaḥ somasya purogā iti juhoti prajñātān aṃśūn nidadhāti
8.7.1	devasya tvety upāṃśusavanaṃ grāvāṇam ādāya vācaṃ yacchaty āgrayaṇasya grahaṇāt
8.7.2	grāvāsīty abhimantrayate
8.7.3	tam adhiṣavaṇa ūrdhvasānuṃ nidhāyendrāya tvā vṛtraghna ity etair mantrai rājānam abhimimīte yathā kraye 'nyad upasamūhanāt
8.7.4	adhiṣavaṇasyaikadeśe rājānam apodūhyādatte yāvantam ekagrahāyāptaṃ manyate pratyupanahyetaraṃ nidadhāti tam upare nyupya vasatīvarībhir upasṛjya śvātrāḥ stha vṛtratura iti nigrābhyābhir upasṛjati
8.7.5	yat te soma divi jyotir ity abhimantrayate
8.7.6	abhimantraṇam eke pūrvaṃ samāmananti
8.7.7	upasṛṣṭasya rājñaḥ ṣaḍ aṃśūn asaṃspṛṣṭān prabṛhya prajñātān nidhāyetarān ādāyopariṣṭād grāvāṇaṃ dhārayann adhastād aṃśūn prāg apāg udag adharāg iti hotṛcamase triḥ pradakṣiṇam anupariplāvayati sa nigrābho bhavati
8.7.8	tān upare nyupya vasatīvarībhir upasṛjya mā bher mā saṃvikthā iti grāvāṇam udyamya dhiṣaṇe vīḍū satī ity adhiṣavaṇaphalake abhimantrayate
8.7.9	anāgasas tvā vayam indreṇa preṣitā upa vāyuṣ ṭe astv aṃśabhūr mitras te astv aṃśabhūr varuṇas te astv aṃśabhūr ahataḥ somo rājeti yatra mūlaṃ tṛṇaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ vā paśyati tasmin deśe same praharati
8.7.10	tṛṇam antardhāyābhiṣuṇotīty ekeṣām
8.7.11	aṣṭaukṛtvo 'gre 'bhiṣutya nigrābham upaiti yathā purastāt
8.7.12	apāttānām aṃśūnāṃ dvābhyām upāśṃupātram apidhāyottarataḥ pratiprasthātopayacchati
8.7.13	vācaspataye pavasva vājinn iti tasminn añjalinādhvaryuḥ somam āsiñcati
8.7.14	evaṃ vihito dvitīyas tṛtīyaś cābhiṣavaḥ
8.7.15	api vaikādaśakṛtvo dvitīyam abhiṣuṇoti dvādaśakṛtvas tṛtīyam
8.7.16	apoddhṛtya pūrvāv aṃśū anyābhyāṃ dvitīye pātram apidhāyopayacchaty anyābhyāṃ tṛtīye devo devānām iti dvitīye somam āsiñcati madhumatīr na iṣas kṛdhīti tṛtīye
8.7.17	na sādayati
8.7.18	svāṃkṛto 'sīty uttiṣṭhati
8.7.19	urv antarikṣam iti gacchati
8.7.20	uttareṇa hotāram atikramya
8.8.1	manas tvāṣṭv ity uttaraṃ paridhisaṃdhim anvavatiṣṭhate
8.8.2	uttaraṃ paridhisaṃdhim anvavahṛtya svāhā tvā subhavaḥ sūryāyeti dakṣiṇāprāñcam ṛjuṃ dīrghaṃ saṃtataṃ juhoti
8.8.3	devebhyas tvā marīcipebhya iti madhyame paridhāv abhyantaraṃ lepaṃ nimārṣṭi
8.8.4	yadi kāmayeta varṣukaḥ parjanyaḥ syād iti brāhmaṇavyākhyātam
8.8.5	āgrayaṇasthālyāṃ saṃpātam avanayati
8.8.6	eṣa te yoniḥ prāṇāya tveti pātraṃ sādayati
8.8.7	tasminn aṃśum avadadhāti sa pariśeta ā tṛtīyasavanāt
8.8.8	abhicaratas tu grahaṃ gṛhītvā amuṣya tvā prāṇe sādayāmīti sādayet taṃ sāvitreṇādāyāmuṃ jahy atha tvā hoṣyāmīty abhimantrya praharṣiṇo madirasya made mṛṣāsāv astv iti juhoti
8.8.9	ā hotor aprāṇann āsīta
8.8.10	yadi dūre syād ā tamitos tiṣṭhet
8.8.11	dveṣyasya nāma gṛhṇāti
8.8.12	devāṃśo yasmai tveḍe tat satyam apariplutā bhaṅgyena hato 'sau phaḍ iti yo 'syāṃśur āśliṣṭa urasi vastre bāhau vā taṃ juhoti
8.8.13	mahābhiṣavāya paryupaviśante purastād adhvaryur dakṣiṇataḥ pratiprasthātā paścān neṣṭottarata unnetā
8.8.14	rājānam apādatte yāvantaṃ prātaḥsavanāyāptaṃ manyate pratyupanahyetaraṃ nidadhāti tam upare nyupyośik tvaṃ deva someti ye 'dābhyā aṃśavas teṣām ekaikam anusavanam apisṛjati yat te somādābhyaṃ nāma jāgṛvīti copāṃśupāvanānāṃ dvaudvau
8.8.15	tān upare nyupya vasatīvarībhir upasṛjya dakṣiṇaiḥ pāṇibhir grāvabhir yathārtham abhiṣutya nigrābham upayanti yathā purastāt
8.8.16	evaṃ vihito dvitīyas tṛtīyaś cābhiṣavaḥ
8.8.17	trirabhiṣutaṃ rājānam ādhavanīye saṃsiñcanti
8.8.18	evaṃ vihito dvitīyas tṛtīyaś ca paryāyaḥ
8.8.19	uttame 'bhiṣave susaṃbhṛtaṃ rājānaṃ kṛtvā pavitreṇa prapīḍyopare grāvṇaḥ saṃmukhān kṛtvā tebhya ṛjīṣaṃ vyapohati
8.8.20	ṛjīṣamukhān karoti
8.8.21	prāñcam udgātāro droṇakalaśaṃ grāvasv adhyūhanti
8.8.22	adhokṣam upakarṣanti
8.9.1	pavitraṃ te vitataṃ brahmaṇaspate prabhur gātrāṇi paryeṣi viśvataḥ / ataptatanūr na tad āmo aśnute śṛtāsa id vahantas tat samāśateti tasminn udīcīnadaśaṃ pavitram udgātāro vitatya dhārayanti
8.9.2	etayaivādhvaryur abhimantrayate
8.9.3	tasya yajamāno nābhiṃ karoti
8.9.4	hotṛcamasena cāsmin saṃtatāṃ dhārāṃ srāvayati
8.9.5	ādhavanīyād unnetodañcanena hotṛcamasa ānayati
8.9.6	sravatyā dhārāyā grahān gṛhṇāti
8.9.7	upayāmagṛhīto 'sy antar yacchety antaryāmam
8.9.8	tasyopāṃśunā kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
8.9.9	dakṣiṇena hotāram atikramya vāk tvāṣṭv iti dakṣiṇaṃ paridhisaṃdhim anvavatiṣṭhate dakṣiṇaṃ paridhisaṃdhim anvavahṛtya svāhā tvā subhavaḥ sūryāyeti prāñcam udañcam ṛjuṃ dīrthaṃ saṃtataṃ juhoti
8.9.10	na paridhau lepaṃ nimārṣṭi nāgrayaṇasthālyāṃ saṃpātam avanayati
8.9.11	eṣa te yonir apānāya tveti pātraṃ sādayati
8.9.12	nāṃśum avadadhāti
8.9.13	te antareṇa vyānāya tvety upāṃśusavanaṃ grāvāṇaṃ saṃspṛṣṭam upāṃśupātreṇa sādayati
8.9.14	yaṃ kāmayeta pramāyukaḥ syād ity asaṃspṛṣṭau tasya sādayed yaṃ kāmayeta sarvam āyur iyād iti saṃspṛṣṭau tasya sādayet
8.9.15	ubhāv udite juhoty atvaramāṇaḥ
8.9.16	tvaramāṇas tv anudita upāṃśum udite 'ntaryāmam
8.9.17	ubhāv anudita ity ekeṣām
8.10.1	rathaṃtarasāmny aindravāyavāgrān gṛhṇīyāt
8.10.2	bṛhatsāmni śukrāgrān
8.10.3	ubhayasāmni yāthākāmī
8.10.4	aindravāyavān gṛhṇīyād vaikārike pṛṣṭhasaṃyoge
8.10.5	aindravāyavāgrāñ jyeṣṭhabandhur gṛhṇīteti nitye kāmye
8.10.6	aindravāyavāgrān gṛhṇīyād āmayāvina iti brāhmaṇavyākhyātāni kāmyāni grahaṇāni teṣāṃ yāthākāmī
8.10.7	purastād aindravāyavād gṛhyante sanne sādyante
8.10.8	aindravāyavaṃ gṛhṇāti
8.10.9	ā vāyo bhūṣety anudrutya pātram upayacchaty upayāmagṛhīto 'si vāyave tveti tasmin gṛhṇāti
8.10.10	pātram apayamyendravāyū ity anudrutya punar evopayacchaty upayāmagṛhīto 'sīndravāyubhyāṃ tveti tasmin punar gṛhṇāti
8.10.11	yad avyāpṛtaṃ pavitraṃ tena parimṛjyaiṣa te yoniḥ sajoṣābhyāṃ tvety āyatane sādayati
8.10.12	purastādupayāmā yajuṣā gṛhyanta upariṣṭādupayāmā ṛcā
8.10.13	sarvagrahāṇāṃ parimārjanaṃ yathāyonisādanaṃ ca
8.10.14	ayaṃ vāṃ mitrāvaruṇeti maitrāvaruṇaṃ rāyā vayaṃ sasavāṃso madema havyena devā yavasena gāvaḥ / tāṃ dhenuṃ mitrāvaruṇā yuvaṃ no viśvāhā dhattam anapasphurantīm iti taṃ śṛtaśītena payasā śrītvā sādayati
8.10.15	ayaṃ vena iti śukraṃ hiraṇyena śrīṇāti
8.10.16	taṃ pratnatheti manthinam
8.10.17	mano na yeṣu havaneṣu juhvad vipaḥ śacyā vanutho dravantā / ā yaḥ śaryābhis tuvinṛmṇo asyāśrīṇītādiśaṃ gabhastāv iti saktubhir manthinaṃ śrīṇāty ātmānam anabhidhvaṃsayann itarāṃś ca grahān
8.10.18	ye devā divy ekādaśa stheti sthālyāgrayaṇam āgrayaṇo 'sīti vā purastādupayāmena yajuṣā
8.10.19	dvābhyāṃ dhārābhyāṃ gṛhṇāti
8.10.20	ya āgrayaṇasthālyāṃ somas tasyaikadeśam anyasmin pātre niṣicya dvitīyāṃ dhārāṃ karoti
8.10.21	vidad yatī saramā rugṇam adrer mahi pāthaḥ pūrvyaṃ sadhriyak kaḥ / agraṃ nayat supady akṣarāṇām acchā ravaṃ prathamā jānatī gād iti purorucam abhicarataḥ kuryāt
8.10.22	triṃśat trayaś ceti bhrātṛvyavataḥ
8.10.23	āgrayaṇaṃ gṛhītvā him iti trir hiṃkaroti śanair agre 'thoccair atha sūccaiḥ somaḥ pavata iti trir āha śanair agre 'thoccair atha sūccaiḥ
8.11.1	asmai brahmaṇe pavate 'smai kṣatrāya pavate 'smai sunvate yajamānāya pavata iṣa ūrje pavate 'dbhya oṣadhībhyaḥ pavate vanaspatibhyaḥ pavate dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ pavate subhūtāya pavate brahmavarcasāya pavate yajamānāya pavate mahyaṃ jyaiṣṭhyāya pavata iti somam abhimantrya vācaṃ visṛjate
8.11.2	atigrāhyān gṛhṇāti
8.11.3	agna āyūṃṣi pavasa ity āgneyam uttiṣṭhann ojasā sahety aindraṃ taraṇir viśvadarśata iti sauryam
8.11.4	ojas tad asya titviṣa ubhe yat samavartayat / indraś carmeva rodasī / adṛśram asya ketavo vi raśmayo janāṃ anu / bhrājanto agnayo yatheti vaitābhyām
8.11.5	upayāmagṛhīto 'sīndrāya tvā bṛhadvate vayasvata ukthyāyuva iti sthālyokthyam
8.11.6	mūrdhānaṃ divo aratiṃ pṛthivyā iti sthālyā dhruvam
8.11.7	dhruvo 'sīti vā purastādupayāmena yajuṣā
8.11.8	pūrṇam
8.11.9	dveṣyasyonam
8.11.10	hiraṇye sādayaty āyuṣkāmasya
8.11.11	taṃ dakṣiṇe havirdhāna āsīno rājaputro gopāyati
8.11.12	sarvān pūrṇān vṛṣṭikāmasya grahān gṛhṇīyāt
8.11.13	yadi kāmayeta yo grāme taṃ grāmān nirūhyeyaṃ yo bahir grāmāt taṃ grāme kuryām itīdam aham amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram amuṣyā viśa utkhidāmīti dhruvam utkhidyedam aham amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram amuṣyāṃ viśi sādayāmīti taṃ punaḥ sādayed ya eva grāme taṃ grāmān nirūhya yo bahir grāmāt taṃ grāme karoti
8.11.14	dhruvaṃ sādayitvā rājānam atipāvayati yāvantaṃ prātaḥsavanāyāptaṃ manyate
8.11.15	viramati dhārā prapīḍya pavitraṃ nidadhāti
8.11.16	maitrāvaruṇacamasīyāś caikadhanaikadeśāṃś cādhavanīye 'vanīya tiraḥpavitraṃ pūtabhṛty ekadeśam avanayati
8.11.17	ata ūrdhvaṃ pūtabhṛti tiraḥpavitram evāvanīyate
8.11.18	pavamānagrahān gṛhṇāti
8.11.19	upayāmagṛhīto 'si prajāpataye tveti droṇakalaśam abhimṛśed indrāya tvety ādhavanīyaṃ viśvebhyas tvā devebhya iti pūtabhṛtam
8.11.20	niḥsarpantaḥ samanvārabhante
8.12.1	adhvaryuṃ prastotānvārabhate prastotāraṃ pratihartā pratihartāram udgātodgātāraṃ brahmā brahmāṇaṃ yajamāno yajamānaṃ brahmety ekeṣām
8.12.2	niḥsṛpya yas te drapsaḥ skandatīti tisro yas te drapsaḥ skandati yas te aṃśuḥ svaḥ paraś ca yo divaḥ puraḥ / ayaṃ devo bṛhaspatiḥ saṃ tat siñcatu rādhaseti vaipruṣān saptahotāraṃ ca hutvodañcaḥ prahvā bahiṣpavamānāya sarpanti
8.12.3	gāyatraḥ panthā vasavo devatāvṛkeṇāparipareṇa pathā svasti vasūn aśīya / vāg agregā agra etv ṛjugā ity adhvaryuḥ pūrvo barhirmuṣṭim īṣad iva vidhūnvan sarpati
8.12.4	dakṣiṇena cātvālam upaviśyāntarvedi cātvālam avekṣamāṇā bahiṣpavamānena stuvate
8.12.5	vāyur hiṃkarteti prastotre barhirmuṣṭiṃ prayacchan stotram upākaroty asarjy asarji vāg asarjy aindraṃ saho 'sarjy upāvartadhvam abhisarpa yajamāneti
8.12.6	sarvān pavamānān evam
8.12.7	upāvartadhvam iti barhirbhyām itarāṇi stotrāṇi
8.12.8	stūyamānaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ brāhmaṇāḥ samabhisarpanti dveṣyaṃ paribādhante
8.13.1	agnīd agnīn vihara barhiḥ stṛṇāhi puroḍāśāṃ alaṃkuru pratiprasthātaḥ paśunehīti stuta uttiṣṭhan saṃpreṣyati
8.13.2	havirdhāne praviśya viṣṇo tvaṃ no antama iti grahān upatiṣṭhate pātrāṇi ca saṃmṛśati
8.13.3	āgnīdhrīyād āgnīdhro 'ṅgārān āhṛtya tair eva mantrair yathānyuptaṃ dhiṣṇiyān viharati
8.13.4	adhvaryuś catuś camase rājānaṃ gṛhītvā pañcagṛhītaṃ cājyaṃ purastāt pratyaṅṅ āsīnas tair eva mantrai yathānyuptaṃ dhiṣṇiyān vyāghārayati
8.13.5	somenāhavanīyam āgnīdhrīyaṃ hotrīyaṃ mārjālīyaṃ cājyenetarān
8.13.6	atihāya vaṣaṭkaroti
8.13.7	vyākhyātaḥ somasya bhakṣaḥ
8.13.8	saṃtatam anupṛṣṭhyaṃ barhiḥ stīrtvāgnīdhraḥ puroḍāśān alaṃkaroti
8.13.9	aiti paśunā
8.13.10	yā vāṃ kaśā madhumatīty āśvinaṃ graham adhvaryur gṛhṇāti
8.13.11	pariplavayā droṇakalaśād upastīrya pūtabhṛta unnīya droṇakalaśād abhighārayati
8.13.12	sarvagrahāṇām eṣa kalpaḥ
8.13.13	taṃ sādayitvā trivṛtā yūpaṃ parivīyāgneyaṃ paśuṃ savanīyam upākaroti
8.13.14	tasya rūpaniyamo na vidyate
8.13.15	hutāyāṃ vapāyāṃ prasṛpsyanto grahāvakalaśair upasthāya saṃprasarpanti
8.13.16	dvau samudrāv iti droṇakalaśādhavanīyau
8.13.17	dve dradhasī iti pūtabhṛtam
8.13.18	paribhūr agnim iti sarvasomam
8.13.19	prāṇāya ma ity upāṃśupātram apānāya ma ity antaryāmaṃ vyānāya ma ity upāṃśusavanaṃ grāvāṇaṃ vāce ma ity aindravāyavaṃ dakṣakratubhyāṃ ma iti maitrāvaruṇaṃ cakṣurbhyāṃ ma iti śukrāmanthinau śrotrāya ma ity āśvinam ātmane ma ity āgrayaṇam aṅgebhyo ma ity ukthyam āyuṣe ma iti dhurvaṃ vīryāya ma ity atigrāhyāṃs tejase ma ojase me varcase ma iti vaitair yathārūpaṃ varcodā varcase pavasveti sarvatrānuṣajati
8.14.1	viṣṇor jaṭharam asīti droṇakalaśam indrasya jaṭharam asīty ādhavanīyaṃ viśveṣāṃ devānāṃ jaṭharam asīti pūtabhṛtaṃ varcodā me varcase pavasveti sarvatrānuṣajati
8.14.2	ko 'si ko nāmeti sarvaṃ rājānam aviśeṣeṇa
8.14.3	bubhūṣan brahmavarcasakāma āmayāvy annādyakāmo 'bhicaran vāvekṣeta
8.14.4	sphyaḥ svastir ity utkare vedikaraṇāni saṃnyastāni yathārūpam
8.14.5	yajñiyā yajñakṛtaḥ stheti sarvāṇi
8.14.6	upa mā dyāvāpṛthivī iti dyāvāpṛthivī
8.14.7	upāstāva iti yatra bahiṣpavamānena stuvate
8.14.8	upa kalaśa iti droṇakalaśam upa soma iti somam upāgnir ity agnim upa devā iti devān upa yajña iti yajñam upa mā hotrā upahave hvayantām iti hotrakān
8.14.9	hvayatāṃ hvayetāṃ hvayantām iti yathārūpaṃ sarvatrānuṣajati
8.14.10	namo 'gnaye makhaghne makhasya mā yaśo 'ryād ity āhavanīyam upatiṣṭhate
8.14.11	namo rudrāya makhaghne namaskṛtyā mā pāhīty āgnīdhram
8.14.12	nama indrāya makhaghna indriyaṃ me vīryaṃ mā nirvadhīr iti hotrīyam
8.14.13	namo yamāya makhagne namaskṛtyā mā pāhīti mārjālīyam
8.14.14	dṛḍhe sthaḥ śithire ity adhiṣvaṇaphalake
8.14.15	dyāvāpṛthivī samīkṣata ity ekeṣām
8.14.16	sūryo mā devo divyād aṃhasas pātv iti sūryaṃ vāyur antarikṣād iti vāyum agniḥ pṛthivyā ity agniṃ yamaḥ pitṛbhya iti yamaṃ sarasvatī manuṣyebhya iti sarasvatīṃ pātu pātv iti sarvatrānuṣajati
8.14.17	devī dvārāv iti dvāryau namaḥ sadasa iti sado namaḥ sadasaspataya iti sadasaspatiṃ namaḥ sakhīnāṃ purogāṇāṃ cakṣuṣa ity ṛtvijo namo diva iti divaṃ namaḥ pṛthivyā iti pṛthivīm
8.14.18	ahe daidhiṣavyeti yatra niṣatsyan bhavati tatas tṛṇaṃ loṣṭaṃ vā nirasyāpa upaspṛśyon nivata ud udvataś ca geṣam ity upaviśati
8.14.19	sadaḥ prasṛpya dakṣiṇārdhaṃ parekṣetāganta pitara iti
8.14.20	atra paśuṃ viśāsti
8.14.21	śrapyamāṇaḥ sarvāṇi savanāni pariśete tṛtīyasavane vā śrapyate
8.15.1	puroḍāśān āsādya taiḥ samavadāya pracarati
8.15.2	juhūpabhṛtor upastīryāvadāyābhighārya prātaḥ prātaḥsāvasyendrāya puroḍāśānām anubrūhi prataḥ prātaḥsāvasyendrāya puroḍāśān prasthitān preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati
8.15.3	aupabhṛtaṃ juhvāṃ paryasyāgnaye 'nubrūhy agnaye preṣyeti sviṣṭakṛti saṃpreṣyati
8.15.4	prāśitram iḍā ca kriyete prāśitram avadāya neḍām avadyati
8.15.5	dvidevatyeṣu marutvatīyayor ādityagrahe sāvitre hāriyojane ca yājyānuvākye
8.15.6	yājyaivetarāsu somāhutiṣu
8.15.7	ubhayīṣv āśrutapratyāśrute yājyāsaṃpraiṣaś ca vyākhyātaḥ
8.15.8	puronuvākyāvatīṣu puronuvākyāsaṃpreṣaḥ
8.15.9	grahaṃ camasaṃ vādāyāśrāvayati yathā darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ
8.15.10	āgnīdhrāgāre dakṣiṇāmukhas tiṣṭhann āgnīdhraḥ sphyaṃ dhārayan pratyāśrāvayati tad vyākhyātam
8.15.11	saṃpraiṣās tv ekadhanā yājyāḥ
8.15.12	tatrādhvaryur āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite 'muṣmai preṣyeti maitrāvaruṇaṃ preṣyati sa hotāraṃ codayati
8.15.13	vaṣaṭkṛte juhoty anuvaṣaṭkṛte hutvā harati bhakṣam
8.15.14	sarvasomānām eṣa kalpaḥ
8.15.15	dvidevatyartugraheṣv ādityagrahasāvitrayoś ca nānuvaṣaṭkāro vidyate kṛtākṛtaḥ śukrāmanthinoḥ pātnīvate ca
8.15.16	dvidevatyaiḥ pracarataḥ
8.15.17	upayāmagṛhīto 'si vāyava indravāyubhyāṃ tvety aindravāyavasyaikadeśam ādityapātreṇa pratiprasthātā pratinirgrāhyaṃ gṛhṇāti
8.15.18	upayāmagṛhīto 'si vākṣasad asīti ca droṇakalaśād dvitīyam
8.15.19	aindravāyavam adhvaryur ādatte droṇakalaśāc ca pariplavayā rājānaṃ pratinigrāhyaṃ pratiprasthātā
8.15.20	upaniṣkramyādhvaro yajño 'yam astu devā iti pariplavayāghārayati yathopāṃśur huto bhavati
8.15.21	vāyava indravāyubhyām anubrūhi vāyava indravāyubhyāṃ preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati
8.15.22	vaṣaṭkṛte juhutaḥ punar vaṣaṭkṛte juhutaḥ
8.15.23	adhvaryoḥ pātre pratiprasthātā saṃpātam avanayati tasyaikadeśam adhvaryuḥ pratiprasthātuḥ pātre
8.15.24	devebhyas tvety ādityasthālyāṃ pratiprasthātā saṃpātam avanayati
8.16.1	viṣṇav uru kramety apidadhāti
8.16.2	mayi vasuḥ purovasur ity adhvaryur hotre bhakṣaṃ prayacchati
8.16.3	tenaiva hotā pratigṛhṇāti
8.16.4	evam uttarābhyāṃ yathādaivataṃ pracarataḥ
8.16.5	nottarayor droṇakalaśād gṛhṇāti nottarayor āghāro vidyate
8.16.6	uttareṇottareṇa mantreṇa sakṛd gṛhṇāti sakṛj juhutaḥ
8.16.7	uttareṇottareṇādityasthālyāṃ pratiprasthātā saṃpātam avanayati tenaiva sarvatrāpidadhāti
8.16.8	uttareṇottareṇādhvaryur hotre bhakṣaṃ prayacchaty etenaiva hotā pratigṛhṇāti
8.16.9	diteḥ putrāṇām aditer akāriṣam uruśarmaṇāṃ bṛhatāṃ varūthinām / yeṣāṃ dhāmāni nihitāni dhāmaśaś citrair yajanti bhuvanāni viśveti vā sarvatrāpidadhāti
8.16.10	yadi kāmayeta pāpam asya saṃsyād iti pratiprasthānena pūrvo gṛhītvā pūrvas tiṣṭhañ juhuyāt pūrvo hutvā sādayet
8.16.11	yadi kāmayeta samāvad vīryo bhrātṛvyeṇa syād iti yugapadgṛhṇīto yugapajjuhuto yugapatsādayataḥ
8.16.12	dhārāgrahakāle gṛhṇātīty ekeṣām
8.16.13	atra pātrāṇy utsādayati
8.16.14	yadi kāmayeta yo grāme taṃ grāmān nirūhya yo bahir grāmāt taṃ grāme kuryād itīdam aham amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣya putram amuṣyai viśo nirūhāmīty adhvaryuḥ pātraṃ nirūhyedam aham amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣya putram amuṣyāṃ viśi sādayāmīti pratiprasthānaṃ sādayed ayajñasaṃyuktaḥ kalpaḥ
8.16.15	ādhavanīyaṃ pūtabhṛty avanīya daśābhiḥ kalaśaṃ mṛṣṭvā nyuñjati
8.16.16	hotā brahmodgātā yajamānaḥ sadasyaś ceti madhyataḥkāriṇo maitrāvaruṇo brāhmaṇācchaṃsī potā neṣṭācchāvāka āgnīdhraś ca hotrakāḥ
8.16.17	ubhaye camasino bhavanti sarveṣāṃ pratipuruṣaṃ camasādhvaryavaḥ
8.17.1	unnīyamānebhyo 'nubrūhi hotuś camasam anūnnayadhvam ubhayataḥśukrān kurudhvam acchāvākasya camasādhvaryo mā tvam unneṣṭhāḥ pratiprasthātaḥ prokṣitāprokṣitāñ chakalān upakalpayonnetaḥ somaṃ prabhāvayeti saṃpreṣyati
8.17.2	hotṛcamasamukhyān daśa camasān unnayaty anyān acchāvākacamasāt
8.17.3	pariplavayonnetā droṇakalaśād upastīrya pūtabhṛta unnīya droṇakalaśād abhighārayati
8.17.4	sarvacamasānām eṣa kalpaḥ
8.17.5	prasthiteṣv evonnīyamāne sūkte tasmin parihite sāvitreṇa grahāv ādadāte
8.17.6	śukram adhvaryur manthinaṃ pratiprasthātā
8.17.7	ādadate camasāṃś camasādhvaravaḥ
8.17.8	prokṣitābhyāṃ śakalābhyāṃ śukrāmanthināv apidhatto 'panuttau śaṇḍāmarkau saha tena yaṃ dviṣma ity aprokṣitābhyām adhastāt pāṃsūn apadhvaṃsayatas tābhyāṃ caivopayacchataḥ
8.17.9	stuto 'si janadhā devās tvā śukrapāḥ praṇayantv iti śukram adhvaryur harati stuto 'si janadhā devās tvā manthipāḥ praṇayantv iti manthinaṃ pratiprasthātā
8.17.10	tāv ādānāv eke samāmananty urv antarikṣam iti gacchataḥ
8.17.11	āyuḥ saṃdhattaṃ taṃ me jinvataṃ prāṇaṃ saṃdhattaṃ taṃ me jinvatam apānaṃ saṃdhattaṃ taṃ me jinvataṃ vyānaṃ saṃdhattaṃ taṃ me jinvataṃ cakṣuḥ saṃdhattaṃ tan me jinvataṃ śrotraṃ saṃdhattaṃ tan me jinvataṃ manaḥ saṃdhattaṃ tan me jinvataṃ vācaṃ saṃdhattaṃ tāṃ me jinvatam ity agreṇa havirdhāne aratnī pātre vā saṃdhattaḥ
8.17.12	anādhṛṣṭāsīty aṅguṣṭhābhyām uttaravedim ākramete
8.17.13	tāṃ viparihantau viparikrāmataḥ
8.17.14	suvīrāḥ prajāḥ prajanayan parīhi śukraḥ śukraśociṣeti dakṣiṇenādhvaryur harati suprajāḥ prajāḥ prajanayan parīhi manthī manthiśociṣety uttareṇa pratiprasthātā
8.17.15	jinvethāṃ supathyā madhvā vītam iti yajamāno 'nuyantrayate 'greṇāhavanīyam
8.17.16	abhito yūpaṃ purastāt pratyañcāv avatiṣṭhete
8.17.17	paścāt prāñcaś camasādhvaryavaḥ
8.17.18	saṃjagmānau diva ā pṛthivyāḥ śukraḥ śukraśociṣety adhvaryuḥ saṃjagmānau diva ā pṛthivyā manthī manthiśociṣeti pratiprasthātāratnī pātre vā saṃdhattaḥ
8.18.1	āyuḥ stha āyur me dhattam āyur yajñāya dhattam āyur yajñapataye dhattaṃ prāṇaḥ sthaḥ prāṇaṃ me dhattaṃ prāṇaṃ yajñāya dhattaṃ prāṇaṃ yajñapataye dhattaṃ cakṣuḥ sthaś cakṣur me dhattaṃ cakṣur yajñāya dhattaṃ cakṣur yajñapataye dhattaṃ śrotraṃ sthaḥ śrotraṃ me dhattaṃ śrotraṃ yajñāya dhattaṃ śrotraṃ yajñapataye dhattaṃ tau devau śukrāmanthinau kalpayataṃ daivīr viśaḥ kalpayataṃ mānuṣīr iṣam ūrjam asmāsu dhattaṃ prāṇān paśuṣu prajāṃ mayi ca yajamāne cety abhimantrayete
8.18.2	prokṣitau śakalāv abhyādhattaḥ śukrasyādhiṣṭhānam asi śukraiṣā te samit tayā samidhyasvety adhvaryur manthino 'dhiṣṭhānam asi manthinn eṣā te samit tayā samidhyasveti pratiprasthātā
8.18.3	nirastaḥ śaṇḍo nirasto marko 'panuttau śaṇḍāmarkau saha tena yaṃ dviṣma ity aprokṣitau bahirvedi nirasyato 'pa upaspṛśya
8.18.4	prātaḥ prātaḥsāvasya śukravato manthivato madhuścuta indrāya somān prasthitān preṣya madhyataḥkāriṇāṃ camasādhvaryavo vaṣaṭkṛtānuvaṣaṭkṛtāñ juhuta hotrakāṇāṃ camasādhvaryavaḥ sakṛtsakṛddhutvā śukrasyābhyunnīyopāvartadhvam iti saṃpreṣyati
8.18.5	vaṣaṭkṛte sarve yugapaj juhvati
8.18.6	sa prathamaḥ saṃkṛtir viśvakarmā sa prathamo mitro varuṇo agniḥ / sa prathamo bṛhaspatiś cikitvāṃs tasmā indrāya sutam ājuhomi svāhety adhvaryus tasmai mitrāya sutam ājuhomi svāheti pratiprasthātā
8.18.7	sānuvaṣaṭkārāv eke samāmananty ananuvaṣaṭkārāv eke 'nyataraṃ sānuvaṣaṭkāram eke
8.18.8	uttarataḥpurastād bahiṣparidhy āhavanīyād aṅgāraṃ nirvartyaiṣa te rudra bhāga iti tasminn etaṃ manthinaḥ saṃsrāvaṃ pratiprasthātā sarvahutaṃ juhoti
8.18.9	madhyataḥkāriṇāṃ camasādhvaryavo 'nuvaṣaṭkṛte juhvati
8.18.10	praitu hotuś camasaḥ pra brahmaṇaḥ prodgātuḥ pra yajamānasya pra sadasyasyeti saṃpreṣyati
8.18.11	sado bhakṣān haranti
8.18.12	sūdavac chukrapātraṃ sādayati
8.18.13	hotrakāṇāṃ camasādhvaryavaḥ sakṛtsakṛddhutvā śukrasyābhyunnīyopāvartante
8.18.14	tair adhvaryuḥ pracarati
8.18.15	maitrāvaruṇacamasam ādāya praśāstar yajeti saṃpreṣyati vaṣaṭkṛtānuvaṣaṭkṛte hutvā camasādhvaryave prayacchati sado bhakṣaṃ harati
8.18.16	evam uttaraiḥ pracarati
8.19.1	brahman yajeti brāhmaṇācchaṃsinaṃ potar yajeti potāraṃ neṣṭar yajeti neṣṭāram agnīd yajety āgnīdhram
8.19.2	tasya camasam ādāya sado gacchati sa hotur ācaṣṭe 'yāḍ agnīd iti
8.19.3	sa bhadram akar yo naḥ somaṃ pāyayiṣyatīti hotā pratyāha
8.19.4	homābhiṣavābhyām adhvaryor bhakṣo vaṣaṭkārāc ca vaṣaṭkartṝṇāṃ samākhyānāc camasinām
8.19.5	vaṣaṭkartā pūrvo bhakṣayati tato 'dhvaryur jaghanyaś camasī
8.19.6	homayor vaṣaṭkāravyavāye bhakṣavyavāye vaṣaṭkārayoś ca homavyavāye pratiśeṣaṃ pratigrahaṇaṃ ca bhakṣaḥ
8.19.7	nānāgṛhītayoś ca samavāye
8.19.8	na vaiśyarājanyayoḥ somabhakṣaṇaṃ vidyate
8.19.9	yady abrāhmaṇaḥ somaṃ pipāsen nyagrodhastibhinīr āhṛtya tāḥ saṃpiṣya dadhany unmṛjya yad anyāṃś camasān unnayaty athaitaṃ yajamānacamasam ata unnayati yad anyāṃś camasāñ juhvaty athaitasya darbhataruṇenopahatyāntaḥparidhy āhavanīyād aṅgāraṃ nirvartyāhaṃ tvad asmīti juhoti yad anyāṃś camasān bhakṣayaty athaitasya camasasya yajamāno bhakṣayati
8.19.10	dvidevatyān bhakṣayanti
8.19.11	hotādhvaryuḥ pratiprasthātā ca
8.19.12	evam anupūrvāḥ
8.19.13	anyonyasminn upahavam icchante
8.19.14	upahvayasvety āmantraṇaḥ
8.19.15	upahūta iti prativacanaḥ
8.19.16	yatra kvacaikakāle bhakṣayeyur anyonyasminn upahavam iccheran
8.19.17	dvir aindravāyavaṃ bhakṣayati sakṛtsakṛd itarau
8.19.18	purastād aindravāyavaṃ prāṇeṣūpanigrāhaṃ purastān maitrāvaruṇaṃ cakṣuṣor upanigrāhaṃ sarvataḥ parihāram āśvinaṃ śrotrayor upanigrāham
8.19.19	sarvān bhakṣayitvā nānutsṛjanty āvanayanāt
8.19.20	sarveṣāṃ saṃpātān hotṛcamase 'vanīya puroḍāśaśakalam aindravāyavasya pātre 'vadadhāti payasyāṃ maitrāvaruṇasya dhānā āśvinasya tāni dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasyottarasyāṃ vartanyāṃ sādayaty ā tṛtīyasavanāt pariśerate
8.19.21	niravadāya hotra iḍām ādadhāti
8.19.22	upahūyamānām upodyacchante camasāṃś camasādhvaryavaḥ
8.19.23	hotṛcamasam āspṛṣṭaṃ dhārayati
8.19.24	upahūtāṃ prāśnanti ye prakṛtau
8.19.25	iḍāśakalam acchāvākāya nidadhāti prāśitāyāṃ mārjayitvā
8.19.26	vājinena carati yathā vaiśvadeve
8.20.1	savanīyānāṃ mārjanaprabhṛtīni karmāṇi pratipadyate yathā nirūḍhapaśubandhe paśupuroḍāśasya
8.20.2	yathācamasaṃ camasino bhakṣayanti teṣāṃ vyākhyāto bhakṣamantraḥ
8.20.3	sarveṣāṃ prathamo hotā sakṛtsakṛd bhakṣayati dviḥ sve camase punaḥ
8.20.4	abhyunnītānām adhvaryur dvirbhakṣitānāṃ sakṛtsakṛd bhakṣayati
8.20.5	tṛtīyaṃ hotrakā antataḥ
8.20.6	asarvān bhakṣayitvāpyāyasva sametu ta ity āpyāyayanti te nārāśaṃsā bhavanti
8.20.7	tān dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasya paścādakṣam udagāyatān sādayaty antarā neṣṭur āgnīdhrasya ca camasau sādayati
8.20.8	upaviśaty acchāvāko 'greṇa svaṃ dhiṣṇiyaṃ bahiḥsadasam
8.20.9	tasmai puroḍāśaśakalam ādadad āhācchāvāka vadasva yat te vādyam iti
8.20.10	upo asmān brāhmaṇān brāhmaṇā hvayadhvam ity acchāvākenocyamāne 'cchāvāko vā ayam upahavam icchate taṃ hotar upahvayasveti saṃpreṣyati
8.20.11	yatrainaṃ hotropahūyamānaṃ jānāti tasmin kāle 'cchāvākacamasam ādāyonnīyamānāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
8.20.12	tasmin parihite 'cchāvāka yajeti saṃpreṣyati vaṣaṭkṛte juhoty anuvaṣaṭkṛte hutvā harati bhakṣam
8.20.13	tena na samaṃ bhakṣayati
8.20.14	nāsminn upahavam icchate
8.20.15	yady asminn upahavam iccheta bhakṣayety eva brūyāt
8.20.16	bhakṣitāpyāyitam antarā neṣṭur āgnīdhrasya ca camasau sādayati
8.20.17	etad evāta ūrdhvam acchāvākacamasasya sthānam
8.21.1	ṛtugrahaiḥ pracarato dvādaśabhir trayodaśabhiś caturdaśabhir vā dvādaśasu sarvān nānā juhutas trayodaśasv anyatarau saha caturdaśasu saha prathamau sahottamau
8.21.2	asannā hūyante
8.21.3	pūrvasyapūrvasya śeṣa uttaramuttaram abhigṛhṇītaḥ
8.21.4	upayāmagṛhīto 'si madhave tveti svena pātreṇādhvaryuḥ pūrvaṃ gṛhṇāty upayāmagṛhīto 'si mādhavāya tveti svena pātreṇa pratiprasthātottaram
8.21.5	vyatiṣaṅgaṃ gṛhṇītaḥ
8.21.6	pūrvo 'dhvaryur aparaḥ pratiprasthātā
8.21.7	pūrveṇapūrveṇa mantreṇādhvaryur uttareṇottareṇa pratiprasthātā
8.21.8	dakṣiṇenādhvaryuḥ saṃcaraty uttareṇa pratiprasthātā
8.21.9	nānyonyam anuprapadyeta
8.21.10	praviśantam adhvaryuṃ graheṇa parigṛhṇāti niṣkrāmantaṃ pātreṇa
8.21.11	ṛtunā preṣyeti trir adhvaryur āha triḥ pratiprasthātā
8.21.12	pātrayor mukhe viparyasyartubhiḥ preṣyeti dvir adhvaryur āha dviḥ pratiprasthātā
8.21.13	punar mukhe viparyasyartunā preṣyeti sakṛd adhvaryur āha sakṛt pratiprasthātā
8.21.14	adhvaryū yajatam ity ucyamāne hotar etad yajeti saṃpreṣyati
8.21.15	svayaṃ vā niṣadya yajataḥ
8.21.16	adhvaryoḥ pātre pratiprasthātā saṃpātam avanayati tasyaikadeśam adhvaryuḥ pratiprasthātuḥ pātre
8.21.17	pratiprasthānena bhakṣayanti
8.21.18	dvir hotā sakṛtsakṛd itare
8.21.19	yasyayasya vaṣaṭkāre juhutas taṃtaṃ prati bhakṣayataḥ
8.21.20	mārjālīye pātraṃ prakṣālyāyatane sādayati
8.22.1	indrāgnī āgataṃ sutam iti svena pātreṇābhakṣitenaindrāgnaṃ kalaśāc chastravantaṃ gṛhṇāti
8.22.2	taṃ sādayitvāgreṇa hotāraṃ prāṅmukha upaviśyeḍā devahūr iti śastram upākaroti
8.22.3	yatrainaṃ hotābhyāhvayate tasmin kāle śoṃsā moda iveti pratyāhvayate śoṃsā moda ivothāmoda iveti vā
8.22.4	uttiṣṭhan pradakṣiṇaṃ paryāvartamānaḥ prathamaṃ pratigaraṃ pratigṛhṇāty abhimukho 'ta ūrdhvas tiṣṭhan prahvo vā
8.22.5	sarveṣu virāmeṣu praṇave ca
8.22.6	nārdharcāl lupyate
8.22.7	nābhi pratigṛṇāti
8.22.8	ubhayaṃ vyāhāve karoti śoṃsāmoda ivothāmoda iveti
8.22.9	yatra kvaca hotā viramed othā moda iveti prabrūyāt
8.22.10	sarvaśastrāṇām eṣa kalpaḥ
8.22.11	ukthaśā iti śastraṃ pratigīrya sarvatra prātaḥsavane japati
8.22.12	śastraṃ pratigīrya graham ādatte camasāṃś camasādhvaryava ukthaśā yaja somasyeti saṃpreṣyati
8.22.13	vaṣaṭkārānuvaṣaṭkārau nārāśaṃsān anuprakampayanti
8.22.14	vyākhyāto grahanārāśaṃsānāṃ bhakṣaḥ
8.22.15	āpyāyanasādane ca nārāśaṃsānām
8.23.1	omāsaś carṣaṇīdhṛta iti śukrapātreṇa vaiśvadevaṃ kalaśāt stutaśastravantaṃ gṛhṇāti
8.23.2	taṃ sādayitvā stotram upākaroti tad vyākhyātam
8.23.3	apavṛtte stotre śastram upākaroti tad vyākhyātam
8.23.4	śastraṃ pratigīrya graham ādatte camasāṃś camasādhvaryava ukthaśā yaja somasyeti saṃpreṣyati vyākhyātam anuprakampanaṃ grahanārāśaṃsānāṃ bhakṣaḥ sarvabhakṣāḥ
8.23.5	nāpyāyanasādane bhavataḥ
8.23.6	tribhir ukthyavigrahaiḥ pracarataḥ
8.23.7	upayāmagṛhīto 'si mitrāvaruṇābhyāṃ tvety ukthyasthālyā ukthyapātreṇa tṛtīyaṃ maitrāvaruṇaṃ gṛhṇāti
8.23.8	eṣa te yonir mitrāvaruṇābhyāṃ tvety āyatane sādayati
8.23.9	punar havir asīti sthālīṃ pratyabhimṛśati
8.23.10	maitrāvaruṇacamasamukhyān ekādaśa camasān unnayati
8.23.11	purastād āgnīdhracamasād acchāvākacamasam unnayati stutaśastre bhavataḥ
8.23.12	śastraṃ pratigīrya graham ādatte camasāṃś camasādhvaryava ukthaśā yaja somānām iti saṃpreṣyati
8.24.1	hutvā devebhyas tvā devāyuvaṃ pṛṇajmi yajñasyāyuṣe juṣṭam iti maitrāvaruṇacamase grahasaṃpātam avanayati
8.24.2	bāhyataḥ sada ālabhya
8.24.3	yadi kāmayetādhvaryur ātmānaṃ yajñayaśasenārpayeyam iti brāhmaṇavyākhyātāny avanayanāni teṣāṃ yāthākāmī
8.24.4	sarveṣāṃ prathamo maitrāvaruṇaḥ sakṛtsakṛd bhakṣayati dviḥ sve camase tasyādhvaryur dvir bhakṣitasya sakṛd bhakṣayati tṛtīyaṃ maitrāvaruṇaḥ
8.24.5	tataḥ pratiprasthātottarābhyām ukthyavigrahābhyāṃ stutaśastravadbhyāṃ pracaraty etenaiva kalpena
8.24.6	indrāya tveti dvitīye grahaṇasādanau saṃnamati punar havir asīti sthālīṃ pratyabhimṛśati
8.24.7	brāhmaṇācchaṃsicamasamukhyāṃś camasān unnayann ekasmai camasagaṇāya rājānam atirecayati
8.24.8	brāhmaṇācchaṃsicamase grahasaṃpātam avanayati na pratiprasthātā bhakṣayati
8.24.9	indrāgnibhyāṃ tveti tṛtīye grahaṇasādanau saṃnamati
8.24.10	na sthālīṃ pratyabhimṛśati
8.24.11	acchāvākacamasamukhyāṃś camasān unnaya sarvaṃ rājānam unnaya mātirīrico daśābhiḥ kalaśau mṛṣṭvā nyubjeti saṃpreṣyati
8.24.12	acchāvākacamasamukhyāṃś camasān unnayati sarvaṃ rājānam unnayati nātirecayati
8.24.13	daśābhiḥ kalaśau mṛṣṭvā nyubjati
8.24.14	acchāvākacamase grahasaṃpātam avanayati na pratiprasthātā bhakṣayati
8.24.15	agniḥ prātaḥsavane pātv asmān iti saṃsthite juhoti
8.24.16	praśāstaḥ prasuveti saṃpreṣyati
8.24.17	sarpatety āha praśāstā
8.24.18	saṃtiṣṭhate prātaḥsavanaṃ prātaḥsavanam
9.1.1	abhiṣavādi mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanaṃ tāyate
9.1.2	tasya prātaḥsavanena kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
9.1.3	dvidevatyartugrahaindrāgnavaiśvadevā darvihomāś ca na vidyante
9.1.4	vasatīvarībhyo niṣicya nigrābhyāḥ karoti
9.1.5	sarvaṃ rājānam abhiṣunvanti
9.1.6	grāvastute somoṣṇīṣaṃ prayacchati
9.1.7	ihā iheti saṃrādhayanto 'bhiṣunvanti
9.1.8	uttamasya paryāyasya madhyame 'bhiṣave bṛhad bṛhad ity abhiṣunvanti
9.1.9	uttame 'bhiṣave susaṃbhṛte rājani
9.1.10	devā grāvāṇa indur indra ity avādiṣur endram acucyavuḥ paramasyāḥ parāvata āsmāt sadhasthād oror antarikṣād ā subhūtam asuṣavur brahmavarcasaṃ ma āsuṣavuḥ samare rakṣāṃsy avadhiṣur apahataṃ brahmajyasyeti pratiprasthātā grāvṇo 'numodate
9.1.11	atra savanīyānāṃ nirvapaṇam eke samāmananti
9.1.12	dhārāgrahakāle śukrāmanthināv evāgre gṛhītvāgrayaṇaṃ tisṛbhyo dhārābhyo gṛhṇāty ādhavanīyāt tṛtīyāṃ dhārāṃ karoty ukthyaṃ gṛhītvā
9.1.13	ṛtupātrābhyāṃ marutvatīyau gṛhṇīto marutvantaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ vāvṛdhānam iti svena pātreṇādhvaryuḥ pūrvaṃ gṛhṇāti marutvāṃ indra vṛṣabho raṇāyeti svena pātreṇa pratiprasthātottaram
9.1.14	gṛhītvā rājānam atipāvayati yāvantaṃ mādhyaṃdināya svanāyāptaṃ manyate
9.1.15	viramati dhārā prapīḍya pavitraṃ nidadhāti
9.1.16	vyākhyātam ekadhanānām ādhavanīye 'vanayanam
9.1.17	pavamānagrahān kalaśāñ śukrāmanthināv āgrayaṇam ukthyaṃ ca grahāvakāśair upasthāya niḥsarpantaḥ samanvārabhante
9.1.18	vaipruṣān saptahotāraṃ ca hutvā mādhyaṃdinaṃ pavamānaṃ sarpanti tasya bahiṣpavamānena kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
9.2.1	traiṣṭubhaḥ panthā rudrā devatāvṛkeṇāparipareṇa pathā svasti rudrān aśīyeti mantraṃ saṃnamati
9.2.2	uttareṇa havirdhānaṃ gatvottareṇāgnīdhrīyaṃ dhiṣṇiyaṃ parītya dakṣiṇena vā mārjālīyam antareṇa vā
9.2.3	pūrveṇa dvāreṇa sadaḥ praviśyādhvaryur yajamāno brahmā cāvatiṣṭhante 'greṇa praśāstrīyaṃ dhiṣṇiyaṃ parītyodgātāro mādhyaṃdinena pavamānena stuvate
9.2.4	yad anyat paśvānayanāt tat sampreṣyati pratiprasthātar dadhigharmeṇa careti saṃpraiṣasyāntaṃ saṃnamati
9.2.5	vihṛteṣu vyāghāriteṣu dhiṣṇiyeṣu
9.2.6	stīrṇe barhiṣi
9.2.7	pratiprasthātā paśupuroḍāśaṃ nirūpya savanīyān nirvapati
9.2.8	ekādaśakapālo 'tra puroḍāśaḥ
9.2.9	nāmikṣā vidyate
9.2.10	alaṃkṛteṣu pratiprasthātā dadhigharmeṇa carati
9.2.11	yāvatī dyāvāpṛthivī ity āgnīdhrāgāra audumbaryāṃ sruci dadhi gṛhṇāti
9.2.12	vāk ca tvā manaś ca śrīṇītāṃ prāṇaś ca tvāpānaś ca śrīṇītāṃ cakṣuś ca tvā śrotraṃ ca śrīṇītāṃ dakṣaś ca tvā balaṃ ca śrīṇītām ojaś ca tvā sahaś ca śrīṇītām āyuś ca tvā jarā ca śrīṇītām ātmā ca tvā tanūś ca śrīṇītaṃ śṛto 'si śṛtaṃ kṛtaḥ śṛtāya tvā śṛtebhyas tvety āgnīdhrīye 'dhiśritya
9.2.13	hotar vadasva yat te vādyam iti saṃpreṣyati
9.2.14	yadi śrāto juhotana yady aśrāto mamattanety ucyamāne śrātaṃ havir iti pratyāha
9.2.15	tam ādāyāhavanīyaṃ gatvāśrāvya pratyāśrāvite dadhigharmasya yajeti saṃpreṣyati
9.2.16	yam indram āhur varuṇaṃ yam āhur yaṃ mitram āhur yam u satyam āhuḥ / yo devānāṃ devatamas tapojās tasmai tvā tebhyas tvā svāheti vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti
9.2.17	anuvaṣaṭkṛte hutvā harati bhakṣam
9.2.18	taṃ bhakṣayanti ye pravargye
9.2.19	tasyāraṇye 'nuvākyo bhakṣamantraḥ
9.3.1	puroḍāśān āsādya taiḥ samavadāya pracarati mādhyaṃdinasya savanasyeti saṃpreṣyati
9.3.2	paśupuroḍāśena pracarya samavadāya savanīyaiḥ pracarati
9.3.3	paśupuroḍāśasya savanīyānāṃ ca samānaṃ sviṣṭakṛdiḍam
9.3.4	ādhavanīyaṃ pūtabhṛty avanīya daśābhiḥ kalaśaṃ mṛṣṭvā nyubjati
9.3.5	unnīyamānebhyo 'nubrūhi hotuś camasam anūnnayadhvam ubhayataḥśukrān kurudhvam acchāvākasya camasādhvaryo 'pi tvam unnayasva pratiprasthātaḥ prokṣitāprokṣitāñ chakalān upakalpayonnetaḥ somaṃ prabhāvayeti saṃpreṣyati
9.3.6	hotṛcamasamukhyān ekādaśa camasān unnayati purastād āgnīdhracamasād acchāvākacamasam unnayati
9.3.7	mādhyaṃdinasya savanasya niṣkevalyasya bhāgasya śukravato manthivato madhuścuta indrāya somān prasthitān preṣya madhyataḥkāriṇāṃ camasādhvaryavo vaṣaṭkṛtānuvaṣaṭkṛtāñ juhuta hotrakāṇāṃ camasādhvaryavaḥ sakṛtsakṛddhutvā śukrasyābhyunnīyopāvartadhvam iti saṃpreṣyati yat prāk punarabhyunnītebhyas tasmin kṛte prasarvaṇamantrair hotrakāḥ prasṛpya punarabhyunnītānāṃ yajanti
9.3.8	ayāḍ agnīd iti hotur ākhyāya niravadāya hotra iḍām ādadhāty upahūyamānām upodyacchante camasāṃś camasādhvaryavaḥ
9.3.9	neḍāśakalam acchāvākāya nidadhāti
9.3.10	yathācamasaṃ camasino bhakṣayanti teṣāṃ vyākhyāto bhakṣamantraḥ
9.3.11	sanneṣu nārāśaṃseṣu dakṣiṇena vedim avasthitāsu dakṣiṇāsu dākṣiṇāni juhoti yathā vaisarjanāni
9.3.12	pracchādanārthasya vāsaso daśāyāṃ hiraṇyaṃ baddhvājye 'vadhāya srugdaṇḍe vāsaso 'ntam upaniyamyod u tyaṃ citram iti dvābhyāṃ śālāmukhīye juhoti śeṣam ājyasya karoti
9.3.13	nīyamānāsu pūrvaḥ pratipadyāgne nayeti nayavatyarcāgnīdhre juhoti
9.3.14	śeṣam ājyasya karoti
9.3.15	divaṃ gaccha suvaḥ pateti hiraṇyaṃ hutvodgṛhṇāti
9.3.16	vaneṣu vy antarikṣaṃ tatāneti dvitīyāṃ yady ano ratho 'dhīvāso vā dīyate
9.3.17	prajāpate na tvad etānīti tṛtīyāṃ yady aśvaḥ puruṣo hastī vā dīyate
9.3.18	nītāsu dakṣiṇāsu yajñapatim ṛṣaya enasāhur iti
9.4.1	pañcabhir āgnīdhrīye vaiśvakarmaṇāni juhoti
9.4.2	yathāgṛhītaṃ marutvatīyāv ādāyendrāya marutvate 'nubrūhīndrāya marutvate preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati
9.4.3	hutvā vyavanayete
9.4.4	yathartugraheṣu pratiprasthānena bhakṣayanti
9.4.5	dvir hotā sakṛtsakṛd itarau
9.4.6	mārjālīye pātraṃ prakṣālya hotuḥ sakāśe nidadhāti
9.4.7	janiṣṭhā ugraḥ sahase turāya mandra ojiṣṭho bahulābhimānaḥ / avardhann indraṃ marutaś cid atra mātā yad vīraṃ dadhanad dhaniṣṭhā / indra marutva iha pāhīty anyatareṇa svena pātreṇābhakṣitena tṛtīyaṃ marutvatīyaṃ kalaśāc chastravantaṃ gṛhṇāti
9.4.8	ṛtupātram ārabhya pratigṛṇāti
9.4.9	ukthaṃ vācīti śastraṃ pratigīrya sarvatra mādhyaṃdine savane japati
