9.13.21	śataṃ te rājan bhiṣajaḥ sahasram ity apo dṛṣṭvā japanti
9.13.22	abhiṣṭhito varuṇasya pāśa ity udakāntam abhitiṣṭhanti
9.13.23	apaḥ pragāhya tiṣṭhanto 'vabhṛthena caranti
9.13.24	oḍhāsu devatāsūdakam upavājya sruvāghāram āghāryāgnīd udakaṃ triḥ saṃmṛḍḍhīti saṃpreṣyati
9.13.25	saṃmṛṣṭe 'psu tṛṇaṃ prāsya
9.13.26	agner anīkam apa āviveśeti srucyam āghārayati
9.13.27	yathopasatsv evaṃ pravaraṃ pravṛṇīte
9.14.1	tiṣṭhety etāvān pravaraḥ
9.14.2	apabarhiṣaḥ prayājān yajati
9.14.3	nopabhṛtaṃ samānayate
9.14.4	apsumantāv ājyabhāgau
9.14.5	tābhyāṃ pracarya puroḍāśād varuṇaṃ yajati
9.14.6	kṛtsnaṃ puroḍāśam avadāyāgnīvaruṇau sviṣṭakṛtau yajati
9.14.7	agnīd udakaṃ sakṛt saṃmṛḍḍhīti saṃpreṣyati
9.14.8	apabarhiṣāv anūyājau yajati devau yaja yajeti pūrvam anūyājaṃ saṃpreṣyati yajety uttaram
9.14.9	etāvat kriyate
9.14.10	yat te grāvṇā cicchiduḥ soma rājan priyāṇy aṅgāni svadhitā parūṃṣi / tat saṃdhatsvājyenota vardhayasvānāgaso adham it saṃkṣayema / yat te grāvā bāhucyuto acucyavur naro yat te duduhur dakṣiṇena / tat ta āpyāyatāṃ tat te niṣṭhyāyatāṃ deva soma / yat te tvacaṃ bibhidur yac ca yoniṃ yad āsthānāt pracyuto venasi tmanā / tvayā tat soma guptam astu naḥ sā naḥ saṃdhāsat parame vyoman / ahāc charīraṃ payasā sametyānyo'nyo bhavati varṇo asya / tasmin vayam upahūtās tava sma ā no bhaja sadasi viśvarūpa iti catasṛbhir udumbaraśākhayā dadhnarjīṣam abhijuhoti pañcabhiḥ saptabhir navabhir ekādaśabhis trayodaśabhir vā
9.14.11	ṛjīṣasya srucaṃ pūrayitvā samudre te hṛdayam ity apsūpamārayati
9.14.12	apsu dhautasya soma deva ta iti yo bhindūnām uccarati tam avaghreṇa bhakṣayaty upaspṛśati vā
9.14.13	avabhṛtha nicaṅkuṇety avabhṛthaṃ saṃpravidhyanti
9.14.14	devīr āpa ity upatiṣṭhante
9.14.15	sumitrā na iti mājayante
9.15.1	unnetar vasīyo na unnayābhy ud u tye madhumattamā giraḥ stomāsa īrate satrājito dhanasā akṣitotayo vājayanto rathā iva kaṇvā iva bhṛgavaḥ sūryā iva viśvam iddhītam ānaśur ity unnetāraṃ saṃpreṣyati
9.15.2	ud eta prajām uta varco dadhānā yuṣmān rāya uta yajñā asṛkṣata / gāyatraṃ chando 'nusaṃrabhadhvam athā syāma surabhayo gṛheṣv ity unnetā hotṛprathamān yajamānaprathamān vonnayati
9.15.3	pratiyuto varuṇasya pāśa ity udakāntaṃ pratiyauti
9.15.4	pratyasto varuṇasya pāśa ity udakāntaṃ pratyasya
9.15.5	audumbarīḥ samidho dhārayantaḥ
9.15.6	apāma somam amṛtā abhūmeti mahīyāṃ japantaḥ / unnetāraṃ puras kṛtvāpratīkṣam āyanti
9.15.7	parogoṣṭhe mārjayante
9.15.8	edho 'sy edhiṣīmahīty āhavanīye samidho 'bhyādadhati
9.15.9	apo anvacāriṣam ity upatiṣṭhante
9.15.10	evaṃ patnī gārhapatye 'bhyādhāyopatiṣṭhate
9.16.1	prāgvaṃśa udayanīyāyās tantraṃ prakramayati
9.16.2	tasyāḥ prāyaṇīyayā kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
9.16.3	anūyājasamidham upasaṃnahyati
9.16.4	yasyāṃ sthālyāṃ prāyaṇīyaṃ śrapayati tasyāṃ saniṣkāsāyāṃ tena mekṣaṇena śrapayati
9.16.5	patnīṃ saṃnahyati
9.16.6	na juhvām ājyaṃ gṛhṇāti yadi prayājā na bhavanti
9.16.7	kṛtākṛtāḥ prayājāḥ
9.16.8	pathyāṃ svastim uttamām ājyena devatāṃ yajati
9.16.9	na sthālīṃ niṣkāsaṃ mekṣaṇaṃ ca nidadhāti
9.16.10	na dhruvāyāḥ śeṣaṃ karoti
9.16.11	kṛtsnā saṃtiṣṭhate
9.16.12	anūbandhyāyās tantraṃ prakramayati
9.16.13	tasyā nirūḍhapaśubandhena kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
9.16.14	maitrāvaruṇīṃ vaśām upākaroti
9.16.15	tisro vā dvirūpāṃ maitrāvaruṇīṃ bahurūpāṃ vaiśvadevīṃ śitipṛṣṭhāṃ bārhaspatyām iti
9.16.16	upāṃśu madhyato vaiśvadevyā pracaraty āśrutapratyāśrute apy upāṃśu bhavata uccair itarābhyām
9.16.17	anūbandhyāyāḥ paśupuroḍāśaṃ nirūpya daivikāni havīṃṣy anunirvapati
9.16.18	dhātre puroḍāśaṃ dvādaśakapālaṃ nirvapatīti yathāsamāmnātam
9.16.19	somasthālīṣv ete caravaḥ payasi śrapyante
9.16.20	anūbandhyāyāḥ paśupuroḍāśasya devikāhavīṣāṃ ca samānaṃ sviṣṭakṛdiḍam
9.16.21	maitrāvaruṇīṃ puronuvākyām anvāha
9.16.22	saṃpraiṣaś ca bhavati
9.16.23	anūyājānte svaruṃ juhoti hṛdayaśūlena carati yathā purastāt
9.16.24	maitrāvaruṇīm āmikṣām eke 'nūbandhyāyāḥ sthāne samāmananti havirāhutiprabhṛti
9.17.1	iḍāntā saṃtiṣṭhate
9.17.2	sadohavirdhānānāṃ prathamakṛtān granthīn visrasyodīcī havirdhāne bahirvedi nirvartya
9.17.3	yat kusīdam apratīttam ity āhavanīyād vedim upoṣati
9.17.4	prāgvaṃśe gārhapatyāt patnī
9.17.5	etaṃ sadhastha pari te dadāmīti tisṛbhir dhūmam udyantam anumantrayate
9.17.6	viśvalopa viśvadāvasya tvāsañ juhomīty añjalinā saktūn pradāvye juhuyād yadi miśram iva caritvā manyate
9.17.7	pṛthagaraṇīṣv agnīn samāropayate prājihitaṃ gārhapatyaṃ dakṣiṇāgniṃ śālāmukhīyaṃ gataśriyas tṛtīyam
9.17.8	prācīnam udīcīnaṃ vodavasāya vihāraṃ sādhayitvodavasānīyām iṣṭiṃ nirvapaty āgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ pañcakapālaṃ vā
9.17.9	tasyopāṃśu sarvaṃ kriyata ottamād anūyājāt
9.17.10	uru viṣṇo vikramasveti pūrṇāhutim eka udavasanīyāyāḥ sthāne samāmananti
9.17.11	sā yāvadrātrau kiyadrātreṇa vā saṃtiṣṭhate tadaiva sāyamagnihotraṃ juhuyāt kāla eva prātarhomaḥ
9.17.12	saṃtiṣṭhate 'gniṣṭomaḥ
9.18.1	ukthyaḥ ṣoḍaśy atirātro 'ptoryāmaś cāgniṣṭomasya guṇavikārā bhavanti
9.18.2	ukthyena paśukāmo yajeta
9.18.3	tasyāgniṣṭomena kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
9.18.4	pañcadaśachadi sadaḥ
9.18.5	kratukaraṇaṃ hutvaitenaiva mantreṇa madhyame paridhāv abhyantaraṃ lepaṃ nimārṣṭi
9.18.6	aindrāgnam ukthye dvitīyaṃ savanīyam ālabhate
9.18.7	tṛtīyasavane dhārāgrahakāla āgrayaṇaṃ gṛhītvokthyaṃ gṛhṇāti
9.18.8	agniṣṭomacamasān unnayaṃs tribhyaś camasagaṇebhyo rājānam atirecayati
9.18.9	sarvaṃ rājānam unnaya mātirīrico daśābhiḥ kalaśau mṛṣṭvā nyubjeti ca lupyate
9.18.10	etad agniṣṭomacamasānāṃ saṃpraiṣasya yoya uttamaḥ saṃsthānacamasagaṇas tam unnayann etat saṃpreṣyati
9.18.11	agniṣṭomacamasaiḥ pracarya tribhir ukthyavigrahaiḥ pracarato yathā purastāt
9.18.12	indrāvaruṇābhyāṃ tveti prathame grahaṇasādanau saṃnamatīndrābṛhaspatibhyāṃ tveti dvitīya indrāviṣṇubhyāṃ tveti tṛtīye
9.18.13	ṣoḍaśinā vīryakāmaḥ
9.18.14	tasyokthyena kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
9.18.15	tasya śuṇṭhyādhīlodhakarṇayā somaṃ krīṇāti
9.18.16	saptadaśachadi sadaḥ
9.18.17	pātrasaṃsādanakāla uttare 'ṃse khādiraṃ catuḥsrakti ṣoḍaśipātraṃ prayunakti
9.18.18	kratukaraṇaṃ hutvaitenaiva mantreṇa droṇakalaśaṃ rarāṭīṃ vopaspṛśati
9.18.19	aindraṃ vṛṣṇiṃ ṣoḍaśini tṛtīyaṃ savanīyam ālabhate
9.18.20	ātiṣṭha vṛtrahann ity eteṣām ekena ṣoḍaśinaṃ gṛhṇāti
9.18.21	purastād uttamād ukthyaparyāyāt pūrvayoḥ savanayor droṇakalaśād gṛhṇāti sarvair ukthyaparyāyaiḥ pracarita āgrayaṇāt tṛtīyasavane
9.19.1	yasmān na jātaḥ paro anyo asti ya āviveśa bhuvanāni viśvā / prajāpatiḥ prajayā saṃvidānas trīṇi jyotīṃṣi sacate sa ṣoḍaśī / eṣa brahmā ya ṛtviya indro nāma śruto gaṇe pra te mahe vidathe śaṃsiṣaṃ harī / ya ṛtviyaḥ pra te vanve vanuṣo haryataṃ madam / indro nāma ghṛtaṃ na yo haribhiś cāru secate / śruto gaṇe ā tvā viśantu harivarpasaṃ gira iti sarveṣu grahaṇeṣu ṣoḍaśinam abhimantrayate
9.19.2	acchāvākacamasamukhyāṃś camasān unnayann ekasmai camasagaṇāya rājānam atirecayati
9.19.3	taiḥ pracarya ṣoḍaśinā pracarati
9.19.4	samayāviṣite sūrye hiraṇyena barhirbhyāṃ ca ṣoḍaśinaḥ stotram upākaroti
9.19.5	śvetam aśvaṃ purastād dhārayaty aruṇapiśaṅgaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ vā
9.19.6	hiraṇyaṃ sāṃpradāyaṃ stuvate
9.19.7	harivac chastram
9.19.8	upariṣṭāt stotriyānurūpābhyām othā moda iva made madā moda ivom atheti vyatyāsaṃ pratigṛṇāti
9.19.9	anuṣṭupsu siddhaḥ pratigaraḥ
9.19.10	śastraṃ pratigīrya graham ādatte camasāṃś camasādhvaryava ukthaśā yaja somānām iti saṃpreṣyati
9.20.1	indrādhipate 'dhipatis tvaṃ devānām asy adhipatiṃ mām āyuṣmantaṃ varcasvantaṃ manuṣyeṣu kurv iti ṣoḍaśinaṃ juhoti
9.20.2	indraś ca samrāḍ varuṇaś ca rājā tau te bhakṣaṃ cakratur agra etaṃ tayor anu bhakṣaṃ bhakṣayāmi vāg juṣāṇā somasya tṛpyastv iti grahasya bhakṣayati
9.20.3	ādityavadgaṇena camasānām
9.20.4	anuṣṭupcchandasa iti bhakṣamantraṃ saṃnamati
9.20.5	atirātreṇa brahmavarcaskāmaḥ
9.20.6	tasya ṣoḍaśinā kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
9.20.7	ekaviṃśatichadi sadaḥ
9.20.8	na kratukaraṇaṃ juhoti na droṇakalaśaṃ rarāṭīṃ vopaspṛśaty etad eva yajur vadan havirdhāne prapadyata etāvān kratukaraṇaḥ
9.20.9	sārasvatīṃ meṣīm atirātre caturthīṃ savanīyām ālabhate meṣam ity ekeṣām
9.20.10	ṣoḍaśinaś camasān unnayaṃs trayodaśabhyaś camasagaṇebhyo rājānam atirecayati
9.20.11	taiḥ pracarya rātriprayāyaiḥ pracarati
9.20.12	upayāmagṛhīto 'sīndrāya tvāpi śarvarāyeti mukhyaṃmukhyaṃ camasam unnayati
9.20.13	stutaśastre bhavataḥ
9.20.14	hotṛcamasamukhyān prathamān unnayati maitrāvaruṇacamasamukhyān dvitīyān brāhmaṇācchaṃsicamasamukhyāṃs tṛtīyān acchāvākacamasamukhyāṃś caturthān
9.20.15	sa prathamo rātriparyāyaḥ
9.20.16	evam vihito dvitīyas tṛtīyaś ca rātriparyāyaḥ
9.20.17	taiḥ pracaryāśvinasya pātrasaṃsādanaprabhṛtīni karmāṇi pratipadyata āśvinaṃ dvikapālaṃ nirvapati
9.20.18	tam āsādya
9.20.19	hotṛcamasamukhyān saṃdhicamasān unnayati
9.20.20	stutaśastre bhavataḥ
9.21.1	trivṛdrāthantaraṃ saṃdhistotram
9.21.2	āśvinaṃ śastram
9.21.3	udita āditya āśvinaṃ paridhāya hotṛcamasam adhvaryur ādatte puroḍāśaṃ pratiprasthātā ca
9.21.4	ādadate camasāṃś camasādhvaryavaḥ
9.21.5	aśvibhyāṃ tiroahniyānāṃ somānām anubrūhy aśvibhyāṃ tiroahniyān somān prasthitān preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati
9.21.6	saha somaiḥ puroḍāśaṃ pratiprasthātā sarvahutaṃ juhoti
9.21.7	paṅkticchandasa iti bhakṣamantraṃ saṃnamati
9.21.8	aptoryāmeṇa paśukāmaḥ
9.21.9	tasyātirātreṇa kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
9.21.10	saṃdhicamasān unnayaṃś caturbhyaś camasagaṇebhyo rājānam atirecayati
9.21.11	catvāraś camasagaṇāḥ satutaśastravanto hotur maitrāvaruṇasya brāhmaṇācchaṃsino 'cchāvākasya ca
9.21.12	teṣāṃ saṃdhicamasaiḥ pracaraṇakalpo vyākhyātaḥ
9.21.13	aticchandāś chandasa iti bhakṣamantraṃ saṃnamati
9.21.14	agnīd aupayajān aṅgārān āharety etatprabhṛtīni pāśukāni karmāṇi sarvāsu saṃsthāsu samānāni kriyanta ā prātaragnihotrāt
9.22.1	kratupaśava aikādaśināś ca vikalpante
9.22.2	teṣāṃ samavāye vibhavanti tantram aṅgāny avibhavanti pratyakṣārthāni pratisaṃskāram abhyāvartante
9.22.3	yathārtham ūhaḥ
9.22.4	yūpāhutiṃ hutvāgniṣṭhaprathamān ekādaśa yūpān upaśayapātnīvatau ca cchinnatti
9.22.5	ekayūpena vikalpate
9.22.6	daśarathākṣām ekādaśoparāṃ rajjuṃ mītvā tasyāś caturviṃśena bhāgena vediṃ vimimīte prakramasthānīyā bhavati
9.22.7	agniṣṭhaṃ dvābhyāṃ raśanābhyāṃ parivīyaikādaśinīraśanā agniṣṭhe parivīya vāsayati
9.22.8	śvo bhūta āśvinaṃ gṛhītvā yūpān saṃminoti
9.22.9	pūrvedyuḥ saṃmānam eke samāmananti
9.22.10	tantram abhrer ādānaṃ parilekhano 'bhyāvartate
9.22.11	dakṣiṇam agniṣṭhāt parilikhyottaraṃ parilikhaty evaṃ vyatyāsam udagapavargān
9.22.12	rathākṣamātrāṇi yūpāntarālāni bhavanti
9.22.13	vedisaṃmitāṃ vā minoti
9.22.14	samānajātīyenaikaikam anusameti kṛtsnam ekaikam āñjanaprabhṛti dviraśanam apavarjayati
9.22.15	pratiyūpaṃ svaravaḥ
9.22.16	uparasaṃmitāṃ muniyāt pitṛlokakāmasya
9.22.17	raśanasaṃmitāṃ madhye ca saṃmitāṃ manuṣyalokakāmasya
9.22.18	caṣālasaṃmitām indriyakāmasya
9.22.19	sarvān samān pratiṣṭhākāmasya
9.22.20	ye trayo madhyamās tān samān paśukāmasya vyatiṣajed itarān prajayaivainaṃ paśubhir vyatiṣajati
9.22.21	yaṃ kāmayeta pramāyukaḥ syād iti gartamitaṃ tasya minuyād uttarārdhyaṃ varṣiṣṭham athetarān hrasīyasaḥ
9.22.22	dakṣiṇārdhyaṃ varṣiṣṭhaṃ minuyāt svargakāmasyāthetarān hrasīyasohrasīyasaḥ
9.22.23	ārāgrām abhicaratas teṣām agniṣṭhaṃ varṣiṣṭham athetarān hrasīyasohrasīyasaḥ
9.22.24	samavasrāviṇīṃ vṛṣṭikāmasya teṣām agniṣṭhaṃ hrasiṣṭham athetarān varṣīyasovarṣīyasaḥ
9.22.25	vyatyastaṃ bhrātṛvyavato hrasvaṃ dīrghaṃ ca vyatiṣajet
9.22.26	yadi kāmayeta viṭkṣatrād ojīyasī syād iti ye 'gniṣṭhād dakṣiṇe tān varṣīyaso varṣīyaso minuyāt
9.22.27	yadi kāmayeta kṣatraṃ viśa ojīyaḥ syād iti ye 'gniṣṭhād uttare tān varṣīyasovarṣīyaso minuyāt
9.23.1	āyāmata uparāṇi samānāni syus tiryakto madhyāni raśanāś ca prathimnaś caṣālāni
9.23.2	upaśayam aṅktvā dvābhyāṃ raśanābhyāṃ parivīyāgreṇa dakṣiṇārdhyaṃ yūpaṃ nidadhyāt
9.23.3	yady abhicared idam aham amum āmuṣyāyaṇam indrasya vajreṇābhinidadhāmīti prāñcam upaśayaṃ nidadhyāt
9.23.4	paśukāla āgneyam asitaśīrṣam agniṣṭha upākaroti sārasvatīṃ meṣīm uttarataḥ saumyaṃ babhruṃ dakṣiṇata evaṃ vyatyāsaṃ dakṣiṇāpavargān pauṣṇaṃ śyāmaṃ śitipṛṣṭhaṃ bārhaspatyaṃ śilpaṃ vaiśvadevam aindram aruṇaṃ mārutaṃ kalmāṣam aindrāgnaṃ saṃhitam adhorāmaṃ sāvitraṃ vāruṇaṃ petvam uttamam
9.23.5	yadi kāmayeta yo 'vagataḥ so 'parudhyatāṃ yo 'paruddhaḥ so 'vagacchatv ity aindrasya loke vāruṇam ālabheta vāruṇasya loka aindraṃ ya evāvagataḥ so 'parudhyate yo 'paruddhaḥ so 'vagacchati
9.23.6	yadi kāmayeta prajā muhyeyur iti paśūn vyatiṣajed iti prajā eva mohayati
9.23.7	yad abhivāhato 'pāṃ vāruṇam ālabheta prajā varuṇo gṛhṇīyād dakṣiṇata udañcam ālabhate 'pavāhataḥ
9.23.8	āraṇyaṃ paśum ākhuṃ voṣaśaye nirdiśaty asau te paśus iti nirdiśed yaṃ dviṣyād yadi na dviṣyād ākhus te paśur iti brūyāt
9.23.9	sarveṣāṃ pratipaśu barhīṃṣi vapāśrapaṇyaḥ kumbhyo hṛdayaśūlāḥ plakṣaśākhāś ca
9.23.10	tantram agner haraṇam adhrigur uttamaḥ prayājas tathā pūrvaḥ parivapyo 'ntataḥ saṃjñaptahomo raśanānām udasanam uttaraḥ parivapyo vapāśrapaṇīnām anupraharaṇam abhihomo mārjanaṃ varadānaṃ ca
9.24.1	tasyatasyābhyāvartate manotā vā
9.24.2	sarveṣāṃ tryaṅgāṇi samavattaṃ ca
9.24.3	tasyatasyardharce vasāhomaṃ juhoti
9.24.4	sarveṣāṃ gudair upayaja upayajati
9.24.5	jāghanībhiś ca patnīḥ saṃyājayanti
9.24.6	anūbandhyāvapāyāṃ hutāyām agreṇa śālāmukhīyam adhonābhim acaṣālaṃ dviraśanaṃ pātnīvatasya yūpaṃ saṃmāya tasmiṃs tvāṣṭraṃ sāṇḍaṃ lomaśaṃ piṅgalaṃ bahurūpam upākaroti paryagnikṛtam utsṛjyājyena śeṣaṃ saṃsthāpayet
9.24.7	yadi kāpeyī paśvekādaśinī syād abhita āgneyam aindrau paśū bhavataḥ sārasvataḥ saumyaḥ pauṣṇo bārhaspatya ity uttarato vaiśvadevo mārutaḥ sāvitro vāruṇa iti dakṣiṇataḥ
9.24.8	tām etāṃ kāpeyā vidus tām atirātracarama ālabheta
9.24.9	sāhīneṣu liṅgasaṃyogāt
9.24.10	satrīyetarā bhavati
9.24.11	ukṣarṣabho vaśā vehad dhenur vatso 'naḍvān iti gonāmabhir gavyān paśūn pratīyāt
9.24.12	svair itarān
9.24.13	ekadevateṣv ananyadevatavyaveteṣu samānaḥ paśupuroḍāśo bhavati bhavati
10.1.1	agniṣṭomasya yājamānaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
10.1.2	purastād dīkṣābhyo rājānam āhārya pariveveṣṭi
10.1.3	tad dīkṣāsu nivartate
10.1.4	brāhmaṇān ārṣeyān ṛtvijaḥ ṣoḍaśaikaikaśo vṛṇīte
10.1.5	hotā maitrāvaruṇo 'cchāvāko grāvastuc ca hotāro 'dhvaryuḥ pratiprasthātā neṣṭonnetā cādhvaryavo brahmā brāhmaṇācchaṃsy āgnīdhraḥ potā ca brahmāṇa udgātā prastotā pratihartā subrahmaṇyaś codgātāraḥ
10.1.6	sadasyaḥ saptadaśaḥ
10.1.7	athartvijo vṛṇīte
10.1.8	agnir devo daivyo hotā sa me hotāstv ity upāṃśu daivyaṃ hotāraṃ vṛṇīte asau mānuṣas taṃ hotāraṃ vṛṇa ity uccair mānuṣam
10.1.9	evam itareṣūpāṃśu daivyaṃ vṛṇīta uccair mānuṣam
10.1.10	ādityo devo daviyo 'dhvaryuḥ sa me 'dhvaryur astv asau mānuṣas tam adhvaryuṃ vṛṇa ity adhvaryuṃ candramā devo daivyo brahmā sa me brahmāstv asau mānuṣas taṃ brahmāṇaṃ vṛṇa iti brahmāṇaṃ parjanyo devo daivya udgātā sa ma udgātāstv asau mānuṣas tam udgātāraṃ vṛṇa ity udgātāram ākāśo devo daivyaḥ sadasyaḥ sa me sadasyo 'stv asau mānuṣas taṃ sadasyaṃ vṛṇa iti sadasyam āpo devīr daivyā hotrāśaṃsinyas tā me hotrāśaṃsinyaḥ santv amī mānuṣās tān hotrāśaṃsinīr vṛṇa iti hotrakān raśmayo devā daivyāś camasādhvaryavas te me camasādhvaryavaḥsantv amī mānuṣās tān camasādhvaryūn vṛṇa iti camasādhvaryūn
10.2.1	api vā hotāram adhvaryuṃ brahmāṇam udgātāraṃ caitān eva vṛṇīte
10.2.2	atha kṣatriyaṃ devayajanaṃ yācate
10.2.3	sa ced dadāti devayajanavān bhūyā ity enam āha na ced yad ahaṃ devayajanaṃ veda tasmiṃs tvā vṛścānīty evam āha
10.2.4	athainam abhivyāhārayanti
10.2.5	vācam upāvadhīr vāk tvā hāsyatīti hotā prāṇam upāvadhīḥ prāṇas tvā hāsyatīty adhvaryur mana upāvadhīr manas tva hāsyatīti brahmā cakṣur upāvadhīś cakṣus tvā hāsyatīty udgātā śrotram upāvadhīḥ śrotraṃ tvā hāsyatīti hotrakā ātmānam upāvadhīr ātmā tvā hāsyatīti sadasyo 'ṅgāny upāvadhīr aṅgāni tvā hāsyantīti camasādhvaryavaḥ prajāpatim upāvadhīḥ prajāpatis tvā hāsyatīti yajamāno bhūtāny upāvadhīr bhūtāni tvā hāsyantīti sarve
10.2.6	athartvijo devayajanaṃ yācate
10.2.7	agnir me hotā sa me devayajanaṃ dadātv ity upāṃśu hotar devayajanaṃ me dehīty uccair mānuṣam
10.2.8	evam itareṣūpāṃśu devatānāmadheyam abhivyāharaty uccair mānuṣasya
10.2.9	ādityo me 'dhvaryuḥ sa me devayajanaṃ dadātv adhvaryo devayajanaṃ me dehīty adhvaryuṃ candramā me brahmā sa me devayajanaṃ dadātu brahman devayajanaṃ me dehīti brahmāṇaṃ parjanyo ma udgātā sa me devayajanaṃ dadātūdgātar devayajanaṃ me dehīty udgātāram ākāśo me sadasyaḥ sa me devayajanaṃ dadātu sadasya devayajanaṃ me dehīti sadasyam āpo me hotrāśaṃsinyas tā me devayajanaṃ dadatu hotrāśaṃsinyo me devayajanaṃ me datteti hotrakān raśmayo me camasādhvaryavas te me devayajanaṃ dadatu camasādhvaryavo devayajanaṃ me datteti camasādhvaryūn
10.3.1	yācitvaidam aganma devayajanaṃ pṛthivyā iti devayajanam adhyavasyati
10.3.2	yat samaṃ pratiṣṭhitam oṣadhivad anūṣaram abhaṅguram anupahitam aniriṇam avisragdāri
10.3.3	prācīnapravaṇam udīcīnapravaṇaṃ prāgudakpravaṇaṃ vā
10.3.4	yasmāt sthalāntaram abhito bhavati
10.3.5	na devayajanamātraṃ purastād atiśinaṣṭi
10.3.6	yāvān vā śamyāprāsaḥ
10.3.7	yāvat samaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ tad gataśrīr yajeteti nitye kāmye
10.3.8	atipravrakhye 'bhicaran yajeta guhākye 'bhiśasyamānaḥ
10.3.9	purohaviṣi devayajane yājayed iti brāhmaṇavyākhyātāni kāmyāni devayajanāni teṣāṃ yāthākāmī
10.3.10	aparāhṇe dīkṣate
10.3.11	yaḥ kāmayeta tapasvī syām iti sa pūrvāhṇe
10.3.12	yad asya yajñārthaṃ tan nirādiśya śeṣād bhuñjate 'nirādiśya vā tasya na bhuñjate prāg agnīṣomīyāt
10.3.13	svasty uttarāṇy aśīyeti sarvatra keśeṣūpyamāneṣu japati
10.3.14	kṛte nāpitakṛtya audumbareṇa dato dhāvate lohitam anāgamayan
10.3.15	hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā ity eṣā hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā vṛtraṃ bhitvā pracakramur hitvāvadyam āpaḥ / śataṃ pavitrā vitatā hy āsāṃ tābhir no devaḥ savitā punātu / āpo asmān mātaraḥ śudhantv iti ca śaṅkhini hrade hiraṇyam avadhāya sthāvarāsu snāti
10.3.16	yal lomaśam avakāśaṃ tīrthaṃ tasmin snāti kuṇḍe snātīty ekeṣām
10.3.17	ud ābhyaḥ śucir ā pūta emīti snātvodgāhate
10.3.18	upaspṛśyācamaya
10.4.1	dīkṣāsi tanūr asi tāṃ tvā śivāṃ syonāṃ paridhiṣīyeti kṣaumaṃ vāso 'hataṃ mahat paridhatte somasya tanūr asi tanuvaṃ me pāhīti ca
10.4.2	sūryasya vāso 'si nīvir nāmorjam asmāsu dhehīti tasya nīvim anuparikalpayate
10.4.3	ūrje tvety aśnāty ūrjam asmāsu dhehīti vā yad asya manasaḥ priyaṃ sarpirmiśraṃ dadhi madhu vābhyupasekam
10.4.4	āśito bhavati
10.4.5	kanīyaḥkanīyo 'ta ūrdhvaṃ vratayati
10.4.6	mahīnāṃ payo 'sīti darbhapuñjīlābhyāṃ gavyaṃ navanītaṃ samudyauti varcodhā asi varco mayi dhehīti tenābhyaṅkte mukham agre 'nulomam itarāṇy aṅgāni svabhyakto bhavati
10.4.7	vṛtrasya kanīnikāsīti traikakudenāñjanenāṅkte
10.4.8	tasminn avidyamāne yenaiva kenacit
10.4.9	satūlayā śareṣīkayā darbheṣīkayā vā darbhapuñjīlena vābhyantaram anidhāvayaṃs trir ekaikaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ pūrvam āṅkte
10.4.10	dvir vā savyam
10.4.11	dvir dakṣiṇaṃ sakṛt savyam ity ekeṣām
10.4.12	na punar niṣecayati
10.4.13	tasya te pavitrapate pavitreṇeti pāvyamāno japati citpatir mā punātu vākpatir mā punātu devo mā savitā punātv iti ca pavamānaḥ suvarjana iti caitam anuvākam
10.5.1	ā vo devāsa īmaha iti pūrveṇa dvāreṇa prāgvaṃśaṃ praviśañ japati
10.5.2	vidyud asīty apa upaspṛśyāpareṇāhavanīyaṃ dakṣiṇātikramya dakṣiṇata upaviśati
10.5.3	tasyaiṣa eva saṃcara ā sutyāyāḥ
10.5.4	indrāgnī dyāvāpṛthivī ity āhavanīyam abhimantrayate
10.5.5	antarvedi kṛṣṇājinasyāstīrṇasyarksāmayoḥ śilpe stha iti śuklakṛṣṇe rājī ālabhate
10.5.6	suśarmāsīti dakṣiṇato bhasatta ārohatīmāṃ dhiyaṃ śikṣamāṇasya deveti ca sutrāmāṇaṃ pṛthivīṃ dyām anehasam iti cemāṃ su nāvam āruham iti vā
10.5.7	āhaṃ dīkṣām aruham ṛtasya patnīṃ gāyatreṇa chandasā brahmaṇā cartaṃ satye 'dhāyi satyam ṛte 'dhāyy ṛtaṃ ca me satyaṃ cābhūtāṃ jyotir abhūvaṃ suvar agamaṃ suvargaṃ lokaṃ nākasya pṛṣṭhaṃ bradhnasya viṣṭapam agamam ity āruhya japati
10.5.8	viṣṇoḥ śarmāsīti kṛṣṇājinena dakṣiṇam aṃsaṃ pracchādayati
10.5.9	nakṣatrāṇāṃ mātīkāśāt pāhīti vāsasā śiraḥ praveṣṭayate
10.5.10	prattayā kṛṣṇaviṣāṇayā kṛṣyai tvā susasyāyā iti veder loṣṭam uddhanti
10.5.11	supippalābhyas tvauṣadhībhya iti śirasi kaṇḍūyate
10.5.12	viṣāṇe viṣyaitaṃ granthiṃ yad asya gulphidaṃ hṛdi mano yad asya gulphidam ity avaśiṣṭāny aṅgāni
10.5.13	sūpasthā devo vanaspatir ūrdhvo mā pāhy odṛca iti daṇḍaṃ pratigṛhṇāti
10.6.1	agnir dīkṣitaḥ pṛthivī dīkṣā tayāgnir dīkṣayā dīkṣito yayāgnir dīkṣayā dīkṣitaḥ sā mā dīkṣā dīkṣayatu tayā dīkṣayā dīkṣe
10.6.2	vāyur dīkṣito 'ntarikṣaṃ dīkṣā tayā vāyurdīkṣayā dīkṣito yayā vāyurdīkṣayā dīkṣitaḥ sā mā dīkṣā dīkṣāyatu tayā dīkṣayā dīkṣe
10.6.3	ādityo dīkṣito dyaur dīkṣā tayādityo dīkṣayā dīkṣito yayādityo dīkṣayā dīkṣitaḥ sā mā dīkṣā dīkṣayatu tayā dīkṣayā dīkṣe
10.6.4	candramā dīkṣito nakṣatrāṇi dīkṣā tayā candramā dīkṣayā dīkṣito yayā candramā dīkṣayā dīkṣitaḥ sā mā dīkṣā dīkṣayatu tayā dīkṣayā dīkṣe
10.6.5	varuṇo rājā dīkṣita āpo dīkṣā tayā varuṇo rājā dīkṣayā dīkṣito yayā varuṇo rājā dīkṣayā dīkṣitaḥ sā mā dīkṣā dīkṣayatu tayā dīkṣayā dīkṣe
10.6.6	somo rājā dīkṣita oṣadhayo dīkṣā tayā somo rājā dīkṣayā dīkṣito yayā somo rājā dīkṣayā dīkṣitaḥ sā mā dīkṣā dīkṣayatu tayā dīkṣayā dīkṣe
10.6.7	prāṇo dīkṣito vāg dīkṣā tayā prāṇo dīkṣayā dīkṣito yayā prāṇo dīkṣayā dīkṣitaḥ sā mā dīkṣā dīkṣayatu tayā dīkṣayā dīkṣe
10.6.8	prajāpatir dīkṣito mano dīkṣā tayā prajāpatir dīkṣayā dīkṣito yayā prajāpatir dīkṣayā dīkṣitaḥ sā mā dīkṣā dīkṣayatu tayā dīkṣayā dīkṣe
10.6.9	vācā me vāg dīkṣatām agnaye samaṣṭavā u prāṇena me prāṇo dīkṣatāṃ vāyave samaṣṭavā u cakṣuṣā me cakṣur dīkṣatāṃ sūryāya samaṣṭavā u manasā me mano dīkṣatāṃ prajāpataye samaṣṭavā u dyauś ca pṛthivī cāhaś ca rātriś ca kṛṣiś ca vṛṣṭiś ca tviṣiś cāpacitiś cāpaś cauṣadhayaś cork ca sūnṛtā ca tā mā dīkṣamāṇam anu dīkṣantāṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ suvaḥ satyaṃ ma ātmā śraddhā me kṣitis tapo me pratiṣṭhā śraddhā satyaṃ gṛhapatir iti keśinīṃ dīkṣāṃ japitvā
10.6.10	svāhā yajñaṃ manaseti dve aṅgulī nirbhujati svāhā dyāvāpṛthivībhyām iti dve svāhoror antarikṣād iti dve svāhā yajñaṃ vātād ārabha iti muṣṭī kṛtvaiṣṭrīḥ stheti catasro 'ṅgulīrutsṛjati tābhiryathāsukhaṃ carati vācaṃ ca yacchati
10.6.11	yadi pramatto vyāhared vaiṣṇavīm āgnāvaiṣṇavīṃ sārasvatīṃ bārhaspatyām ity anūcya vyāhṛtīś ca punar vācaṃ yacchati
10.6.12	nānṛtaṃ vadati
10.6.13	na māṃsam aśnāti
10.6.14	na striyam upaiti
10.6.15	nopary āste
10.6.16	na niṣṭhīvate
10.6.17	na dato dhavate
10.6.18	nāviṣkurute
10.6.19	nānatau smayetāpigṛhya smayeta
10.6.20	abaddhaṃ mana ity amedhyaṃ dṛṣṭvā japati
10.6.21	undatīr balaṃ dhattety abhivṛṣyamāṇo japati
10.6.22	dakṣiṇena vihāraṃ dīkṣitāgāre viharati
10.7.1	nānyatra kṛṣṇājinād āste śete vā
10.7.2	nainam anyatra dīkṣitavimitāt sūryo 'bhinimrocen nābhyudiyāt
10.7.3	naktam eva mūtrapurīṣe kuryād divā vā chāyāyām
10.7.4	mūtraṃ cikīrṣann iyaṃ te yajñiyā tanūr iti viṣāṇayā loṣṭaṃ kiṃcid vopahatya tad ādāyāpo muñcāmi na prajām aṃhomucaḥ svāhākṛtāḥ pṛthivīm āviśateti prasrāvayaty apa upaspṛśyācamya pṛthivyāṃ saṃbhaveti tat pratinidadhāti pṛthivyāḥ saṃbhaveti vā
10.7.5	nainaṃ śūdro 'nupraviśati

10.7.11	laukikīṃ vācaṃ vadan nāmadheyeṣu vicakṣaṇaṃ canasitaṃ cāntato dadhāti

10.8.1	yāḥ paśūnām ṛṣabhe vācas tāḥ sūryo agre śukro agre tāḥ prahiṇyo yathābhāgaṃ vo atra śivā nastāḥ punar āyantu vāca ity udyantam ādityam upatiṣṭhate
10.8.2	udita āditye vrataṃ kṛṇuteti saṃpreṣyati
10.8.3	evam astamite
10.8.4	madhyaṃdine madhyarātre ca vratayati
10.8.5	nainam adīkṣitā vratayantaṃ paśyanti
10.8.6	payo brāhmaṇasya yavāgū rājanyasyāmikṣā vaiśyasya
10.8.7	ekadugdhaṃ yavāgūṃ vaikadugdhe
10.8.8	yadi dadhīyād etad asmai dadhi kuryuḥ
10.8.9	yadyan nīyād dhānā asmā anvāvapeyuḥ saktūn vāsmā anvāvapeyur ghṛtaṃ vāsmā anvāvapeyuḥ
10.8.10	api vāgnihotrahaviṣām ekaṃ vratayet

10.8.12	sarveṣām upasatsu stanakalpāḥ
10.8.13	uruvyacā asi janadhāḥ svabhakṣo mā pāhīti kaṃsaṃ vratapradānam anumantrayate
10.8.14	daivīṃ dhiyaṃ manāmaha iti hastāv avanenikte
10.8.15	ye devā manojātā manoyuja iti vratayati
10.8.16	śivāḥ pītā bhavatha yajñiyāso yūyam āpo 'smākaṃ yonāv udare suśevāḥ / irāvatīḥ pururūpā anāgasaḥ śivā no bhavatha pītaya ity udakaṃ pibati yadāpītaṃ bhavati yadā pipāsati
10.8.17	dakṣiṇenāhavanīyaṃ prāṅ śete
10.8.18	dakṣiṇena pārśvena
10.8.19	nottānaḥ śayīta
10.8.20	nāgneḥ parāṅ paryāvarteta
10.8.21	agne tvaṃ su jāgṛhīti svapsyann āhavanīyam upatiṣṭhate
10.8.22	viśve devā abhi mām āvavṛtrann ity upaparyāvartate yady apaparyāvarteta
10.8.23	punar manaḥ punar āyur ma āgāt punaś cakṣuḥ punaḥ śrotraṃ ma āgāt punaḥ prāṇaḥ punar ākūtaṃ ma āgāt punaś cittaṃ punar ādhītaṃ ma āgād vaiśvānaro me 'dabdhas tanūpā antas tiṣṭhatu duritāni viśvā / vaiśvānaro viśvabhṛd viśvaśaṃbhūr avabādhatāṃ duritāni viśvā sa no divā sa riṣaḥ pātu naktaṃ tvam agne vratapā asīti pratibudhya japati
10.8.24	tvam agne vratapā asīty anubrūyād yadyad īkṣitavādaṃ vadet
10.8.25	muṣṭī vācaṃ ca visarjayitvā
10.8.26	dīkṣaṇīyāprabhṛtīyaṃ vṛttiḥ
10.8.27	daṇḍān na cchidyate na pratimucya kṛṣṇājinaṃ caṃkramyate kṛṣṇaviṣāṇayā kaṇḍūyate 'pigṛhya smayata ity upayogaprabhṛtīny etāni vratāni bhavanti
10.9.1	pūṣā sanyeti sanīhārān saṃśāsti
10.9.2	dvādaśāhaṃ bhikṣācaryaṃ caraty aparimite dīkṣākalpe parimite yāthākāmī
10.9.3	hiraṇyaṃ vāso gāmaśvaṃ chāgaṃ meṣaṃ ca yāvat parimitā gāva ekaikam itareṣāṃ jātīnām
10.9.4	tāni pratigṛhṇāti candram asīty etair yathārūpam
10.9.5	devaḥ saviteti sarvatrānuṣajati
10.9.6	vāyave tveti tāsāṃ yā naśyet tām anudiśet
10.9.7	varuṇāya tvety apsu magnām
10.9.8	nirṛtyai tvety avasannām
10.9.9	rudrāya tveti sarpadaṣṭāṃ marudbhyas tveti hrādunihatām aśanihatāṃ vendrāya tveti meṣkahatāṃ yamāya tveti mahādevahatāṃ mṛtyave tvety avijñātena mṛtyunā
10.9.10	anudiṣṭām adhigamya yajamāno goṣu na cārayet
10.9.11	yadi prayāyāt pṛthag araṇīṣv agnīn samāropya rathena prayāti
10.9.12	rathe 'vidyamāne rathāṅgena saha
10.9.13	yady apo nāvyās taraty araṇī rathaṃ cādhāya saha tarati
10.9.14	yady apo 'nāvyā rathena tarati harati caināḥ
10.9.15	yady avagāheta devīr āpa ity avagāheta
10.9.16	acchinnaṃ tantuṃ pṛthivyā anugeṣam apāṃ setur asīti loṣṭaṃ vimṛdgann ā pārād gantos tarati
10.9.17	pṛthivyāḥ saṃbhaveti
10.10.1	sikatā loṣṭān vā madhye tīrayoś ca nyasyati pṛthivyā saṃbhaveti vā
10.10.2	atra devayajanādhyavasānam eke samāmananti
10.10.3	prāgvaṃśasya madhyamaṃ sthūṇārājam ālabhyainaṃ mantraṃ japati
10.10.4	ekarātraṃ dīkṣito rājānaṃ krīṇāti dvyahe tryahe caturahe 'parimite vā
10.10.5	prattaṃ padaṃ tote rāya iti patnyai prayacchati tava te rāya iti vā
10.10.6	krīyamāṇasya rājño dakṣiṇata āste
10.10.7	krīte some maitrāvaruṇāya daṇḍaṃ prayacchati
10.10.8	śvaḥ sutyāyāṃ vā kriyamāṇāyām
10.10.9	vayaḥ suparṇās iti pratyaporṇute śiro 'gre 'nupūrvam itarāṇy aṅgāni
10.10.10	mitro na ehi sumitradhā ity ūrāv āsannaṃ rājānamupasvaja upaiva gṛhṇīte
10.10.11	ud āyuṣety uttiṣṭhati
10.10.12	urv antarikṣam iti gacchati
10.10.13	śakaṭaṃ prāpyādhvaryave rājānaṃ pradadāti
10.10.14	namo mitrasya varuṇasya cakṣasa iti prāgvaṃśam ohyamānaṃ pratīkṣate
10.10.15	anu me dīkṣāṃ dīkṣāpatir manyatām iti tānūnapraṃ samavamṛśati
10.10.16	tantriṣu vrateṣu pratipanno bhakṣayati yad adhvaryur nāvajighrati
10.10.17	agne vratapata ity avāntaradīkṣām upaiti
10.10.18	saṃtarāṃ mekhalāṃ samāyacchate saṃtarāṃ muṣṭī kurute taptavrato bhavati madantībhir udakārthān kurute
10.11.1	vyākhyātaṃ pāṇiprakṣālanam āpyāyanaṃ nihnavanaṃ ca
10.11.2	yā te agne rudriyā tanūr iti vratayati
10.11.3	daikṣam etad ahar vrataparimāṇaṃ bhavati
10.11.4	aupasado 'ta ūrdhvaṃ vratakalpaḥ
10.11.5	catuḥstanam etāṃ rātriṃ vrataṃ vratayati tristanaṃ madhyame 'hani dvistanaṃ rātrāv ekastanam uttame 'hani
10.11.6	ārāgrām avāntaradīkṣām upeyād iti brāhmaṇavyākhyātāni kāmyāni vrataparimāṇāni teṣāṃ yāthākāmī
10.11.7	pra tad viṣṇuḥ stavate vīryāyeti saṃmitāddhavirdhānāt prāg upaniṣkramya tair eva mantrair yathānyuptaṃ dhiṣṇiyān upatiṣṭhate
10.11.8	samrāḍ asi kṛśānur ity āhavanīyaṃ pariṣadyo 'si pavamāna iti yatra bahiṣpavamānena stuvate pratakvāsi nabhasvān iti cātvālam asaṃmṛṣṭo 'si havyasūda iti paśuśrapaṇam ṛtadhāmāsi suvarjyotir ity audumbarīṃ brahmajyotir asi suvardhāmeti brahmasadanam ajo 'sy ekapād iti prājihitaṃ gārhapatyam ahir asi budhniya iti śālāmukhīyaṃ kavyo 'si kavyavāhana iti dakṣiṇāgniṃ samūhyo 'si viśvavyacā ity utkaraṃ samudro 'si viśvabharā iti sadaḥ sadasyo 'si malimluca iti sadasyāyatanaṃ raudram anīkaṃ sarvatrānuṣajati
10.12.1	yatra havirdhāne brahmā rājānaṃ prapādayati tasmin kāle pūrveṇa dvāreṇa havirdhāne praviśyaiṣa vo deva savitaḥ soma iti śakaṭe rājānam āsannam abhimantrayate
10.12.2	idam ahaṃ manuṣyo manuṣyān iti pradakṣiṇam āvartate
10.12.3	namo devebhya iti prācīnam añjaliṃ karoti svadhā pitṛbhya iti dakṣiṇā
10.12.4	idam ahaṃ nir varuṇasya pāśād ity upaniṣkrāmati
10.12.5	suvar abhivikhyeṣam iti sarvaṃ yajñam anuvīkṣate vaiśvānaraṃ jyotir ity āhavanīyaṃ parekṣate
10.12.6	agne vratapata ity avāntaradīkṣāṃ visṛjate
10.12.7	vitarāṃ mekhalāṃ samāyacchate vitarāṃ muṣṭī kurute
10.12.8	svāhā yajñaṃ vāci vāte visṛja iti muṣṭī vācaṃ ca visarjayitvā yathāsukham ata ūrdhvaṃ hastābhyāṃ carati
10.12.9	vartate 'nyā dīkṣitavṛttiḥ
10.12.10	jāgarty etāṃ rātrim
10.12.11	na vrataṃ bhavati daikṣo 'ta ūrdhvaṃ vratakalpaḥ
10.12.12	saptahotrā grāvasv āsannaṃ rājānam abhimṛśati
10.12.13	yatra havirdhānam apaḥ prapādayīta tā anu prapadyate yaśa enam upanāmukaṃ bhavati
10.12.14	dvādaśa dhenūḥ paṣṭhauhīr vā garbhiṇīḥ kṛttyadhīvāsaṃ cāṃśāv adhvaryave dadāty evam adābhye
10.12.15	dhruve gṛhīte na mūtraṃ karoty āvanayanāt
10.12.16	vasvyai hiṃ kuru tasya prastuhi tasyai me 'varuddhyā iti purastād bahiṣpavamānād vyāhṛtīr daśahotāraṃ ca japati
10.12.17	śyeno 'si gāyatrachandā anu tvārabhe svasti mā saṃpārayeti
10.13.1	stūyamānam anvārabhate
10.13.2	madhyamāyāṃ stotrīyāyāṃ vā
10.13.3	stutasya stutam asīti sarvāṇi stotrāṇi stutaṃ stutam anumantrayate
10.13.4	śastrasya śastram asīti sarvāṇi śastrāṇi
10.13.5	indriyāvanto vanāmaha iti sarvatrānuṣajati
10.13.6	bhūr asi śreṣṭho raśmīnām ity aindravāyave hūyamāna ādityam upatiṣṭhate
10.13.7	yo na indravāyū ity aindravāyave hute 'ṅguṣṭham avabādheta yadi śreyasā spardhetāṅguṣṭhenāṅgulīṃ yadi pāpīyasā
10.13.8	yo no mitrāvaruṇāv iti maitrāvaruṇe yo no 'śvināv ity āśvine
10.13.9	acchinnasya te rayipate suvīryasyendreṇa sayujo vayam iti śukraṃ hūyamānam anvārabhate
10.13.10	yatrāsmai camasam āharati taṃ bhakṣayati
10.13.11	yathetare camasāḥ
10.13.12	gṛhapate yajety ucyamāne hotar etad yajeti saṃpreṣyati svayaṃ vā niṣadya yajati
10.13.13	jyotiṣe hiṃ kuru tasyai prastuhi tasyai me 'varuddhyā iti purastād ājyānām ekaikasya stotrasya vyāhṛtīś caturhotāraṃ pañcahotāraṃ ca japati
10.13.14	iḍāyai hiṃ kuru tasyai prastuhi tasyai me 'varuddhyā iti purastān mādhyaṃdināt pavamānād vyāhṛtīś caturhotāraṃ pañcahotāraṃ ca japati
10.13.15	suparṇo 'si triṣṭupcchandā anu tvā rabhe svasti mā saṃpārayeti stūyamānam anvārabhate
10.14.1	vyākhyātaṃ śukrasyānvārambhaṇam
10.14.2	sanneṣu nārāśaṃseṣu dakṣiṇena vedim avasthitā dakṣiṇā dadāti
10.14.3	gavāṃ saptaikaviṃśatiś caturviṃśatiḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ śataṃ sahasraṃ dvādaśaśataṃ sarvavedasam aparimitā vā
10.14.4	manthaudanatilamāṣā hiraṇyaṃ vāso 'virajā ca niyuktāny etāni bhavanti
10.14.5	ano ratho 'dhīvāso 'śvaḥ puruṣo hastī vāniyuktāni
10.14.6	tā rūpeṇa vo rūpam abhyaimīti hiraṇyam ājyaṃ cādāyābhyeti
10.14.7	tutho vo viśvavedā vibhajatv iti madhyam avakramya vibhajati
10.14.8	dvādaśadvādaśa madhyataḥkāribhyaḥ ṣaṭṣaḍ ardhibhyaś catasraścatasras tṛtīyibhyas tisrastisraḥ pādibhyaḥ
10.14.9	evaṃ śeṣam
10.14.10	hotādhvaryur brahmodgātā ca madhyataḥkāriṇaḥ
10.14.11	maitrāvaruṇaḥ pratiprasthātā brāhmaṇācchaṃsī prastotā cārdhino 'cchāvāko neṣṭāgnīdhraḥ pratihartā ca tṛtīyinaḥ śeṣāḥ pādinaḥ
10.14.12	etat te agne rādha aiti somacyutam iti vibhaktā ānayati
10.14.13	agreṇa prāgvaṃśam apareṇa sado dakṣiṇenāgnīdhrīyam antareṇa cātvālotkarāv udīcīr utsṛjati
10.14.14	ṛtasya pathā preta candradakṣiṇā iti gacchantīr anumantrayate
10.14.15	brāhmaṇam adya rādhyāsam ṛṣim ārṣeyam iti hiraṇyaṃ dakṣiṇābhāgaṃ cādāyāgnīdhram abhyeti
10.14.16	etenaiva mantreṇa hiraṇyaṃ dakṣiṇābhāgaṃ cāgnīdhre dadāti
10.14.17	vi suvaḥ paśya vy antarikṣam iti sadaḥ prekṣate
10.14.18	asmaddātrā devatrā gacchateti dakṣiṇāḥ
10.14.19	pūrveṇa dvāreṇa sadaḥ praviśya
10.15.1	ātreyāya hiraṇyam uttamaṃ dadāti tenaiva mantreṇa yenāgnīdhre
10.15.2	tasminn avidyamāne ya ārṣeyo 'nūcāno 'nūcānaputras tasmai tāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadyāt
10.15.3	athartvigbhyo dakṣiṇābhāgān brahman manas te dadāmi tad anena niṣkrīṇāmīti brahmaṇe brahmasadana āsīnāyedaṃ dadāmīti yad dāsyan bhavati tad anudiśati brahmaṇe
10.15.4	evam itarebhyaḥ
10.15.5	hotar vācaṃ te dadāmi tam anena niṣkrīṇāmīti hotre hotṛṣadana āsīnāya
10.15.6	adhvaryo prāṇaṃ te dadāmi tam anena niṣkrīṇāmīty adhvaryave havirdhāna āsīnāya
10.15.7	udgātaś cakṣus te dadāmi tad anena niṣkrīṇāmīty udgātra audumbaryām āsīnāya
10.15.8	hotrakāḥ śrotraṃ vo dadāmi tad anena niṣkrīṇāmīti hotrakebhyo 'ntaḥsadasaṃ yathādhiṣṇiyamā sīnebhyaḥ
10.15.9	pratiprasthātre ca havirdhāna āsīnāya
10.15.10	yathāśraddhaṃ sadasyāya camasādhvaryubhyaḥ prasarpakebhyaś ca dadāti
10.15.11	sadasyātmānaṃ te dadāmi tam anena niṣkrīṇāmīti sadasyāyāntaḥsadasaṃ dakṣiṇārdha āsīnāya
10.15.12	camasādhvaryavo 'ṅgāni vo dadāmi tāny anena niṣkrīṇāmīti camasādhvaryubhyo havirdhāna āsīnebhyaḥ
10.15.13	prasarpakā lomāni vo dadāmi tāny anena niṣkrīṇāmīti prasarpakebhyo 'ntaḥsadasaṃ dakṣiṇārdha āsīnebhyaḥ
10.15.14	idaṃ dadāmīti sarvatrānuṣajati
10.15.15	na bhīto dadāti
10.15.16	na yācamānāya
10.15.17	na kaṇvakāśyapebhyaḥ
10.15.18	na vīṇāgāthibhyaḥ
10.15.19	nānṛtvije
10.15.20	na jñātaye
10.15.21	nāprasṛptāya
10.15.22	nāśrotriyāya
10.15.23	nābrāhmaṇāya
10.15.24	vedavide dadyāt
10.15.25	yām anyo dīyamānāṃ pratyācakṣīta yaṃ dviṣyāt tasmai tāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadyāt
10.15.26	sa hānyayā pratigṛhṇīyāt
10.15.27	antataḥ pratihartre dadāty ātreyāya vā
10.15.28	na marutvatīyayor anūktā dadyāt
10.15.29	yadi dadyād anūbandhyāvapāyāṃ hutāyāṃ dadyād udavasānīyāyāṃ veṣṭhau
10.16.1	nītāsu dakṣiṇāsu hariṇasya raghuṣyato 'dhiśīrṣāṇi bheṣajaṃ sakṣetriyaṃ viṣāṇayā viṣūcīnam anīnaśad ity unmucya kṛṣṇaviṣāṇām anu tvā hariṇo mṛgaḥ padbhiś caturbhir akramīn māhir bhūmnā pṛdākur iti cātvāle prāsyati
10.16.2	rathaṃtare varaṃ dadāti
10.16.3	vāmedevye varaṃ dadāti
10.16.4	niṣkevalye varaṃ dadāti
10.16.5	ādityagrahaṃ hūyamānam anvārabhate
10.16.6	āyuṣe hiṃ kuru tasyai prastuhi tasyai me 'varuddhyā iti purastād ārbhavāt pavamānād vyāhṛtīḥ pañcahotāraṃ ca japati
10.16.7	saghāsi jagatīchandā anu tvārabhe svasti mā saṃpārayeti stūyamānam anvārabhate
10.16.8	yatra svaṃ camasaṃ nyante trīn puroḍāśaśakalān dakṣiṇata upāsyati
10.16.9	tat kṛtvā prācīnāvītaṃ kṛtvā ṣaḍḍhotāraṃ vyākhyāya dānaprabhṛtīn pratyāyanāntān piṇḍapitṛyajñamantrāñ japati
10.16.10	yajñāyajñiye varaṃ dadāti
10.16.11	purastād agniṣṭomastotrād vyāhṛtīḥ saptahotāraṃ ca japati
10.16.12	subhūr asi śreṣṭho raśmīnāṃ priyo devānāṃ saṃsādhanīyaḥ / taṃ svā subho devā abhisaṃviśantv iṣo 'si tveṣo 'si nṛmṇo 'si yaho 'si vrato 'si svo 'si cāraṇo 'si śūdro 'sy āryo 'si tasya ta iṣasya tveṣasya nṛmṇasya yahvasya vratasya svasya cāraṇasya śūdrasya cāryasya ca bhukṣiṣīya yathā tvaṃ sūryo 'si viśvadarśata evam ahaṃ viśvadarśato bhūyāsam ity agniṣṭomaṃ niṣpādyādityam upatiṣṭhate yady astamitaḥ syād āhavanīyam evādityopasthānenopatiṣṭhate
10.17.1	vyākhyāto hāriyojanaḥ
10.17.2	dadhidrapsaḥ
10.17.3	apsuṣomaḥ
10.17.4	mindayopasthānam
10.17.5	śakalābhyādhānam
10.17.6	sakhyavisarjanaṃ ca
10.17.7	huteṣu samiṣṭayajuḥṣu agninā devena pṛtanā jayāmīti jāgatān viṣṇukramān krāmati
10.17.8	upasṛjan dharuṇaṃ mātre mātaraṃ dharuṇo dhayan / rāyaspoṣam iṣam ūrjam asmāsu dīdharad ity upaniṣkrāmann audumbarīm utkhidati
10.17.9	ava te heḍo varuṇety unmucya kṛṣṇājinaṃ cātvāle prāsyati
10.17.10	ud u tyaṃ citram iti dvābhyām ādityam upatiṣṭhate yady astamitaḥ syād āhavanīyam evādityopasthānenopatiṣṭhate
10.17.11	vyākhyātaṃ nidhanopāyanam
10.17.12	sumitriyā ca mārjanam
10.17.13	indriyāj jyaiṣṭhyāc chraiṣṭhyān mā yoṣam ity unmucya kṛṣṇājinam abhyukṣya nidadhāti yadi purastād aprāstaṃ bhavati
10.17.14	sumitrā na ity abhipragāhyānupamajjantau sahaśiraskau snāto 'nyonyasya pṛṣṭhaṃ prakṣālayataḥ pratīpam āplavamānau gāhete
10.17.15	vi te muñcāmi raśanā iti mekhalāṃ yajamāno visraṃsayate
10.17.16	imaṃ viṣyāmīti yoktrapāśaṃ patnī
10.17.17	mekhalāṃ yoktraṃ jālaṃ dīkṣitavasane ca praplāvya somopanahanaṃ yajamānaḥ paridhatte somapariśrayaṇaṃ patnī
10.17.18	tāv ahatavāsasāv uditaḥ
10.17.19	te udayanīyāyām adhvaryave dattaḥ
10.18.1	vyākhyātam unnayanam
10.18.2	mahīyā
10.18.3	samidabhyādhānam
10.18.4	upasthānaṃ ca
10.18.5	apareṇa śālāmukhīyam upaviśya juhvāṃ pañcagṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā kṛṣṇājinam upastha ādhāya mayīndra indriyaṃ jyaiṣṭhyaṃ śraiṣṭhyaṃ dadhātv iti juhoti
10.18.6	kṛṣṇājinaṃ pra vāpayate
10.18.7	srugavadhānaṃ vā kurute
10.18.8	haviṣo vātha peṣaṇam
10.18.9	punardīkṣāyā evainan nidhatte
10.18.10	putrāya vainad brahmacāriṇe vā dadyāt
10.18.11	yadi purastādaprāstaṃ bhavati
10.18.12	udayanīyāyāṃ vratam upaiti
10.18.13	anūbandhyāvapāyāṃ hutāyāṃ dakṣiṇasyāṃ vediśroṇyāṃ pariśrite yajamānasya keśaśmaśrūṇi vāpayate 'tra dadāti yad dāsyan bhavati
10.18.14	vyākhyātaḥ svaruhṛdayaśūlo yūpopasthānaṃ ca
10.18.15	mithunau gāvau maitrāvaruṇyām āmikṣāyāṃ dadāti
10.18.16	saktuhome hūyamāne 'yaṃ no nabhasā pura ity agnim upatiṣṭhate
10.18.17	sa tvaṃ no nabhasaspata iti vāyuṃ deva saṃsphānety ādityam
10.18.18	anaḍvāham anaḍuho vā hiraṇyam audavasānīyāyāṃ dadāti
10.18.19	yathāśakti pūrṇāhutau
10.18.20	apavṛtte ṣoḍaśinaḥ stotre tam evāśvam aśvatarīṃ vā dakṣiṇāṃ dadāti
10.19.1	dakṣiṇāṃ pratigrahīṣyan pratigṛhya vā saptadaśakṛtvo 'pāniti
10.19.2	barhiṣā pratīyād gāṃ vāśvaṃ vā
10.19.3	annena puruṣam
10.19.4	gandhena ca priyodyena ca talpam
10.19.5	barhiḥ pratyuttiṣṭhati barhir vai dakṣiṇāyāḥ priyaṃ dhāma priyo dakṣiṇāyā bhavaty enaṃ dakṣiṇāgacchati
10.19.6	devā vai varuṇam ayājayan sa yasyaiyasyai devatāyai dakṣiṇām anayat tām avlīnāt te 'bruvan vyāvṛtya pratigṛhṇāma tathā no dakṣiṇā na vleṣyatīti te vyāvṛtya pratyagṛhṇan tato vai tān dakṣiṇā nāvlīnād ya evaṃ vidvān vyāvṛtya dakṣiṇāṃ pratigṛhṇāti nainaṃ dakṣiṇā vlīnātīti
10.19.7	vyāvṛtya pratigrahaṇam
10.19.8	tān trīṇāṃ dakṣiṇānāṃ darśayati
10.20.1	devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ pratigṛhṇāmi rājā tvā varuṇo nayatu devi dakṣiṇe 'gnaye hiraṇyaṃ tenāmṛtatvam aśyāṃ vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyam astu pratigrahītre ka idaṃ kasmā adāt kāmaḥ kāmāya kāmo dātā kāmaḥ pratigrahītā kāmaṃ samudram āviśa kāmena tvā pratigṛhṇāmi kāmaitat ta eṣā te kāma dakṣiṇottānas tvāṅgīrasaḥ pratigṛhṇātu somāya vāso gnās tvākṛntann apaso 'tanvata varūtrayo 'vayann avadhiyo apṛñcata rudrāya gāṃ varuṇāyāśvaṃ prajāpataye puruṣaṃ manave talpaṃ tvaṣṭre 'jāṃ pūṣṇe 'viṃ nirṛtyā aśvataragardabhau himavato hastinaṃ gandharvāpsarābhyaḥ sragalaṃkaraṇe viśvebhyo devebhyo dhānyaṃ vāce 'nnaṃ brahmaṇa odanaṃ samudrāyāpa uttānāyāṅgīrasāyāno vaiśvānarāya rathaṃ vaiśvānaraḥ pratnathā nākam āruhad divaḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhandamānaḥ sumanmabhiḥ sa pūrvavaj janayaj jantave dhanaṃ samānam ajmā pariyāti jāgṛvir iti vaiśvānaryarcā rathaṃ pratigṛhṇāti
10.20.2	sarveṣāṃ sāvitram ekaikasyādito dadhāti tenāmṛtatvam aśyām ity anuṣaṅgam antataḥ
10.21.1	saṃvatsaraṃ caturṇām eko nāśnīyād iti caturhotṝṇām upayogavrataṃ bhavati
10.21.2	yaḥ kāmayeta bahu syāṃ prajāyeteti so 'raṇyaṃ paretya darbhastambe daśahotāram ūnayā pūrṇayā vā srucā juhuyāt
10.21.3	yaḥ prajayā paśubhir naiva prabhaved varāsiṃ paridhāya taptaṃ piban dvādaśa rātrīr adhaḥ śayīta dvādaśyāṃ prātaḥ prāṅ udetya prāṇyāpānyāpraṇan daśahotāraṃ vyākhyendraṃ gaccha svāhety apānyāt
10.21.4	devānāṃ patnībhiḥ putrakāmo yajeta saṃvatsaram
10.21.5	caturbhir yajurbhir antarā tvaṣṭāraṃ devānāṃ ca patnībhiḥ putrakāmeṇa hotavyaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ cen na jāyeta tad anādṛtya caturhotrā yājayet
10.21.6	rājānam aparuddhaṃ saṅgrāme saṃyatte khile 'cchadir darśe caturgṛhītenājyena caturhotrā pūrvām āhutiṃ juhoti graheṇottarām api vā caturhotāraṃ manasānudrutya pūrveṇa graheṇārdhaṃ juhoty ardham uttareṇa yat tatra vinderaṃs tato dakṣiṇā syāc chatam eke samāmananti
10.21.7	caturhotrā yājayet prajākāmam
10.21.8	tasya sa eva homakalpaḥ
10.21.9	varo dakṣiṇā
10.21.10	pañcahotrā yājayet paśukāmam
10.21.11	caturgṛhītenājyena pañcahotrā pūrvām āhutiṃ juhoti graheṇottarām api vā pañcahotāram anudrutya pūrveṇa graheṇārdhaṃ juhoty ardham uttareṇa
10.21.12	tasyaitāś catasro dakṣiṇā aśvo hiraṇyaṃ vāso gauḥ
10.21.13	bhrātṛvyavantaṃ cādakṣiṇena homagrahābhyāṃ saptahotrā yājayet
10.21.14	yo yajñasyānusaṃsthāṃ pāpīyān syāc caturgṛhītenājyena saptahotrā pūrvām āhutiṃ juhoti graheṇottarām
10.22.1	vyākhyātāḥ kratusaṃyuktāḥ
10.22.2	abhicaran daśahotāraṃ juhuyāt svakṛta iriṇe pradare vā phaḍ iti vaṣaṭkaroti yaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vidyāṃ vidvāṃsaṃ yaśo narchet so 'raṇyaṃ paretya darbhastambam udgrathya brāhmaṇaṃ dakṣiṇato niṣādyoccaiś caturhotṝn vyācakṣīta sagrahān sasvāhākārān sasaṃbhārayajuṣkān sapatnīkān sapratigrahaṇamantrān api vā caturhotṝn eva yo brāhmaṇo dakṣiṇata āste varaṃ tasmai dadyād yad evainaṃ tatra yaśa ṛcchati tad varuṇo 'varundha iti vijñāyate
10.22.3	yady enam ārtvijyād vṛtaṃ santaṃ nirharerann āgnīdhre juhuyād daśahotāraṃ caturgṛhītenājyena navagṛhītenety ekeṣāṃ purastāt pratyaṅ tiṣṭhan pratilomaṃ vigrāhaṃ prāṇān evāsyopadāsayati yady enaṃ punar upaśikṣeyur āgnīdhra eva juhuyād daśahotāraṃ caturgṛhītenājyena navagṛhītenety ekeṣāṃ paścāt prāṅ āsīno 'nulomam avigrāhaṃ prāṇān evāsmai kalpayati
10.22.4	prāyaścittī vāg ghotety ṛtumukhaṛtumukhe ṣaḍḍhotāraṃ juhuyāt
10.22.5	yaḥ kāmayeta bahor bhūyān syām iti sa daśahotāraṃ prayuñjīta
10.22.6	yaḥ kāmayeta vīro ma ājāyeteti sa caturhotāram
10.22.7	yaḥ kāmayeta paśumān syām iti sa pañcahotāram
10.22.8	yaḥ kāmayetartavo me kalperann iti sa ṣaḍḍhotāram
10.22.9	yaḥ kāmayeta somapaḥ somayājī syām ā me somapaḥ somayājī jāyeteti sa saptahotāram
10.22.10	yaḥ kāmayeta priyaḥ syām iti yaṃ vā kāmayeta priyaḥ syād iti tasmā etaṃ sthāgaram alaṃkāraṃ kalpayitvā daśahotāraṃ dakṣiṇataḥ pañcahotāraṃ paścāt ṣaḍḍhotāram uttarataḥ saptahotāram upariṣṭāt saṃbhāraiś ca patnibhiś ca mukhe 'laṃkṛtyāsyārdhaṃ vrajet priyo haiva bhavati
10.22.11	teṣāṃ ye homārthe śrūyante sagrahāḥ sasvāhākārās te prayujyeran ye tv ahomārthe 'grahā asvāhākārās te
10.22.12	ye japā ye yājamānās te 'pi kratusaṃyuktāḥ
10.22.13	ta āhitāgner ubhayor akratusaṃyuktā bhavanti
10.23.1	vāsiṣṭho brahmā jyotiṣṭome
10.23.2	yo vā kaścit stomabhāgān adhīyāt
10.23.3	anyonyasmai vā ṛtvijo yajñasaṃpradāyaṃ caranti
10.23.4	yāvad ṛcārtvijyaṃ kriyate hotṛṣv eva tāvad yajño bhavati
10.23.5	yāvad yajuṣādhvaryuṣv eva tāvat
10.23.6	yāvat sāmnodgātṛṣv eva tāvat
10.23.7	yatra kvaca yajñasya virataṃ brahmaṇy eva tāvad yajño bhavati
10.23.8	tasmād etasminn antardhau brahmā vācaṃyamaḥ syāt
10.23.9	yadi pramatto vyāhared vaiṣṇavīm ṛcaṃ japitvā vyāhṛtīś ca punar vācaṃ yacchati
10.23.10	rājani mīyamāne 'gnau kriyamāṇe mahāvedyām uttaravedyāṃ ca kriyamāṇāyāṃ rājani hriyamāṇe 'bhiṣūyamāṇe bahiṣpavamāne stūyamāne
10.23.11	ukhāyāṃ saṃbhriyamāṇāyām ukhākarmasu ca kriyamāṇeṣu
10.23.12	pravṛjyamānāyāṃ ca
10.23.13	agnau mīyamāne
10.23.14	kṛṣyamāṇe
10.23.15	opyamāne
10.23.16	citer upadhīyamānāyāḥ
10.23.17	saṃcitakarmasu ca
10.23.18	eteṣu karmasu yathākālaṃ kriyamāṇeṣu dakṣiṇata āste
10.23.19	rājany ohyamāne 'gnau praṇīyamāne havirdhānayoḥ prohyamāṇayoḥ
10.23.20	ukhāyāṃ saṃbhariṣyamāṇāyām
10.23.21	ohyamānāyāṃ ca
10.23.22	nairṛtīr upadhāsyatām
10.23.23	cityagnīnāṃ praṇīyamānānām
10.23.24	vasatīvarīḥ savanīyāś ca gacchatām
10.23.25	āhriyamāṇāsu ca
10.23.26	avabhṛthaṃ cābhyavaiṣyatām
10.23.27	udyatsu ca
10.23.28	eteṣu karmasu yathākālaṃ kriyamāṇeṣu dakṣiṇata eti
10.23.29	sadohavirdhāneṣu saṃmīyamāneṣv antareṇa cātvālotkarāv anvetyāpareṇottaravedim atikramya dakṣiṇata upaviśati
10.24.1	ā vaisarjanakālād anvāste
10.24.2	hoṣyamāṇeṣu vaisarjaneṣu yathetaṃ pratyetyottareṇāgnīdhrīyaṃ dhiṣṇiyaṃ parītya pūrveṇa dvāreṇa prāgvaṃśaṃ praviśyāpareṇa śālāmukhīyam atikramya dakṣiṇata upaviśati
10.24.3	evā vandasvety upasthe rājānaṃ kurute
10.24.4	ā vaisarjanahomād anvāste
10.24.5	hute vaisarjane 'nvag agner gacchati
10.24.6	pūrvo vā
10.24.7	āgnīdhrīyaṃ prāpya dakṣiṇata upaviśaty ā vaisarjanahomād anvāste hute vaisarjane 'nyasmai rājānaṃ pradāyottareṇāgnīdhrīyaṃ dhiṣṇiyaṃ parītya rājānaṃ pratyādāya somo jigāti gātuvid iti saumyarcāpareṇa dvāreṇa havirdhāne praviśyādhvaryave rājānaṃ pradāya yathetaṃ pratyetyāpareṇottaravedim atikramya dakṣiṇata upaviśati
10.24.8	agnīṣomīyasyā vapāyā homād anvāste
10.24.9	hutāyāṃ vapāyāṃ mārjayate
10.24.10	vasatīvarīṣu parigṛhyamāṇāsu vācaṃ yacchaty ā subrahmaṇyāyāḥ
10.24.11	mahārātre budhyamāneṣu budhyate
10.24.12	upākṛte prātaranuvāke vācaṃ yacchaty ā paridhānīyāyāḥ
10.24.13	savanīyāsu prapādyamānāsu pūrveṇa dvāreṇa havirdhāne praviśyāgreṇa kharaṃ parītya dakṣiṇata upaviśati
10.25.1	ā grahakālād anvāste
10.25.2	graheṣu gṛhyamāṇeṣu vācaṃ yacchaty āgrayaṇasya grahaṇāt
10.25.3	bahiṣpavamānaṃ sarpatsu samanvārabhya sarpati
10.25.4	brahman stoṣyāmīty ucyamāne deva savitar etat te prāha tat pra ca suva pra ca yaja bṛhaspatir brahmāyuṣmatyā ṛco mā gāta tanūpāt sāmnaḥ satyā va āśiṣaḥ santu satyā ākūtaya ṛtaṃ ca satyaṃ ca vadata stuta devasya savituḥ prasava oṃ stuteti prasauti
10.25.5	sarvastotrāṇām eṣa kalpaḥ
10.25.6	raśmir asi kṣayāya tvā kṣayaṃ jinvety ekatriṃśataḥ stomabhāgāḥ stotre stotra uttaramuttaram ādadhāti
10.25.7	dvādaśāgniṣṭome trayodaśātyagniṣṭome pañcadaśokthye ṣoḍaśa ṣoḍaśini saptdaśa vājapeya ekānnatriṃśatam atirātre trayastriṃśatam aptoryāme
10.25.8	stute bahiṣpavamāne yathetaṃ pratyetyāpareṇottaravedim atikramya dakṣiṇata upaviśati savanīyasyā vapāyā homād anvāste
10.25.9	hutāyāṃ vapāyāṃ mārjayitvā pūrveṇa dvāreṇa sadaḥ praviśyāgreṇa praśāstrīyaṃ dhiṣṇiyaṃ parītya dakṣiṇata upaviśaty āsaṃsthānād anvāste
10.25.10	yatrāsmai camasam āharati taṃ bhakṣayati yathetare camasān
10.25.11	stutaśastrayor vācaṃ yacchati
10.25.12	saṃsthite savane yathetaṃ pratiniṣkrāmati
10.25.13	evaṃ vihita uttarayoḥ savanayoḥ saṃcaro brahmatvaṃ ca
10.25.14	ādhvaryava evāto 'nyāni karmāṇi brāhmaṇa āmnātāni bhavanti
10.25.15	evaṃ vihitaṃ saṃsthānāṃ brahmatvaṃ brahmatvam
11.1.1	agniṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.1.2	sa uttarakratvarthaḥ / anyatra sādyaskrebhyo vājapeyāt ṣoḍaśinaḥ sārasvatāc ca satrāt / agniśinastomo yathopadiṣṭaṃ vā / rātrisatreṣu samahāvrateṣv aśravaṇārthā punaścitiḥ
11.1.3	api vā dhāryamāṇe 'gnau prajāpatis tvā sādayatu tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīdety antarvedim abhimṛśet / tisro vā svayamātṛṇṇā upadhāya tāsām upadhānakalpaḥ svayamātṛṇṇā sāma purīṣaṃ viśvajyotiḥ / evaṃ vihitā dvitīyāh purīṣā tṛtīyā
11.1.4	api vā tisraś ca svayamātṛṇṇāḥ sarvāś ca viśvajyotiṣas tāsām upadhānakalpaḥ svayamātṛṇṇā sāma purīṣaṃ viśvajyotir evaṃ vihitā dvitīyā tṛtīyasyāṃ tu viśvajyotiḥ prathamā / atha purīṣam / atha svayamātṛṇṇām / atha sāma
11.1.5	taṃ ceṣyamāṇo 'māvāsyāyāṃ paurṇamāsyām āpūryamāṇapakṣe vā puṇye nakṣatra ṛtvijo vṛtvā
11.1.6	bṛhaspatipurohitā devānāṃ devāḥ prathamajā devā deveṣu parākramadhvaṃ prathamā dvitīyeṣu dvitīyās tṛtīyeṣu trir ekādaśās trayastriṃśā anu va ārabha idaṃ śakeyaṃ yad idaṃ karomi svāhety āhutiṃ juhoti
11.1.7	juhūṃ sruvaṃ ca saṃmṛjya caturgṛhītam ājyam aṣṭagṛhītaṃ vā gṛhītvā yuñjānaḥ prathamaṃ mana iti yajuraṣṭamābhir ṛgbhir antarvedy ūrdhvas tiṣṭhan sāvitrāṇy ekām āhutiṃ juhoti
11.1.8	yaṃ kāmayeta pāpīyānt syād ity ekaikaṃ tasya juhuyāt / yaṃ kāmayeta vasīyant syād iti sarvāṇi tasyānudrutya juhuyāt
11.1.9	yadi kāmayeta cchandāṃsi yajñayaśasenārpayeyam ity ṛcam antimāṃ kuryāt / yadi kāmayeta yajamānaṃ yajñayaśasenārpayeyam iti yajur antimaṃ kuyāt
11.1.10	ṛcā stomaṃ samardhayeti caturgṛhītenottarām
11.1.11	devasya tveti caturbhir abhrimādatte // khādirīṃ vaiṇaivīṃ vā kalmāṣīṃ suṣirām asuṣirāṃ vobhayataḥkṣṇū tām anyatarataḥkṣṇū tāṃ vā pālāśīm audumbarīm arkamayīṃ śamīmayīṃ vā / yo vā kaścana vṛkṣaḥ phalagrahis tasya muṣṭimātriṃ prādeśamātrīm aratnimātriṃ bāhumātriṃ vyāmamātrīm aparimitāṃ vā
11.1.12	imām agṛbhṇan raśanām ṛtasyety aśvābhidhānīm ādāya pratūrtaṃ vājinn ādravety aśvam abhidadhāti
11.1.13	tūṣṇīṃ gardabhasyādāya yuñjāthāṃ rāsabhaṃ yuvam iti gardabham
11.1.14	yogeyoge tavastaram iti tisṛbhir aśvaprathamāḥ prāñco gacchanti yatra mṛdaṃ khaniṣyanto bhavanti
11.1.15	agniṃ purīṣyam aṅgirasvad acchehīti yena dveṣyeṇa saṃgaccheta tam abhimantrayetāpaśyan nirdiśati
11.1.16	agniṃ purīṣyam aṅgirasvad acchema iti vā
11.1.17	sūryasyodayanaṃ prati valmīkavapām upatiṣṭhate 'gniṃ purīṣyam aṅgirasvad bhariṣyāma iti
11.1.18	atraike samāmananti agniṃ purīṣyam aṅgirasvad bharāmaḥ
11.1.19	anv agnir uṣasām agram akhyad iti valmīkavapāyāḥ prakrāmati
11.1.20	āgatya vājy adhvana ākramya vājin pṛthivīm iti dvābhyāṃ mṛtkhanam aśvam ākramayati
11.1.21	dyaus te pṛṣṭham ity aśvasya pṛṣṭhaṃ saṃmārṣṭi
11.1.22	abhitiṣṭha pṛtanyato 'dhare santu śatravaḥ / indra iva vṛtrahā tiṣṭhāpaḥ kṣetrāṇi saṃjayann iti yaṃ dveṣṭi tam adhas padam aśvasya manasā dhyāyati
11.1.23	utkrāmodakramīd iti dvābhyāṃ mṛtkhanād aśvam utkramayanti
11.1.24	apo devīr upasṛjety aśvasya pade 'pa upasṛjati
11.1.25	tasmin hiraṇyaṃ nidhāya jigharmy agnim ā tvā jigharmīti manasvatībhyām ekām āhutiṃ juhoti
11.1.26	apādāya hiraṇyaṃ pari vājapatir iti tisṛbhir abhryā mṛtkhanaṃ parilikhati bāhyāṃ varṣīyasīm
11.1.27	devasya tveti dvābhyāṃ khanati
11.1.28	apāṃ pṛṣṭham asīti puṣkaraparṇam āharati / etayaiva viveṣṭayati / upariṣṭāt kṛṣṇājinam uttareṇa mṛtkhanaṃ śarma ca stho varma ca stha iti // dvābhyāṃ prācīnagrīvam uttaralomāstṛṇāty uttaraṃ puṣkaraparṇam adhastāddaṇḍam uttānam
11.1.29	purīṣyo 'si viśvabharā iti mṛdam abhimṛśya
11.1.30	kṛṣṇājine puṣkaraparṇe ca saṃbharati tvām agne puṣkarād adhīti tisṛbhir gāyatrībhir brāhmaṇasya / uttarābhis triṣṭugbhī rājanyasya jagatībhir vaiśyasya
11.1.31	yaṃ kāmayeta vasīyānt syād ity ubhayībhis tasya saṃbharet / gāyatrībhiś ca triṣṭugbhiś ca
11.1.32	janiṣvā hi jenya iti saṃbhṛtām abhimantrayate
11.1.33	saṃ te vāyur mātariśvā dadhātv iti mṛtkhane 'pa upasṛjati
11.1.34	saṃlobhya mṛtkhanaṃ samudgṛhya kṛṣṇājinasyātnān sujāto jyotiṣā saheti mauñjenārkamayeṇa vā trivṛtā dāmnopanahyati
11.1.35	ud u tiṣṭha svadhvareti dvābhyām uttiṣṭhati
11.1.36	sa jāto garbho asi rodasyor iti harati
11.1.37	sthiro bhava vīḍvaṅga iti gardabhasya pṛṣṭha āsādayati
11.1.38	śivo bhava prajābhya ity āsannam abhimantrayate
11.1.39	praitu vājī kanikradad iti tisṛbhir atvaramāṇā aśvaprathamāḥ pratyāyanti
11.1.40	agniṃ purīṣyam aṅgirasvad bharāma iti yena dveṣyeṇa saṃgaccheta tam abhimantrayetāpaśyan nirdiśati
11.1.41	uttareṇa vihāraṃ pariśrita oṣadhayaḥ pratigṛhṇītāgnim etam iti dvābhyām oṣadhīṣu puṣpavatīṣu phalavatīṣūpāvaharati
11.1.42	vi pājaseti visraṃsayati
11.1.43	āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhir apa upasṛjati
11.1.44	mitraḥ saṃsṛjya pṛthivīm iti dvābhyāṃ saṃsarjanīyaiḥ saṃsṛjati // armakapālair veṇvaṅgārair vrīhituṣaiḥ palāśakaṣāyaiś ca śarkarābhiḥ piṣṭābhiḥ kṛṣṇājinalomabhir ajalomabhir yac cānyad dṛḍhārtham upārthaṃ manyate
11.1.45	makhasya śiro 'sīti piṇḍaṃ karoti
11.1.46	yajñasya pade stha iti kṛṣṇājinaṃ puṣkaraparṇaṃ cābhimantrayate
11.1.47	rudrāḥ saṃbhṛtya pṛthivīm iti catasṛbhiḥ piṇḍān prayacchati
11.1.48	vasavas tvā kṛṇvantv iti caturbhiś chandobhir mahiṣy ukhāṃ karoti bahubhāryasya
11.1.49	adhvaryur ekabhāryasya
11.1.50	etair eva yajurbhir yajamānaḥ kriyamāṇām abhimantrayate
11.1.51	tryuddhiṃ pañcoddhiṃ vā karoti
11.1.52	prādeśamātrīm ūrdhvapramāṇenāratnimātrīṃ tiryakpramāṇena vyāyāmamātrīṃ samantaparimāṇenāparimitāṃ vā kurvaṃś catasro 'śrīḥ pratidiśam unnayati
11.1.53	parimaṇḍalāṃ vā karoti
11.1.54	navāśrim abhicarataḥ kuryāt
11.1.55	adityai rāsnāsīti madhyadeśa upabilaṃ vā rāsnāṃ karoti
11.1.56	aśrīṇāṃ rāsnāyāś ca saṃdhau dvau caturaḥ ṣaḍaṣṭau vā stanān karoti
11.1.57	aditis te bilaṃ gṛhṇātv iti bilaṃ karoti
11.1.58	kṛtvāya sā mahīm ukhām ity uttarataḥ sikatāsu pratiṣṭhāpayati
11.1.59	tasyā eva mṛdo 'ṣāḍhām iṣṭakāṃ tryālikhitāṃ tūṣṇīṃ caturaśrāṃ karoti
11.1.60	gārhapatye 'śvaśakṛty upasamādhāya vasavas tvā dhūpayantv iti saptabhiś chandobhir ukhām aśvaśakair dhūpayati
11.1.61	aditis tvā devīr ity agreṇa gārhapatyam avaṭaṃ khātvā lohitapacanaiḥ saṃbhārair avastīrya devānāṃ tvāṃ patnīr iti tasminn ukhām avadadhāti
11.1.62	tūṣṇīm aṣāḍhām anvavadhāya lohitapacanīyaiḥ saṃbhāraiḥ pracchādya dhiṣaṇās tvā devīr iti ṣaḍbhir gārhapatyāt pacati
11.1.63	mitrasya carṣaṇīdhṛta iti pacyamānāṃ maitriyopacarati
11.1.64	devas tvā savitodvapatv iti pakvām udvapati
11.1.65	apadyamānā pṛthivy āśā diśa āpṛṇety uttarataḥ sikatāsu pratiṣṭhāpayati
11.1.66	mitraitām ukhāṃ paridadāmy abhityā eṣā mā bhedīti mitrāya paridāya vasavas tvā chṛndantv iti caturbhiś chandobhir ukhām ajākṣīreṇācchṛṇatti
11.1.67	saptaikaviṃśatiṃ caturviṃśatiṃ vā māṣān ādāya puruṣaśiro 'cchaiti rājanyasya vaiśyasya veṣuhatasyāśanihatasya vā / puṃso māṣān upanyupya
11.1.68	ayaṃ yo 'si yasya ta idaṃ śira iti puruṣaśiraḥ pracchidyaitena tvam atra śīrṣaṇvān edhīti saptadhā vitṛṇṇāṃ valmīkavapāṃ śirasaḥ sthāne pratinidadhāti
11.1.69	yo 'sya kauṣṭhya jagataḥ pārthivasyaika id vaśī / yamaṃ bhaṅgyaśravo gāya yo rājānaparodhyaḥ / yamaṃ gāya bhaṅgyaśravo yo rājānaparodhyaḥ / yenāpo nadyo dhanvāni yena dyauḥ pṛthivī dṛḍhā / hiraṇyakakṣyān sudhurān hiraṇyākṣān ayaḥśaphān / aśvān anaśyato dānaṃ yamo rājābhitiṣṭhatīti tisṛbhiryamagāyābhiḥ parigāyati
11.1.70	āharañ japatīty eke
11.1.71	idam asmākaṃ bhuje bhogāya bhūyād iti puruṣaśira ādatte
11.1.72	udehy agne adhi mātuḥ pṛthivyā ity āharati
11.1.73	pari triviṣṭy adhvaraṃ yāty agnī rathīr iva / ā deveṣu prayo dadhat / pari vājapatiḥ kavir ity eṣā / pari prāgād devo agnī rakṣohāmīvacātanaḥ / sedhan viśvā apa dviṣo dahan rakṣāṃsi viśvaheti tisṛbhiḥ paryagni karoti / mṛdā pralipya nidadhāti
11.2.1	agnibhyaḥ kāmāya paśūn ālabhate / aśvam ṛṣabhaṃ vṛṣṇibastaṃ prājāpatyam ajaṃ tūparaṃ muṣkarā bhavanti
11.2.2	ekaviṃśatiṃ caturviṃśatiṃ vā sāmidhenīḥ parācīr anvāhaikādaśa prākṛtīr anūcya samās tvāgna ṛtavo vardhayantv iti daśāgnikīr anvāhopem asṛkṣi vājayur vacasyāṃ cano dadhīta nādyo giro me / apāṃnapād āśuhemā kurvit sa supeśasas karati joṣiṣaddhi / apāṃnapād ā hy asthād upasthaṃ jihmānām ūrdhvaḥ svayaśā upasthe / ubhe abhi priyatame sadhasthe ā ca parā ca carati prajānann iti tisro 'psumatīr yadi caturviṃśatir bhavanti
11.2.3	amutrabhūyād adha yad yamasyety āmayāvinaḥ kuryāt
11.2.4	bṛhaspate savitar bodhayainam ity anāmayāvinaḥ
11.2.5	rāye agne mahe tvā dānāya samidhīmahi / īḍiṣvā hi mahī vṛṣan dyāvā hotrāya pṛthivīm / ud vayaṃ tamasas parīti jyotiṣmatyā paridadhāti
11.2.6	hiraṇyagarbhaḥ samavartatāgra iti srucyam āghārayati
11.2.7	ūrdhvā asya samidho bhavantīti prayājānām āpriyo bhavanti
11.2.8	āgneyīs triṣṭubha āgneyānāṃ yājyānuvākyā bhavanti
11.2.9	yaḥ prāṇata iti prājāpatyasya
11.2.10	vaiśvānaraḥ prajāpatyo vā dvādaśakapālaḥ paśupuroḍāśo bhavati
11.2.11	siddhaṃ saṃtiṣṭhate
11.2.12	api vāgneyān paryagnikṛtān utsṛjya teṣāṃ śirāṃsi pracchidya mṛdā pralipya nidadhāti
11.2.13	apaḥ kabandhāny abhyavaharati
11.2.14	prājāpatyena saṃsthāpayati
11.2.15	api vaiteṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ sthāne vāyave niyutvate śvetam ajaṃ tūparam ālabheta
11.2.16	tasya prājāpatyena kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
11.2.17	vāyum atī śvetavatī vapāyā yājyānuvākye bhavataḥ
11.2.18	vāyumatī niyutvatī paśor daivatasya vaiśvānaraḥ prājāpatyo vā dvādaśakapālaḥ puroḍāśo bhavati
11.2.19	siddhaṃ saṃtiṣṭhate
11.2.20	mṛdā pralipya vāyavyasya śiro nidadhāti
11.3.1	yat prāg dīkṣaṇīyāyās tat kṛtvā dvihaviṣaṃ trihaviṣaṃ vā dīkṣanīyām iṣṭiṃ nirvapati / āgnāvaiṣṇavam ekādaśakapālam āgnāvaiṣṇavaṃ vā ghṛte carum ādityaṃ ca ghṛte caruṃ vaiśvānaraṃ dvādaśakapālaṃ purastāt tṛtīyam asaṃvatsarabhṛtaḥ
11.3.2	dīkṣāhutikāla ākūtyai prayuje 'gnaye svāheti pañcādhvarikīr hutvākūtim agnim iti ṣaḍ āgnikīr juhoti / viśve devasya netur iti saptamīm
11.3.3	yat prāṅ muṣṭikaraṇāt tat kṛtvā śaṇakulāyena muñjakulāyena vokhām upastīrya mā su bhitthā mā su riṣa iti dvābhyām āhavanīyāṅgāreṣūkhāṃ pravṛṇakti
11.3.4	mitraitām ukhāṃ tapety aṅgāraiḥ paritapati
11.3.5	drvanna iti tasyāṃ kramukam ullikhitaṃ ghṛtenāṅktvāvadadhāti
11.3.6	muñjāñś ca
11.3.7	yo bhūtikāmaḥ syād ya ukhāyai saṃbhavet sa eva tasya syān mathitvā gataśriyo 'vadadhyāt
11.3.8	yaṃ kāmayeta bhrātṛvyam asmai janayeyam ity anyatas tasyāhṛtyāvadadhyāt
11.3.9	ambarīṣād annakāmasya
11.3.10	pradāvyād āhared yaṃ kāmayeta śūro me rāṣṭra ājāyeteti
11.3.11	vṛkṣāgrāj jvalato brahmavarcasakāmasya
11.3.12	bharjanād annakāmasya
11.3.13	kāmyam agniṃ kurvāṇo nāhavanīye 'nupravṛñjyāt
11.3.14	jāta ukhye 'nugamayaty āhavanīyam
11.3.15	parasyā adhi saṃvata ity audumbarīṃ samidham ādadhāti / paramasyāḥ parāvata iti vaikaṅkatīm / tāṃ savitur vareṇyasya citrām iti śamīmayīm
11.3.16	śamīmayīṃ pūrvām eke samāmananti / vaikaṅkatīm uttarām
11.3.17	sīda tvaṃ mātur asyā upastha iti tisṛbhir jātam ukhyam upatiṣṭhate
11.3.18	yad agne yāni kāniceti pañcabhir aparaśuvṛkṇam audumbaram idhmam abhyādadhāti
11.3.19	tailvakam abhicarataḥ kuryād grāhukā hainaṃ samāṃ stenā bhavanti
11.3.20	daṃṣṭrābhyāṃ malimlūn ity āśvatthīṃ samidham ādadhāti / ye janeṣu malimlava iti vaikaṅkatīm
11.3.21	yo asmabhyam arātīyād iti śamīmayīm / tā ādadhadyaṃ dveṣṭi tasya vadhaṃ manasā dhyāyati
11.3.22	saṃśitaṃ me brahmod eṣāṃ bāhū atiram ity uttame audumbaryau samidhāv ādadhāti
11.3.23	atha yajamānaṃ vācayati
11.3.24	brahma kṣatraṃ sayujā na vyathete brahmāha kṣatraṃ jinvati kṣatriyasya kṣatraṃ brahma jinvati brāhmaṇasya yat samīcī kṛṇvato vīryāṇīti japati
11.3.25	māteva putraṃ pṛthivī purīṣyam agniṃ sve yonau bhariṣyaty ukhā / tāṃ viśvair devair ṛtubhiḥ saṃvidānaḥ prajāpatir viśvakarmā yunaktv iti mauñje śikye ṣaḍudyāme dvādaśodyāme vokhām avadadhāti
11.3.26	agne yukṣvā hi ye taveti vaitābhyām ekaviṃśatinirbādho rukmaḥ sūtrotas tam antarvedy āsīno dṛśāno rukma iti bahiṣṭhanirbādhaṃ yajamāno viparyasya pratimuñcate 'dhastānnirbādhaṃ sādayati
11.3.27	naktoṣāseti kṛṣṇājinaṃ pratimuñcate
11.3.28	viśvā rūpāṇīti śikyapāśān
11.3.29	api vā śikyaṃ pratimucya kṛṣṇājinaṃ pratimuñcate
11.3.30	suparṇo 'si garutmān ity ukhyam avekṣate
11.3.31	suparṇo 'si garutmān divaṃ gacchety udyacchate
11.3.32	ūrdhvaṃ nābher dhārayamāṇo viṣṇoḥ kramo 'sīti caturo viṣṇukramān prācaḥ krāmati
11.3.33	akrandad agnir ity ukhyam abhimantrayate
11.3.34	agne 'bhyāvartinn iti catasṛbhiḥ pradakṣiṇam āvartate
11.3.35	ā tvāhārṣam ity āhṛtyopatiṣṭhate yaṃ kāmayeta rāṣṭraṃ syād iti taṃ manasā dhyāyed viśastvā sarvā vāñchantv iti
11.3.36	ud uttamam iti śikyapāśam unmuñcate
11.3.37	agre bṛhann uṣasām ūrdhvo asthād ity unmucyopatiṣṭhate
11.3.38	audumbaryāsandy aratnimātraśīrṣaṇyānūcyā prādeśamātrapādā mauñjavivānā phalakāstīrṇā vā mṛdā pradigdhā sīda tvaṃ mātur asyā upastha iti tasyāṃ catasṛbhir ukhyaṃ sādayati
11.3.39	śarkarāyāṃ vā
11.3.40	haṃsavatyopatiṣṭhata ity eke samāmananti
11.4.1	muṣṭikaraṇaprabhṛtīni karmāṇi pratipadyate
11.4.2	yena devā jyotiṣordhvā udāyann iti prādeśamātraiḥ kāṣṭhair ukhyam upasamindhe
11.4.3	sadā jvalati
11.4.4	annapate 'nnasya no dehīti vratayiṣyann audumbarīṃ samidhaṃ vrate samajyokhye 'bhyādadhāti
11.4.5	devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ gāyatreṇa cchandasā rātrim iṣṭakām upadadhe tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīdeti sāyam ukhyam upatiṣṭhate
11.4.6	devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ gāyatreṇa cchandasāhar iṣṭakām upadadhe tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīdeti prātaḥ
11.4.7	śvo bhūte divas pari prathamaṃ jajñe agnir ity ekādaśabhir vātsapreṇopatiṣṭhate
11.4.8	evaṃ sadākrayaṇāt
11.4.9	pūrvedyur viṣṇukramān krāmati / uttaredyur upatiṣṭhate vātsapreṇeti
11.4.10	yad ahar agniṃ ceṣyamāṇaḥ syāt tad ahar ubhayaṃ samasyet / pracakrāmed upatiṣṭheta
11.4.11	yady ukhye bhriyamāṇe 'yaṃ devaḥ prajā abhimanyeta bhiṣaṅ no agna āvaha / svaṃ rūpaṃ kṛṣṇavartmano asi hotā na īḍyaḥ / tvaṃ no agne bhiṣag bhava deveṣu havyavāhanaḥ / devebhyo havyavāḍ asi / bhiṣajas tvā havāmahe bhiṣajaḥ samidhīmahi / bhiṣag deveṣu no bhavety etābhis tisṛbhis tisraḥ samidha ādadhyāt
11.4.12	yady ukhye bhriyamāṇe kāmayeta varṣed iti sūryo apo vigāhate raśmibhir vājasā tamaḥ / bodhā stotre vayovṛdhaḥ // pari yo raśminā divo 'ntān mame pṛthivyāḥ / ubhe āpaprau rodasī mahitvā // bahiṣṭhebhir viharan yāsi tantum avavyayann asitaṃ deva vasvaḥ / davidhvato raśmayaḥ sūryasya carmevāvādhus tamo apsv antar ity etābhis tisṛbhis tisraḥ samidha ādadhyāt
11.4.13	yady ukhye bhriyamāṇe kāmayeta na varṣed ity adṛśram asya ketavo vi raśmayo janāṃ anu / bhrājanto agnayo yathā // taraṇir viśvadarśata ity eṣā // divo rukma urucakṣā udeti dūrearthas taraṇir bhrājamānaḥ / nūnaṃ janāḥ sūryeṇa prasūtā āyann arthāni kṛṇvann apāṃsīty etābhis tisraḥ samidha ādadhyāt
11.4.14	yady ukhye bhriyamāṇe kiṃcin naśyed agne 'bhyāvartinn iti catasṛbhir upatiṣṭhate / vindaty evaitad iti vijñāyate
11.5.1	ud u tvā viśve devā ity ukhyam udyacchate
11.5.2	sīda tvaṃ mātur asyā upastha iti catasṛbhir dvīṣe śakaṭa āsādayati
11.5.3	tūṣṇīm itarāv agnī āsādya pred agne jyotiṣmān iti prayāti
11.5.4	akrandad agnir ity akṣaśabdam abhimantrayate
11.5.5	adhyavasāyaudumbarīṃ samidhaṃ ghṛtānuṣiktām atithivatyokhye 'bhyādadhāti samidhāgniṃ duvasyateti gāyatryā brahmaṇasya / pra prāyam agnir iti triṣṭubhā rājanyasya / jagatyā vaiśyasya
11.5.6	indhane vratane 'dhyavasāne ca sarvāsu saṃnipātitāsu ghṛtānuṣiktāṃ prathamām ādadhāti
11.5.7	yady ukhāṃ bhasmābhisaṃsīded ukhyam ādāyodakāntaṃ gatvemaṃ suyoniṃ suvrataṃ hiraṇmayam prapyātam agne sarirasya madhye / utsaṃ juṣasva madhumantam ūrva samudriyaṃ sadanam āviśasva iti dvābhyām ukhyam upāvaharati
11.5.8	āpo devīḥ pratigṛbhṇīta bhamasitad iti tisṛbhir apsu bhasma praveśayati
11.5.9	bhasmanaḥ pratyādāya prasadya bhasmanā yonim iti dvābhyām ukhyāyāṃ pratyavadadhāti
11.5.10	punar ūrjā saha rayyeti dvābhyāṃ pratyeti
11.5.11	punas tvādityā rudrā vasavaḥ samindhatām ity upasamindhe
11.5.12	bodhā sa bodhīti // bodhavatībhyām upatiṣṭhate
11.5.13	nityam apsu bhasmapraveśanaṃ kṛtvā dīkṣitasya kṛtāsv iṣṭakāsu akṛtāsv iṣṭakānāṃ saṃsargārthaṃ bhavati
11.5.14	purīṣe paśukāmaḥ kurvīta
11.5.15	apsu yāyāvaraḥ pravapet
11.5.16	tisro rātrīr dīkṣitaḥ syāt / ṣaḍ rātrīr dīkṣitaḥ syād iti brāhmaṇavyākhyātāḥ kāmyā dīkṣākalpās teṣāṃ yāthākāmī
11.5.17	dīkṣitasyeṣṭakāḥ karoti māsaprabhṛtiṣu dīkṣākalpeṣu purastād adīkṣitasyetareṣūpariṣṭāt prājāpatyāt paśoḥ
11.5.18	mṛnmayīr iṣṭakā aviṣamāś caturaśrās tāsāṃ tisro maṇḍaleṣṭakā ṛjulekhā dakṣiṇāvṛtaḥ savyāvṛtaś ca tryālikhitāḥ
11.5.19	nirmanthyena lohinīḥ pacanti
11.5.20	na kṛṣṇāṃ na lakṣmaṇāṃ na bhinnāṃ copadadhāti
11.5.21	puṣkaraparṇaṃ rukmo hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣaḥ srucau sapta svayamātṛṇṇāḥ śarkarā hiraṇyeṣṭakāḥ pañca ghṛteṣṭakā dūrvāstambaḥ kūrma ulūkhalaṃ musalaṃ śūrpam aśmānaḥ paśuśirāṃsi sarpaśiraś cāmṛnmayīr iṣṭakāḥ
11.5.22	yāvad agnimānā mantrā yathārthaṃ lokaṃpṛṇā jānudaghnaṃ sāhasraṃ cinvīta prathamaṃ cinvānaḥ / nābhidaghnaṃ dviṣāhasraṃ dvitīyam / āsyadaghnaṃ triṣāhasraṃ tṛtīyam / uttaramuttaraṃ jyāyāṃsam
11.5.23	mahāntaṃ bṛhantam aparimitaṃ svargakāmaś cinvīteti vājasaneyakam
11.5.24	apavṛtte dīkṣāparimāṇe 'peta vīteti devayajanam adhyavasyati
11.5.25	uddhatya citer āyatanaṃ vyāyāmamātram // caturaśraṃ parimaṇḍalaṃ vāpeta vīteti hariṇyā palāśaśākhayā saṃsṛjyādbhir avokṣyāgner bhasmāsīti sikatā navapati
11.5.26	saṃjñanam asi kāmadharaṇam ity ūṣān
11.5.27	tān nivapan yad adaś candramasi kṛṣṇaṃ tad ihāstv iti manasā dhyāyati
11.5.28	saṃ yā vaḥ priyās tanuva ity ūṣān sikatāś ca saṃsṛjyānuvyūhati
11.5.29	citaḥ stha paricita ity ekaviṃśatyā śarkarābhir gārhapatyaciter āyatanaṃ pariśrayati
11.5.30	tisrastisraḥ saṃhitāḥ karoti
11.5.31	ayaṃ so agnir iti catasṛbhir gārhapatyacitau catasraḥ prācīr iṣṭakā upadadhāti
11.5.32	iḍām agne 'yaṃ te yonir ṛtviya iti dve purastādūrdhvasaṃhite cid asi paricid asīti dve paścādūrdhvasaṃhite lokaṃ pṛṇa chidraṃ pṛṇety avaśiṣṭaṃ trayodaśabhir lokaṃpṛṇābhiḥ pracchādayati
11.5.33	dvābhyāṃdvābhyāṃ mantrābhyām ekaikāṃ lokaṃpṛṇām upadadhāti
11.5.34	pūrvayopadhāya sūdadohasābhimṛśati
11.5.35	sarvāsv iṣṭakāsu tayādevatam antato dadhāti
11.5.36	kṛṣṇo 'śvaḥ śyāvo vottaratas tiṣṭhati
11.5.37	tam ālabhya cātvālāt purīṣam āhṛtya pṛṣṭo divīty anuvyūhati
11.5.38	sā citir bhavati
11.5.39	pañcacitīkaṃ cinvīta prathamaṃ cinvānas tricitīkaṃ dvitīyam ekacitīkaṃ tṛtīyam
11.5.40	ekacitīko nityaḥ kalpaḥ
11.6.1	sam itam iti catasṛbhir gārhapatyacitāv ukhyaṃ nivapati
11.6.2	māteva putram iti śikyād ukhāṃ nirūhati
11.6.3	atraivaike pūraṇam āmananti na riktām avekṣeta
11.6.4	yad asya pāre rajasa iti vaiśvānaryā śikyam ādatte
11.6.5	nairṛtīr iṣṭakāḥ kṛṣṇās tisras tuṣapakvāḥ śikyaṃ rukmasūtram āsandīṃ cādāya dakṣiṇāparam avāntaradeśaṃ hṛtvā svakṛta iriṇe pradare vā namaḥ su te nirṛta iti parācīr asaṃspṛṣṭā upadadhāti
11.6.6	tasyeṣṭakābhiḥ pāśam abhyupadadhāti
11.6.7	yasyās te asyāḥ krūra āsañ juhomīty etābhis tisṛbhiḥ parācīr asaṃspṛṣṭā dakṣiṇāpavargam
11.6.8	na tayādevataṃ karoti
11.6.9	yat te devī nirṛtir ābabandheti śikyam adhinyasyati
11.6.10	atrāsandīṃ rukmasūtraṃ ca nidadhāti
11.6.11	yad asya pāre rajasa iti vaiśvānaryā pariṣiñcati
11.6.12	namo bhūtyā iti pradakṣiṇam āvartate
11.6.13	śaṃ no devīr abhiṣṭaya iti mārjayante
11.6.14	ūrjaṃ bibhrad vasumanāḥ sumedhā gṛhān aimi manasā modamānaḥ suvarcāḥ / aghoreṇa cakṣuṣāhaṃ śivena gṛhāṇāṃ paśyan vaya uttirāṇīty apratīkṣam āyanti
11.6.15	niveśanaḥ saṃgamano vasūnām ity āhavanīyam upatiṣṭhante / gārhapatyaṃ vā
11.6.16	prāyaṇīyena pracarite rājānaṃ nyupya vediṃ kṛtvā samūlaṃ haritaṃ darbhastambaṃ madhye 'gner nikhāya juhvā pañcagṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā sajūr abdo 'yāvabhir iti samudgṛhṇan darbhastambe pañcāhutīr juhoti
11.6.17	yāvān puruṣa ūrdhvabāhus tāvatā veṇunāgniṃ vimimīte
11.6.18	trīn prācaḥ puruṣāṃś catura udīcas tiryañcaṃ puruṣamātrāṇi pakṣapucchāni bhavanti
11.6.19	ātmā catuḥpuruṣo 'ratninā dakṣiṇato dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣaṃ pravardhayati
11.6.20	prādeśena vitastyā vā paścāt puccham aratninottarata uttaraṃ pakṣam
11.6.21	syonā pṛthivi bhavānṛkṣarā niveśanī / yacchā naḥ śarma saprathāḥ / baḍ itthā parvatānām iti dvābhyāṃ vimitam agnim ākramante
11.6.22	saṃ varatrā dadhātaneti saṃpreṣyati
11.6.23	niṣkṛtāhāvam avaṭam ity avaṭam āhāvāṃś ca khanati
11.6.24	udriṇaṃ siñce akṣitam ity avaṭād āhāveṣūdakam utsiñcati
11.6.25	teṣu balīvardān pāyayanti
11.6.26	ud yojanam antaryāmam īṣāṃ khagalyaṃ śapham / aṣṭrāṃ tālaṃ pratīnāham ubhe maṇḍūkyau yujāv iti yugalāṅgalaṃ saṃprasārayati
11.6.27	sīrā yuñjantīti dvābhyāṃ sīraṃ yunakti / ṣaḍgavaṃ dvādaśagavaṃ caturviṃśatigavaṃ vā // sīrā yuñjantīti dve pūṣā yunaktu savitā yunaktu bṛhaspatir vo yunaktv agnes tejasā sūryasya varcaseti tisṛbhir yunakti ṣaḍgavaṃ dvādaśagavaṃ vety ekeṣām
11.6.28	uṣṭārayor bilvayor atho ābandhanīyayoḥ / sarveṣāṃ vidma vo nāma vāhāḥ kīlālapeśasa iti yuktān anumantrayate
11.6.29	brahma jajñānam ity eṣā / anāptā yā vaḥ prathamā yasyāṃ karmāṇi kṛṇvate / vīrān no atra mā dabhaṃs tad va etat puro dadhe // pary ū ṣu pra dhanva vājasātaye pari vṛtrāṇi sakṣaṇiḥ / dviṣas taradhyai ṛṇayā na īyase // sahasradhāre 'va te samasvaran divo nāke madhujihvā asaścataḥ / asya spaśo na nimiṣanti bhūrṇayaḥ padepade pāśinaḥ santi setava iti brahmavarmāṇi juhoti
11.6.30	udasthād gojid dhanajid aśvajiddhiraṇyajit sūnṛtayā parīvṛtaḥ / ekacakreṇa savitā rathenorjaṃ bhāgaṃ pṛthivīm etv āpṛṇann iti lāṅgalam ucchrayati
11.6.31	malimluco nāmāsi trayodaśo māsa indrasya varmāsīndrasya śarmāsīndrasya varūtham asi taṃ tvā prapadye / sā me śarma ca varma ca bhava / gāyatrīṃ lomabhiḥ praviśāmi / triṣṭubhaṃ tvacā praviśāmi / jagatīṃ māṃsena praviśāmi / anuṣṭubham asthnā praviśāmi
11.6.32	paṅktiṃ majjñā praviśāmi / aindrāgnaṃ varma bahulaṃ yad ugraṃ viśve devā nātividhyanti sūrāḥ / tan nas trāyatāṃ tan no viśvato mahad āyuṣmanto jarām upagacchema devā iti vimitam agnim ākramante / lāṅgalaṃ pavīravam iti dvābhyāṃ kṛṣati
11.6.33	kīnāśā balīvardān ajanti
11.6.34	pucchaśiro 'dhi kṛṣati
11.6.35	prakṣiṇam āvartayaṃs tisrastisraḥ sītāḥ saṃhitāḥ kṛṣanti kāmaṃ kāmadughe dhukṣveti
11.6.36	sītāṃ pratyavekṣate
11.6.37	ghṛtena sīteti sītāntarālān saṃmṛśati
11.6.38	dakṣiṇasmāt pakṣād uttaraṃ pakṣam abhikṛṣati
11.6.39	dakṣiṇasyāḥ śroṇer uttaram aṃsam uttarasyāḥ śroṇer dakṣiṇam aṃsam itarathā vā dvādaśa saṃpādayati
11.6.40	madhye saṃbhinnā bhavati
11.6.41	vimucyadhvam aghniyā devayānā atāriṣma tamasas pāram asya / jyotir āpāma suvar aganmeti dakṣiṇe 'ṃse balīvardān vimucyottare vā prāca udīco votsṛjati
11.6.42	tān adhvaryave dadāti
11.6.43	pañcadaśodacamasān ninayati
11.6.44	dvādaśānusītaṃ trīn akṛṣṭe
11.6.45	yā jātā oṣadhaya iti caturdaśabhir oṣadhīr vapati / sapta gramyā oṣadhayaḥ saptāraṇyāḥ
11.6.46	kṛṣṭe grāmyā vapaty anusītam akṛṣṭa āraṇyāḥ
11.6.47	yā oṣadhīnāṃ nādhigacchet tasyāḥ sthāne yavān madhumiśrān vapet
11.6.48	manasā dhyāyed uptā me 'sīti vā
11.6.49	adhigatāyāṃ yaḥ prathama idhma āgacchati tasminn upanahyati
11.6.50	ye vanaspatīnāṃ phalagrahayas tān idhma upasaṃnahya prokṣet
11.6.51	yat prāg ātithyāyās tat kṛtvā mā no hiṃsīj janiteti catasṛbhir digbhyo loṣṭān samasyati
11.6.52	ye 'ntarvidhād bahirvidham āpannā bhavanti
11.6.53	iṣam ūrjam aham ita ādada iti yasyām asya diśi dveṣyaḥ syāt tasyai diśo loṣṭam āharet
11.6.54	tathopakrameta yathā tasyāṃ diśy apavargaḥ syād uttaravedim upavapati / yāvān agnir vyāghāraṇāntaṃ kṛtvā
11.6.55	agne tava śravo vaya iti ṣaḍbhiḥ sikatā nivapati
11.6.56	citaḥ stha paricita ity aparimitābhiḥ śarkarābhir āhavanīyaciter āyatanaṃ pariśrayati yathā gārhapatyaciteḥ
11.6.57	trisaptābhiḥ paśukāmasya
11.6.58	triṇavābhir bhrātṛvyavataḥ
11.6.59	aparimitābhiḥ pariminuyāt
11.6.60	ā pyāyasva saṃ ta iti saumībhyāṃ sikatā vyūhati
11.6.61	apivā gāyatriyā brāhmaṇasya vyūhet triṣṭubhā rājanyasyāsāvi somo aruṣo vṛṣā harī rājeva dasmo abhi gā acikradat / punāno vāraṃ paryety avyayaṃ śyeno na yoniṃ ghṛtavantam āsadam iti jagatyā vaiśyasya
11.6.62	yaṃ kāmayetāpaśuḥ syād ity aparimitya tasya śarkarāḥ sikatā vyūhet / yaṃ kāmayeta paśumānt syād iti parimitya tasya śarkarāḥ sikatā vyūhet
11.7.1	ātithyāprabhṛtīni karmāṇi pratipadyate
11.7.2	prathamābhyāṃ paurvāhṇikībhyāṃ pravargyopasadbhyāṃ pracaryāgreṇa prāgvaṃśaṃ rohite carmaṇy ānaḍuhe prācīnagrīva uttaralomni prathamāyāś citer iṣṭakāḥ saṃsādayati
11.7.3	apivā tisraḥ svayamātṛṇṇāḥ sarvāś ca viśvajyotiṣaḥ
11.7.4	darbhāgram uṣṭinājyenāvokṣya tāḥ samudyamya cityagnibhyaḥ praṇīyamānebhyo 'nubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati / praṇīyamānebhyo 'nubrūhīti vā
11.7.5	triranūktāyām aśvaprathamāḥ prañco gacchanti
11.7.6	uttaravediṃ prāpya prajāpatis tvā sādayatu tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīdety uttaravedim abhimṛśya mayi gṛhṇāmi yo no agnir iti dvābhyām ātmann agniṃ gṛhītvā yās te agne samidho yāni dhāmeti svayaṃcityābhimṛśati
11.7.7	iṣṭakābhir agniṃ cinoty adhvaryur yajamāno brahmā vā svayam agniṃ cinvann ātmann agniṃ gṛhṇīte na svayaṃcityābhimṛśati
11.7.8	dakṣiṇāvṛto dakṣiṇata upadadhāty uttarataḥ savyāvṛta ṛjulekhāḥ paścāt purastāc ca bhavanti
11.7.9	tryālikhitā madhye prācīr upadadhāti
11.7.10	pratīcīr upadadhātīti gaṇeṣu rītivādaḥ / prācīm upadadhāti pratīcīm upadadhātīti kartur mukhavādaḥ purastād anyāḥ pratīcīr upadadhāti / paścād anyāḥ prācīr apavargavādā vacanāt pakṣapuccheṣu śroṇyor aṃsayor ity upadadhāti
11.7.11	śveto 'śvo dakṣiṇatas tiṣṭhati
11.7.12	tam ālabhyeṣṭakā upadadhāti
11.7.13	indraṃ viśvā avīvṛdhann ity aindriyarcākramaṇaṃ pratīṣṭakām upadadhyāt // uttarataḥ paścād upacāro vāgniḥ
11.7.14	vāṅ ma āsan nasoḥ prāṇa ity agnim adhikrāman sarveṣv ākramaṇeṣu japati
11.7.15	tat tvā yāmi brahmaṇā vandamāna iti vāruṇyarcā śālāmukhīye juhoti
11.7.16	abhyasthād viśvāḥ pṛtanā arātīr iti prāñcam aśvaṃ dakṣiṇena pādena darbhastambam ākramayati
11.7.17	yad akrandaḥ prathamaṃ jāyamāna iti pradakṣiṇam aśvaṃ paryāṇayati
11.7.18	dakṣiṇato dhāryamāṇe 'pāṃ pṛṣṭham asīti darbhastambe puṣkaraparṇam adhastāddaṇḍam uttānam upadadhāti
11.7.19	tapo yonir asi viśvābhis tvā dhībhir acchidraṃ sajātavanasyāyā upadadhāmy amṛtaṃ yonir brahma yoniḥ kṣatraṃ yoniḥ pṛthivī yonir antarikṣaṃ dyaur yonir diśo yonir iti vā
11.7.20	brahma jajñānam iti puṣkaraparṇe rukmam adhastānnirbādham upadadhāti
11.7.21	hiraṇyagarbhaḥ samavartatāgra iti hiraṇmayaṃ puruṣaṃ prāñcam uttānaṃ dakṣiṇato rukmasya drapsaś caskandety abhimṛśya puruṣasāmnābhigīyate
11.7.22	namo astu sarpebhya iti tisṛbhiḥ sarpanāmabhir upatiṣṭhate
11.7.23	kṛṇuṣva pāja iti pañcabhir akṣṇayā puruṣaṃ vyāghārayati yathottaravedim
11.7.24	ghṛtasya dadhnaś ca pūrṇe srucāv abhitaḥ puruṣam upadadhāti agnes tvā tejasā sādayāmīti
11.7.25	ghṛtasya pūrṇāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ kārṣmaryamayīm indrasya tvaujasā sādayāmīti dadhnaḥ pūrṇām uttarām audumbarīṃ te upadhāya mūrdhanvatībhyām upatiṣṭhate
11.7.26	apivā tūṣṇīm upadhāya mūrdhanvatībhyām upatiṣṭhate / mūrdhanvatībhyām upadhāya yajurbhyām upatiṣṭhata ity ekeṣām
11.7.27	rukmaṃ vyāghārayati / yathāpuruṣam
11.7.28	dhruvāsi dharuṇeti svayamātṛṇṇām abhimṛśyāśvenāvaghrāpya prajāpatis tvā sādayatu pṛthivyāḥ pṛṣṭhe vyacasvatīm iti madhye 'gner aviduṣā brāhmaṇena sahopadadhāti / bhūr iti caitayā vyāhṛtyā
11.7.29	citiṃ juhomīti svayamātṛṇṇāyāṃ hutvānuprāṇiti
11.7.30	avidvān brāhmaṇo varaṃ dadāti / ekaṃ dvau trīn vā
11.7.31	tejo 'si tejo me yaccha pṛthivīṃ yaccha pṛthivyai mā pahīti hiraṇyeṣṭakām / pṛthivy udapuram annena viṣṭā manuṣyās te goptāra iti maṇḍaleṣṭakām / bhūr asi bhuvanasya reta iṣṭakāḥ svargo loko manasā tvānvārohāmi suvar asi suvanasya reta iṣṭakāḥ svargo loko manasā tvānvārohāmīty anvārohe dve upadadhāti
11.7.32	kāṇḍātkāṇḍāt prarohantīti dvābhyāṃ dūrvāstambaṃ saloṣṭam apracchinnāgraṃ yathāsya svayamātṛṇṇām agraṃ prāpnuyāt
11.7.33	hiraṇyaśakalau prabāhug iṣṭakāyām adhyūhya yās te agne sūrye ruca iti dvābhyāṃ vāmabhṛtam
11.7.34	virāḍ jyotir adhārayad iti tisro retaḥsicaḥ
11.7.35	dve eke samāmananti
11.7.36	tāḥ prathamāyāṃ cityāṃ yūna upadadhyāt / madhyamāyāṃ vivayasaḥ / prathamāyām uttamāyāṃ ca sthavirasya
11.7.37	bṛhaspatis tvā sādayatu pṛthivyāḥ pṛṣṭhe jyotiṣmatīm iti viśvajyotiṣam / agner yāny asi devānām agner yāny asīti dve saṃyānyau / madhuś ca mādhavaś ceti dve ṛtavye / samānatayā devate bhavataḥ
11.7.38	sarvāsv ṛtavyāsv avakām upadadhāti
11.7.39	gharmeṣṭakām upadadhāti / tasyāḥ pravargye mantra āmnātaḥ
11.7.40	aṣāḍhāsīty upariṣṭāllakṣmāṇam aṣāḍhāṃ dveṣyasyādhastāllakṣmāṇaṃ yās te agna ārdrā yonayo yāḥ kulāyinīḥ / ye te agna indavo yā u nābhayaḥ / yās te agne tanuva ūrjo nāma tābhis tvam ubhayībhiḥ saṃvidānaḥ / iha prajānāṃ tanvā niṣīdeti kulāyinīm
11.7.41	madhu vātā ṛtāyata iti tisṛbhir dadhnā madhumiśreṇa kūrmam abhyanakti
11.7.42	apāṃ gambhīraṃ gaccha mā tvā sūryaḥ parītāpsīn mo agnir vaiśvānaraḥ / aghoraḥ prajā abhi vipaśyānu tvā divyā vṛṣṭiḥ sacatām // saṃsarpa trīn samudrānt svasalilārgyāṃl lokān apāṃpatir vṛṣabha iṣṭakānām / tatra gaccha yatra pūrve paretāḥ purīṣaṃ vasānaḥ svāṃ yoniṃ yathāyatham ity abhimantrya mahī dyauḥ pṛthivī ca naś catasra āśā iti dvābhyāṃ purastāt pratyañcaṃ jīvantaṃ prāṅmukha upadadhāti // avakābhiḥ parītasya jālenāvacchādya śaṅkubhiḥ pariṇihanti
11.7.43	yac ciddhi tvaṃ gṛhegṛha ulūkhalaka yujyase / iha dyumattama vada jayatām iva dundubhir iti dakṣiṇasyāṃ śroṇyām ulūkhalaṃ musalaṃ prayunakti
11.7.44	audumbaraṃ prādeśamātraṃ catuḥsrakty ulūkhalam aparimitaṃ musalaṃ bhavati
11.7.45	uta sma te vanaspate vāto vivāty agram iti / atho indrāya pātave sunu somam ulūkhaleti sarvauṣadhasya pūrayitvāvahanti
11.7.46	tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam iti madhye 'gner ulūkhalaṃ musalam upadadhāti viṣṇoḥ karmāṇi paśyateti vā musalam
11.7.47	divo vā viṣṇa iti śūrpam
11.7.48	sikatābhir ukhāṃ pūrayati
11.7.49	dadhnā madhunā ghṛtena vā
11.7.50	yaṃ kāmayeta kṣodhuk syād ity ūnāṃ tasyopadadhyāt / yaṃ kāmayetānupadasyad annam adyād iti pūrṇāṃ tasyopadadhyāt
11.7.51	syūtā devebhir amṛtenāgā ukhāṃ svasāram adhi vedim asthāt / satyaṃ pūrvair ṛṣibhiś cākṛpāṇo 'gniḥ pravidvān iha tat karotv ity ukhām ādāya dhruvāsi pṛthivīti ca // pṛthivī pṛthivyāṃ sīda mātā mātari mātā syonā syonāyāṃ kratur devānāṃ mahimānam īmahe 'gniṃ sadhasthe sadaneṣu sukratuḥ / vaiśvānaraṃ brahmaṇā viśvavyacasaṃ stomasya dhāman nihitaṃ purīṣyam // samiddham agniṃ samidhā samidhyase 'gniṃ sadhasthe sadaneṣv acyutam // vaiśvānaraṃ brahmaṇā viśvavyacasaṃ stomasya dhāma nidadhe purīṣyam / nyayur mātrayā kavayo vayodhaso 'gniṃ sadhasthe sadaneṣv āhutam // vaiśvānaraṃ brahmaṇā viśvavyacasaṃ stomasya dhāman pavamānam ābhṛtam // dhruvāsi pṛthivī tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīdeti madhye 'gner ukhām upadadhāti
11.7.52	upariṣṭād ulūkhalasyety ekeṣām
11.7.53	agne yukṣvā hi ye taveti yuktavatībhyām // ukhāyām ekāhutiṃ juhoti
11.7.54	puruṣaśirasaḥ prāṇeṣu hiraṇyaśalkān pratyasyati / ṛce tveti dakṣiṇe 'kṣikaṭe / ruce tvety uttare bhāse tveti dakṣiṇasyāṃ nāsikāyāṃ jyotiṣe tvety uttarasyām abhūd idaṃ viśvasya bhuvanasya vājinam ity āsye 'gnir jyotiṣā jyotiṣmān iti dakṣiṇe karṇe rukmo varcasā varcasvān ity uttare
11.7.55	sam it sravanti sarito na dhenā iti śṛtātaṅkyena dadhnā madhumiśreṇa puruṣaśiraḥ pūrayitvā sahasradhā asi sahasrāya tvety ādāyādityaṃ garbhaṃ payasā samañjann ity ukhāyām uttānaṃ prākcubukam upadadhāti
11.7.56	ud u tyaṃ citram iti sauryarcābhyām akṣikaṭayor abhijuhoti
11.7.57	paśuśīrṣāny upadadhāti
11.7.58	yaṃ kāmayetāpaśuḥ syād iti viṣūcīnāni tasyopadadhyāt / yaṃ kāmayeta paśumānt syād iti samīcīnāni tasyopadadhyāt / yaṃ kāmayeta kanīyo 'syānnaṃ syād iti saṃtarāṃ tasya paśuśīrṣāṇy upadadhyāt // yaṃ kāmayeta samāvad asyānnaṃ syād ity abhitas tasya svayamātṛṇṇām upadadhyāt / yaṃ kāmayeta bhūyo 'syānnaṃ syād ity anteṣu tasya vyuduhyopadadhyāt
11.7.59	vātasya dhrajim iti purastāt pratīcīnam aśvasyopadadhāti / ajasram indum iti paścāt prācīnam ṛṣabhasya / varūtriṃ tvaṣṭur iti dakṣiṇata udīcīnaṃ vṛṣṇer uttarato vā dakṣiṇaṃ yo agnir agner ity uttarato dakṣiṇaṃ bastasya dakṣiṇato vodīcīnaṃ tāny utsargair avyavāyan pradakṣiṇam anu parikrāman pratidiśam upatiṣṭhate // imaṃ mā hiṃsīr dvipādam iti puruṣasya / imaṃ mā hiṃsīr ekaśapham ity aśvasya / imaṃ samudram ity ṛṣabhasya / imām ūrṇāyum iti vṛṣṇeḥ / ajā hy agner iti bastasya
11.7.60	atha yadi vāyavyasya śiro bhavati
11.7.61	mukhyasthāne sarvair upadhāya sarvair utsargair upatiṣṭhate
11.7.62	apivā tasyatasya sthāna upadhāya tasyatasyotsargeṇopatiṣṭhate
11.7.63	namo astu sarpebhya ity eteṣām ekenottare 'ṃse sarpaśira upadadhāti / viṣūcīnaṃ paśuśirobhiḥ
11.7.64	apivā yajur eva vaden nopadadhyāt
11.7.65	mā chandas tat pṛthivy agnir devatā tenarṣiṇā tena brahmaṇā tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīda / pramā chandas tad antarikṣaṃ vāto devatā / pratimā chandas tad dyauḥ sūryo devatā / asrīviś chandas tad diśaḥ somo devatā / virāṭ chandas tac cakṣuḥ pūṣā devatā / gāyatrī chandas tad ajā bṛhaspatir devatā / triṣṭub chandas taddhiraṇyam indro devatā / jagatī chandas tad gauḥ prajāpatir devatā / anuṣṭup chandas tad vāg varuṇo devatā / uṣṇihā chandas tad āyur mitro devatā / paṅktiś chandas tat kṛṣiḥ parjanyo devatā / bṛhatī chandas tad aśvaḥ parameṣṭhī devatā tenarṣiṇā tena brahmaṇā tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīdeti dvādaśabhis trir abhyāvartayan ṣaṭtriṃśatā purastāt pratīcīṃ puruṣākṛtiṃ citiṃ cinoti
11.7.66	puruṣaśiro 'syāḥ śiro bhavati
11.7.67	tam upadhāya sahasraśīrṣā puruṣaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapād iti puruṣeṇa nārāyaṇenopatiṣṭhate
11.8.1	apasyā upadadhāti / apāṃ tvemant sādayāmīti pañca purastāt pratīcīḥ / arṇave sadane sīdeti pañca dakṣiṇata udīcīḥ / apāṃ tvā sadane sādayāmīti pañca paścāt prācīḥ / gāyatrī chanda iti pañcottarato dakṣiṇāḥ
11.8.2	ye yajñaṃ samagṛbhṇan devā devebhyaḥ pari / tān gāyatrī nayatu prajānatī svarge loke amṛtaṃ duhānā / ye jyotīṃṣi saṃdadhati svar ārohanto amṛtasya lokam / te yantu prajānanto yajñaṃ vidānāḥ sukṛtasya loke / ye paśavo medhyāso yajñasya yonim abhisaṃbabhūvuḥ / tān dadante kavayo vipaścito yajñaṃ vidānāḥ sukṛtasya loke / yaḥ panthā vitato devayānaś chandobhir vigṛhīta eti / tenātiṣṭhad divam antarikṣaṃ yajñaṃ gṛhītvā sukṛtasya lokam / yo yajñaḥ sahasradhāro dyāvāpṛthivyor adhi nirmitaḥ / tenaitu yajamānaḥ svastyā divo 'dhi pṛṣṭham asthād iti pañca hiraṇyeṣṭakāś catasraḥ pratidiśam ekāṃ madhye
11.8.3	āyave svāhā yoṣkṛte svāhā yoṣyatvane svāhā viṣṇave svāhā bṛhaspataye svāheti pañca hiraṇyeṣṭakāś catasraḥ pratidiśam ekāṃ madhye / trivṛt te agne śiras tan me agne śiraḥ pañcadaśau te agne bāhū tau me agne bāhū saptadaśas te agna ātmā sa me agna ātmaikaviṃśau te agna ūrū tau me agna ūrū triṇavau te agne 'ṣṭhīvantau tau me agne 'ṣṭhīvantau trayastriṃśaṃ te agne pratiṣṭhānaṃ tan me agne pratiṣṭhānam ity etāḥ śirasi pakṣāt puccheṣu śroṇyor aṃsayor upadadhāti / trivṛtte agne śiras tena mābhipāhi pañcadaśau te agne bāhū tābhyāṃ mābhipāhi sapatadaśas te agna ātmā tena mābhipāhy ekaviṃśau te agna ūrū tābhyāṃ mābhipāhi triṇavau te agne 'ṣṭhīvantau tābhyāṃ mābhipāhi trayastriṃśaṃ te agne pratiṣṭhānaṃ tena mābhipāhīty upahitā yajamāno 'numantrayate
11.8.4	adbhyaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ pṛthivyai rasāc ca viśvakarmaṇaḥ samavartatādhi / tasya tvaṣṭā vidadhad rūpam eti tat puruṣasya viśvam ājānam agra ity etām upadhāyartasad asi satyasad asi tejaḥsad asi varcaḥsad asi yaśaḥsad asi gṛṇānāsi / dhāmāsi dhāmyai tvā dhāmabhyas tvā dhāmasu sīda / sanir asi sanyai tvā saneyam / vittir asi vittyai tvā videyam / śktir asi śaktyai tvā śakeyam / bhūtir asi bhūtyai tvā bhūyāsam / karmāsi karmaṇe tvā kriyāsam / gūrdo 'si gūrdāya tvā gūrdebhyas tvā gūrde sīda / kṣatraṃ pāhi kṣatraṃ pinva kṣatraṃ jinva kṣatraṃ yaccha kṣatraṃ dṛṃha kṣatram asi kṣatrāya tvā kṣatrebhyas tvā kṣatre sīda / viśveṣu tvā pārthiveṣu sādayāmi / viśveṣu tvāntarikṣeṣu sādayāmi / viśveṣu tvā divyeṣu sādayāmi / viśveṣu tvā deveṣu sādayāmi / viśvāsu tvāpsu sādayāmi / viśvāsu tvaupadhīṣu sādayāmi / viśveṣu tvā vanaspatiṣu sādayāmi / viśvāsu tvā dikṣu sādayāmi / divi sīda / svarjid asi pṛtanājid asi bhūrijid asy abhijid asi viśvajid asi sarvajid asi satrājid asi dhanajid
